vāgarthāv iva saṃpṛktau vāgarthapratipattaye jagataḥ pitarau vande pārvatīparameśvarau  Ragh kva sūryaprabhavo vaṃśaḥ kva cālpaviṣayā matiḥ titīrṣur dustaram mohād uḍupenāsmi sāgaram  Ragh mandaḥ nigṛhītadhenur manuṣyavācā manuvaṃśaketum vismāyayan vismitam ātmavṛttau siṃhorusattvaṃ nijagāda siṃhaḥ  Ragh alaṃ mahīpāla tava śrameṇa prayuktam apy astram ito vṛthā syāt na pādaponmūlanaśakti raṃhaḥ śiloccaye mūrchati mārutasya  Ragh kailāsagauraṃ vṛam ārurukṣoḥ pādārpaṇānugrahapūtapṛṣṭam avehi māṃ kiṃkaram aṣṭamūrteḥ kumbhodaraṃ nāma nikumbhamitram  Ragh amuṃ puraḥ paśyasi devadāruṃ putrīkṛto sau vṛṣabhadhvajena yo hemakumbhastananiḥsṛtānāṃ skandasya mātuḥ payasāṃ rasajñaḥ  Ragh kaṇḍūyamānena kaṭaṃ kadācid vanyadvipenonmathitā tvag asya athainam adres tanayā śuśoca senānyam ālīḍham ivāsurāstraiḥ  Ragh tadā prabhṛty eva vanadvipānāṃ trāsārtham asminn aham adikukṣau vyāpāritaḥ śūlabhṛtā vidhāya siṃhatvam aṅkāgatasattvavṛtti  Ragh tasyālam eṣā kṣudhitasya tṛptyai pradiṣṭakālā parameśvareṇa upasthitā śoṇitapāraṇā me suradviṣaś cāndramasī sudheva  Ragh sa tvaṃ nivartasva vihāya lajjāṃ guror bhavān darśitaśiṣyabhaktiḥ śastreṇa rakṣyaṃ yad aśakyarakṣaṃ na tad yaśaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ kṣiṇoti  Ragh iti pragalbhaṃ purusādhirājo mṛgādhirājasya vaco niśamya pratyāhatāstro giriśaprabhāvād ātmany avajñāṃ śithilīcakāra  Ragh pratyabravīc cainam iṣuprayoge tatpūrvasaṅge vitathaprayatnaḥ jaḍīkṛtas tryambakavikṣaṇena vajraṃ mumukṣann iva vajrapāṇiḥ  Ragh pratyāha vainaṃ śaramokṣavandhyo mā pattraparvāt svarabhedam āptaḥ prahīṇapūrvadhvaninādhirūḍhas tulām asārena śaradghanena  Ragh saṃruddhaceṣṭasya hetuḥ hāsyaṃ vacas tad yad ahaṃ vivakṣuḥ antargataṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ hi veda sarvaṃ bhavān bhāvam ato bhidhāsye  Ragh mānyaḥ sa me sthāvarajaṅgamānāṃ sargasthitipratyavahārahetuḥ guror apīdaṃ dhanam āhitāgner naśyat purastād anupekṣaṇīyam  Ragh sa tvaṃ madīyena śarīravṛttiṃ dehena nirvartayituṃ prasīda dināvasānotsukabālavatsā visṛjyatāṃ dhenur iyaṃ maharṣeḥ  Ragh athāndhakāraṃ girigahvarāṇāṃ daṃṣṭrāmayūkhaiḥ śakalāni kurvan bhūyaḥ sa bhūteśvarapārśvavartī kiṃcid vihasyārthapatiṃ babhāṣe  Ragh ekātapatraṃ jagataḥ prabhutvaṃ navaṃ yayaḥ kāntam idaṃ vapuś ca alpasya hetor bahu hātum icchan vicāramūdhaḥ pratibhāsi me tvam  Ragh bhūtānukampā tava ced iyaṃ gaur ekā bhavet svastimatī tvadante jīvan punaḥ śaśvad upaplavebhyaḥ prajāḥ prajānātha piteva pāsi  Ragh athaikadhenor aparādhacaṇḍād guroḥ kṛṣānupratimād bibheṣi śakyo sya manyur bhavatā vinetuṃ gāḥ koṭiśaḥ sparśayatā ghaṭodhnīḥ  Ragh tad rakṣa kalyāṇaparaṃparāṇāṃ bhoktāram ūrjasvalam ātmadeham mahītalasparśanamātrabhinnam ṛddhaṃ hi rājyaṃ padam aindram āhuḥ  Ragh etāvad uktvā virate mṛgendre pratisvanenāsya guhāgatena śiloccayo pi kṣitipālam uccaiḥ prītyā tam evārtham abhāṣateva  Ragh niśamya devānucarasya vācaṃ manuṣyadevaḥ punar apy uvāca dhenvā tadadhyāsitakātarākṣyā nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ sutarāṃ dayāluḥ  Ragh kṣatāt kila trāyata ity udagraḥ kṣatrasya śabdo bhuvaneṣu rūḍhaḥ rājyena kiṃ tadviparītavṛtteḥ prāṇair upakrośamalīmasair vā  Ragh kathaṃ nu śakyo nunayo maharṣer viśrāṇanāc cānyapayasvinīnām imām anūnāṃ surabher avehi rudraujasā tu pahṛtaṃ tvayāsyām  Ragh seyaṃ svadehārpaṇaniṣkrayeṇa nyāyyā mayā mocayituṃ bhavattaḥ na pāraṇā syād vihatā tavaivaṃ bhaved aluptaś ca muneḥ kriyārthaḥ  Ragh bhavān apīdaṃ paravān avaiti mahān hi yatnas tava devadārau sthātuṃ niyoktur na hi śakyam agre vināśya rakṣyaṃ svayam akṣatena  Ragh kim apy ahiṃsyas tava cen mato haṃ yaśaḥśarīre bhava me dayāluḥ ekāntavidhaṃsiṣu madvidhānāṃ piṇḍeṣv anāsthā khalu bhautikeṣu  Ragh saṃbandham ābhāṣaṇapūrvam āhur vṛttaḥ sa nau saṃgatayor vanānte tad bhūtanāthānuga nārhasi tvaṃ saṃbandhino me praṇayaṃ vihantum  Ragh tatheti gām uktavate dilīpaḥ sadyaḥ pratiṣṭambhavimuktabāhuḥ sa nyasta śastro haraye svadeham upānayat piṇḍam ivāmiṣasya  Ragh tasmin kṣaṇe pālayituḥ prajānām utpaśyataḥ siṃhanipātam ugram avāṅmukhasyopari puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta vidyādharahastamuktā  Ragh uttiṣṭha vatsety amṛtāyamānaṃ vaco niśamyotthitam utthitaḥ san dadarśa rājā jananīm iva svāṃ gām agrataḥ prasraviṇīṃ na siṃham  Ragh taṃ vismitaṃ dhenur uvāca sādho māyāṃ mayodhbhāvya parīkṣito si ṛṣiprabhāvān mayi nāntako pi prabhuḥ prahartuṃ kim utānyahiṃsrāḥ  Ragh bhaktyā gurau mayy anukampāya ca prītāsmi te putra varaṃ vṛṇīṣva na kevalānāṃ payasāṃ prasūtim avehi māṃ kāmadughāṃ prasannām  Ragh tataḥ samānīya samānitārthī hastau svahastārjitavīraśabdaḥ vaṃśasya kartāram anantakīrtiṃ sudakṣiṇāyāṃ tanayaṃ yayāce  Ragh saṃtānakāmāya tatheti kāmaṃ rājñe pratiśrutya payasvinī sā dugdhvā payaḥ pattrapuṭe madīyaṃ putr opabhuṅkṣv eti tam ādideśa  Ragh vatsasya homārthavidheś ca śeṣam ṛṣer anujñām adhigamya mātaḥ ūdhasyam icchāmi tavopabhoktumyaṃ ṣaṣṭhāmśam urvyā iva rakṣitāyāḥ  Ragh itthaṃ kṣitīśena vasiṣṭhadhenur vijñāpitā prītatarā babhūva tadanvitā haimavatāc ca kukṣeḥ pratyāyayāv āśramam aśrameṇa  Ragh tasyāḥ prasannendumukhaḥ prasādaṃ gurur nṛpāṇāṃ gurave nivedya praharṣacihnānumitaṃ priyāyai śaśaṃsa vācā punaruktayeva  Ragh sa nandinīstanyam aninditātmā sadvatsalo vatsahutāvaśeṣam papau vasiṣṭhena kṛtābhyanujñaḥ śubhraṃ yaśo mūrtam ivātitṛṣṇaḥ  Ragh prātar yathoktavratapāraṇānte prāsthānikaṃ svastyayanaṃ prayuja tau daṃpatī svāṃ prati rājadhānīṃ prasthāpayām āsa vaśī vasiṣṭhaḥ  Ragh pradakṣiṇīkṛtya hutaṃ hutāśam anantaraṃ bhartur arundhatīṃ ca dhenuṃ savatsāṃ ca nṛpaḥ pratasthe sanmaṅgalodagrataraprabhāvaḥ  Ragh śrotābhirāmadhvaninā rathena sa dharmapatnīsahitaḥ sahiṣṇuḥ yayāv anudghātasukhena mārgaṃ sveneva pūrṇena manorathena  Ragh tam āhitautsukyam adarśanena prajāḥ prajārthavratakarśitāṅgam netraiḥ papus tṛptim anāpnuvadbhir navodayaṃ nātham ivauṣadhīnām  Ragh puraṃdaraśrīḥ puram utpatākaṃ praviśya paurair abhinandyamānaḥ bhuje bhuaṃgendrasamānasāre bhūyaḥ sa bhūmer dhuram āsasañja  Ragh atha nayanasamutthaṃ jyotir atrer iva dyauḥ surasarid iva tejo vahniniṣṭhyūtam aiśam narapatikulabhūtyai garbham ādhatta rājñī gurubhir abhiniviṣṭaṃ lokapālānubhāvaiḥ  Ragh athepsitaṃ bhartur upasthitodayaṃ sakhījanodvīkṣaṇakaumudīmukham nidānam ikṣvākukulasya saṃtateḥ sudakṣiṇā daurhṛdalakṣaṇaṃ dadhau  Ragh śarīrasādād asamagrabhūṣaṇā mukhena sālakṣyata lodhrapāṇḍunā tanuprakāśena viceyatārakā prabhātakalpā śaśineva śarvarī  Ragh tato viśāṃpatyur ananyasaṃtater manorathaṃ kiṃcid ivodayonmukham ananyasauhārdarasasya dohadaṃ priyā prapede prakṛtipriyaṃvadā  RaghA mukhena sā ketakapattrapāṇḍunā kṛśāṅgayaṣṭiḥ parimeyabhūṣaṇā sthitālpatārāṃ karuṇendumaṇḍalāṃ vibhātakalpāṃ rajanīṃ vyaḍambayat  RaghB tadānanaṃ mṛtsurabhi kṣitīśvaro rahasy upāghrāya na tṛptim āyayau karīva siktaṃ pṛṣataiḥ payomucāṃ śucivyapāye vanarājipalvalam  Ragh divaṃ marutvān iva bhokṣyate bhuvaṃ digantaviśrāntaratho hi tat sutaḥ ato bhilāṣe prathamaṃ tathāvidhe mano babandhānyarasān vilaṅghya sā  Ragh na me hriyā śaṃsati kiṃcid īpsitaṃ spṛhāvatī vastuṣu keṣu māgadhī na hīṣṭam asya tridive pi bhūpater priyāsakhīr uttarakosaleśvaraḥ  Ragh upetya sā dohadaduḥkhaśīlatāṃ yad eva vavre tad apaśyad āhṛtam na hīṣṭam asya tridive pi bhūpater abhūd anāsādyam adhijyadhanvanaḥ  Ragh krameṇa nistīrya ca dohadavyathāṃ pracīyamānāvayavā rarāja sā purāṇapattrāpagamād anantaraṃ lateva saṃnaddhamanojñapallavā  Ragh dineṣu gacchatsu nitāntapīvaraṃ tadīyam ānīlamukhaṃ stanadvayam tiraścakāra bhramarābhilīnayoḥ sujātayoḥ paṅkajakośayoḥ śriyam  Ragh nidhānagarbhām iva sāgarāmbarāṃ śamīm ivābhyantaralīnapāvakām nadīm ivāntaḥsalilāṃ sarasvatīṃ nṛpaḥ sasattvāṃ mahiṣīm amanyata  Ragh priyānurāgasya manaḥsamunnater bhujārjitānāṃ ca digantasaṃpadām yathākramaṃ puṃsavanādikāḥ kriyā dhṛteś ca dhīraḥ sadṛśīr vyadhatta saḥ  Ragh surendramātrāśritagarbhagauravāt prayatnamuktāsanayā gṛhāgataḥ tayopacārāñjalikhinnahastayā nananda pāriplavanetrayā nṛpaḥ  Ragh kumārabhṛtyākuśalair anuṣṭhite bhiṣagbhir āptair atha garbhabharmaṇi patiḥ pratītaḥ prasavonmukhīm priyāṃ dadarśa kāle divam abhrītam iva  Ragh grahais tataḥ pañcabhir uccasaṃśrayair asūryagaiḥ sūcitabhāgyasaṃpadam asūta putraṃ samaye śacīsamā trisādhanā śaktir ivārtham akṣayam  Ragh diśaḥ prasedur maruto vavuḥ sukhāḥ pradakṣiṇārcir havir agnir ādade babhūva sarvaṃ śubhaśaṃsi tatkṣaṇaṃ bhavo hi lokābhyudayāya tādṛśām  Ragh ariṣṭaśayyāṃ parito visāriṇā sujanmanas tasya nijena tejasā niśīthadīpāḥ sahasā hatatviṣo babhūvur ālekhyasamarpitā iva  Ragh janāya śuddhāntacarāya śaṃsate kumārajanmāmṛtasaṃmitākṣaram adeyam āsīt trayam eva bhūpateḥ śaśiprabhaṃ chattram ubhe ca cāmare  Ragh samīkṣya putrasya cirān mukhaṃ pitā nidhānakumbhasya yuveva durgataḥ mudā śarīre prababhūva nātmanaḥ payodhir indūdayamūrchito yathā  Ragh nivātapadmastimitena cakṣuṣā nṛpasya kāntaṃ pibataḥ sutānanam mahodadheḥ pūra ivendudarśanād guruḥ praharṣaḥ prababhūva nātmani  Ragh sa jātakarmaṇy akhile tapasvinā tapovanād etya purodhasā kṛte dilīpasūnur maṇir ākarodbhavaḥ prayuktasaṃskāra ivādhikaṃ babhau  Ragh sukhaśravā maṅgalatūryanisvanāḥ pramodanṛtyaiḥ saha vārayoṣitām na kevalaṃ sadmani māgadhīpateḥ pathi vyajṛmbhanta divaukasām api  Ragh na saṃyatas tasya babhūva rakṣitur visarjayed yaṃ sutajanmaharṣitaḥ ṛṇābhidhānāt svayam eva kevalaṃ tadā pitḥṇāṃ mumuce sa bandhanāt  Ragh śutasya yāyād ayam antam arbhakas tathā pareṣāṃ yudhi ceti pārthivaḥ avekṣya dhātor gamanārtham arthavic cakāra nāmnā raghum ātmasaṃbhavam  Ragh pituḥ prayatnāt sa samagrasaṃpadaḥ śubhaiḥ śarīrāvayavair dine dine pupoṣa vṛddhiṃ haridaśvadīdhiter anupraveśād iva bālacandramāḥ  Ragh umāvṛṣāṅkau śarajanmanā yathā yathā jayantena śacīpuraṃdarau tathā nṛpaḥ sā cu sutena māgadhī nanandatus tatsadṛśena tatsamau  Ragh rathāṅganāmnor iva bhāvabandhanaṃ babhūva yat prema parasparāśrayam vibhaktam apy ekasutena tat tayoḥ parasparasyopari paryacīyata  Ragh uvāca dhātryā prathamoditaṃ vaco yayau tadīyām avalambya cāṅgulim abhūc ca namraḥ praṇipātaśikṣayā pitur mudaṃ tena tatāna so rbhakaḥ  Ragh tam aṅkam āropya śarīrayogajaiḥ sukhair niṣiñcantam ivāmṛtaṃ tvaci upāntasaṃmīlitalocano nṛpaś cirāt sutasparśarasjñatāṃ yayau  Ragh tam aṅkam āropya śarīrayogajaiḥ sthiter abhettā sthitimantam anvayam svamūrtibhedena guṇāgryavartinā patiḥ prajānām iva sargam ātmanaḥ  Ragh sa vṛttacaulaś calakākapakṣakair amātyaputraiḥ savayobhir anvitaḥ liper yathāvadgrahaṇena vāṅmayaṃ nadīmukheneva samudram āviśat  Ragh athopanītaṃ vidhivad vipaścito vininyur enaṃ guravo gurupriyam avandhyayatnāś ca babhūvur arbhake tatāra vidyāḥ pavanātipātibhir  Ragh dhiyaḥ samagraiḥ sa guṇair udāradhīḥ kramāc catasraś caturarṇavopamāḥ tatāra vidyāḥ pavanātipātibhir diśo haridbhir haritām iveśvaraḥ  Ragh tvacaṃ sa medhyāṃ paridhāya rauravīm aśikṣatāstraṃ pitur eva mantravat na kevalaṃ tadgurur ekapārthivaḥ kṣitāv abhūd ekadhanurdharo pi saḥ  Ragh mahokṣatāṃ vatsataraḥ spṛśann iva dvipendrabhāvaṃ kalabhaḥ śrayann iva raghuḥ kramād yauvanabhinnaśaiśavaḥ pupoṣa gāmbhīryamanoharaṃ vapuḥ  Ragh athāsya godānavidher anantaraṃ vivāhadīkṣāṃ niravartayad guruḥ narendrakanyās tam avāpya satpatiṃ tamonudaṃ dakṣasutā ivābabhuḥ  Ragh yuvā yugavyāyatabāhur aṃsalaḥ kapāṭavakṣāḥ pariṇaddhakaṃdharaḥ vapuḥprakarṣād ajayad guruṃ raghus tathāpi nīcair vinayād adṛśyata  Ragh tataḥ prajānāṃ ciram ātmanā dhṛtāṃ nitāntagurvīṃ laghayiṣyatā dhuram nisargasaṃskāravinīta ity asau nṛpeṇa cakre yuvarājaśabdabhāk  Ragh narendramūlāyatanād anantaraṃ ghanavyapāyena gabhastimān iva agacchad aṃśena guṇābhilāṣiṇī navāvatāraṃ kamalād ivotpalam  Ragh vibhāvasuḥ sārathineva vāyunā ghanavyapāyena gabhastimān iva babhūva tenātitarāṃ suduḥsahaḥ kaṭaprabhedena karīva pārthivaḥ  Ragh niyujya taṃ homaturaṃgarakṣaṇe dhanurdharaṃ rājasutair anudrutam apūrṇam ekena śatakratūpamaḥ śataṃ kratūnā apavighnam āpa saḥ  Ragh tataḥ paraṃ tena makhāya vajvanā turaṃgam utsṛṣṭam anargalaṃ punaḥ dhanurbhṛtām agrata eva rakṣiṇāṃ jahāra śakraḥ kila gūḍhavigrahaḥ  Ragh viṣādaluptapratipatti vismitaṃ mamaiva yeneha turaṃgam īkṣase dhenvā niśamyeti vacaḥ samīrtaṃ śrutaprabhāvā dadṛśe tha nandinī  Ragh svedāmbunā mārjaya putra locane mamaiva yeneha turaṃgam īkṣase dhenvā niśamyeti vacaḥ samīritaṃ mudaṃ parām āpa dilīpanandanaḥ  Ragh tadaṅganisyandajalena locane pramṛjya puṇyena puraskṛtaḥ satām atīndriyeṣv apy upapannadarśano babhūva bhāveṣu dilīpanandanaḥ  Ragh sa pūrvataḥ parvatapakṣaśātanaṃ dadarśa devaṃ naradevasaṃbhavaḥ punaḥ punaḥ sūtaniṣiddhacāpalaṃ harantam aśvaṃ ratharaśmisaṃyatam  Ragh sa pūrvataḥ parvatapakṣaśātanaṃ hariṃ viditvā haribhiś ca vājibhiḥ avocad enaṃ gangaspṛśā raghuḥ svareṇa dhīreṇa nivartayann iva  Ragh makhāṃśabhājāṃ prathamo manīṣibhis tvam eva devendra sadā nigadyase ajasradīkṣāprayatasya madguroḥ kriyāvighātāya kathaṃ pravartase  Ragh trilokanāthena sadā makhadviṣas tvayā niyamyā nanu divyacakṣuṣā sa cet svayaṃ karamasu dharmacāriṇāṃ tvam antarāyo bhavasi cyuto vidhiḥ  Ragh tad aṅgam agryaṃ maghavan mahākrator amuṃ turaṃgaṃ pratimoktum arhasi pataḥśruter darśayitāra īśvarā malīmasām ādadate na paddhatim  Ragh iti pragalbhaṃ raghuṇā samīritaṃ vaco niśamyādhipatir divaukasām nivartayām āsa rathaṃ savismayaḥ pracakrame ca prativaktum uttaram  Ragh yad āttha rājanyakumāra tat tathā yaśas tu rakṣyaṃ parato yaśodhanaiḥ jagatprakāśaṃ tad aśeṣam ijyayā bhavadgurur laṅghayituṃ mamodyataḥ  Ragh harir yathaikaḥ puruśottamaḥ smṛto maheśvaras tryambaka eva nāparaḥ tathā vidur māṃ munayaḥ śatakratuṃ dvitīyagāmī na hi śabda eṣa naḥ  Ragh ato yam aśvaḥ kapilānukāriṇā pitus tvadīyasya mayāpahāritaḥ alaṃ prayatnena tavātra mā nidhāḥ padaṃ padavyāṃ sagarasya saṃtateḥ  Ragh tataḥ prahasyāpabhayaḥ puraṃdaraṃ punar babhāṣe turagasya rakṣitā gṛhāṇa śastraṃ yadi sarga eṣa te na khalv anirjitya raghuṃ kṛtī bhavān  Ragh sa evam uktvā maghavantam unmukhaḥ kariṣyamāṇaḥ saśaram śarāsanam atiṣṭhad ālīḍhaviśeṣaśobhinā vapuḥprakarṣeṇa viḍambiteśvaraḥ  Ragh raghor avaṣṭambhamayena pattriṇā hṛdi kṣato gotrabhid apy amarṣaṇaḥ navāmbudānīkamuhūrtalāñchane dhanuṣy amoghaṃ samadhatta sāyakam  Ragh dilīpasūnoḥ sa bṛhad bhujāntaraṃ praviśya bhīmāsuraśoṇitocitaḥ papāv anāsvāditapūrvam āśugaḥ kutūhaleneva manuṣyaśoṇitam  Ragh hareḥ kumāro pi kumāravikramaḥ suradvipāsphālanakarkaśāṅgulau bhuje śacīpattraviśeṣakāṅkite svanāmacihnaṃ nicakhāna sāyakam  Ragh jahāra cānyena mayūrapattriṇā śareṇa śakrasya mahāśanidhvajam cukopa tasmai sa bhṛśaṃ suraśriyaḥ prasahaya keśavyaparopaṇād iva  Ragh tayor upāntasthitasiddhasainikaṃ garutmadāśīviśabhīmadarśanaiḥ babhūva yuddhaṃ tumuulaṃ jayaiṣiṇor adhomukhair ūrdhvamukhaiś ca pattribhiḥ  Ragh atiprabandhaprahitāstravṛṣṭibhis tam āśrayaṃ duṣprahasya tejasaḥ śaśāka nirvāpayituṃ na vāsavaḥ svataś cyutaṃ vahnim ivādbhir ambudaḥ  Ragh tataḥ prakoṣṭhe haricandanāṅkite pramathyamānārṇavadhīra raghuḥ śaśāṅkārdhamukhena pattriṇā śarāsanajyām alunād viḍaujasaḥ  Ragh sa cāpam utsṛjya vivṛddhamatsaraḥ praṇāśanāya prabalasya vidviṣaḥ mahīdhrapakṣavyaparopaṇocitaṃ sphuratprabhāmaṇḍalam astram ādade  Ragh raghur bhṛśaṃ vakṣasi tena tāḍitaḥ papāta bhūmau saha sainikāśrubhiḥ nimeṣamātrād avadhūya tad vyathāṃ sahotthitaḥ sainikaharṣanisvanaiḥ  Ragh tathāpi śastravyavahāraniṣṭhure bipakṣabhāve ciram asya tasthuṣaḥ tutoṣa vīryātiśayena vṛtrahā padaṃ hi sarvatra guṇair nidhīyate  Ragh asaṅgam adriṣv api sāravattayā na me tvadanyena visoḍham āyudham avehi māṃ prītam ṛte turaṃgamāt kim icchasīti sphuṭam āha vāsavaḥ  Ragh tato niṣaṅgād asamagram uddhṛtaṃ suvarṇapuṅkhadyutirañjitāṅgulim narendrasūnuḥ pratisaṃharann iṣuṃ priyaṃvadaḥ pratyavadat sureśvaram  Ragh amocyam aśvaṃ yadi manyase prabho tataḥ samāpte vidhinaiva karmaṇi ajasradīkṣāprayataḥ sa madguruḥ krator aśeṣeṇa phalena yujyatām  Ragh yathā ca vṛttāntam imaṃ sadogatas trilocanaikāṃśatayā durāsadaḥ tavaiva saṃdeṣaharād viśaṃpatiḥ śṛṇoti lokeśa tathā vidhīyatām  Ragh tatheti kāmaṃ pratiśuśruvān raghor yathāgataṃ mātalisārathir yayau nṛpasya nātipramanāḥ sadogṛhaṃ sudakṣināsūnur api nyavartata  Ragh tam abhyanandat prathamaṃ prabodhitaḥ prajeśvaraḥ śāsanahāriṇā hareḥ parāmṛśan harṣajaḍena pāṇinā tadīyam aṅgaṃ kuliśavraṇāṅkitam  Ragh iti kṣitīśo navatiṃ navādhikāṃ mahākratūnāṃ mahanīyaśāsanaḥ samāraurukṣur divam āyuṣaḥ kṣaye tatāna sopānaparaṃparām iva  Ragh atha sa viṣavyāvṛttātmā yathāvidhi sūnave nṛpatikakudaṃ dattvā yūne sitātapavāraṇam munivanatarucchāyāṃ devyā tayā saha śiśriye galitavayasām ikṣvākūṇā idaṃ hi kulavrtam  Ragh sa rājyaṃ guruṇā dattaṃ pratipadyādhikaṃ babhau dinānte nihitaṃ tejaḥ savitreva hutāśanaḥ  Ragh nyastaśastraṃ dilīpaṃ ca taṃ ca śuśruvuṣāṃ patim rājñām uddhṛtanārāce hṛdi śalyam ivārpitam  Ragh dilīpānantaraṃ rājye taṃ niśamya pratiṣṭhitam pūrvaṃ pradūmito rājñāṃ hṛdaye gnir ivotthitaḥ  Ragh puruhūtadhvajasyeva tasyonnayanapaṅktayaḥ navābhyutthānadarśinyo nananduḥ sa prajāḥ prajāḥ  Ragh samam eva samākrāntaṃ tasyonnayanapaṅktayaḥ tena siṃhāsanaṃ pitryam akhilaṃ cārimaṇḍalaṃ  Ragh chāyāmaṇḍalalakṣyena tam adṛśyā kila svayam padmā padmātapatreṇa bheje sāmrājyadīkṣitam  Ragh parikalpitasāṃnidhyā kāle kāle ca bandiṣu stutyaṃ stutibhir arthyābhir upatasthe sarasvatī  Ragh manuprabhṛtibhir mānyair bhuktā yady api rājabhiḥ tathāpy ananyapūrveva tasminn āsīd vasuṃdharā  Ragh sa hi sarvasya lokasya yuktadaṇḍatayā manaḥ ādade nātiśītoṣṇo nabhasvān iva dakṣiṇaḥ  Ragh mandotkaṇṭaḥ kṛtās tena guṇādhikatayā gurau phalena sahakārasya phuṣpodgama iva prajāḥ  Ragh nayavidbhir nave rājñi sad asac copadarśitam pūrva evābhavat pakṣas tasmin nābhavad uttaraḥ  Ragh pañcānām api bhūtānām utkarṣaṃ pupuṣur guṇāḥ nave tasmin mahīpāle sarvaṃ navam ivābhavat  Ragh yathā prahlādanāc candraḥ pratāpāt tapano yathā tathaiva so bhūd anvartho rājā prakṛtirañjanāt  Ragh kāmaṃ karṇāntaviṣrānte viśāle tasya locane cakṣuṣmattā tu śāstreṇa sūkṣmakāryārthadarśinā  Ragh labdhapraśamanasvastham athainaṃ samupasthitā pārthivaśrīr dvitīyeva śarat paṅkajalakṣaṇā  Ragh nirvṛṣṭalaghubhir meghair muktavartmā suduḥsahaḥ svaṃ dhanuḥ śaṅkiteneva yugapad vyānaśe diśaḥ  Ragh adhijyam āyudhaṃ kartuṃ muktavartmā suduḥsahaḥ svaṃ dhanuḥ śaṅkiteneva saṃjahre śatamanyunā  Ragh vārṣikaṃ saṃjahārendro dhanur jaitraṃ raghur dadhau prajārthasādhane tau hi paryāyodyatakārmukau  Ragh puṇḍarīkātapatras taṃ vikasatkāśacāmaraḥ ṛtur viḍambayām āsa āsīt samarasā dvayoḥ  Ragh prasādarīkātapatras taṃ candre ca viśadaprabhe tadā cakṣuṣmatāṃ prītir āsīt samarasā dvayoḥ  Ragh haṃsaśreṇīṣu tārāsu kumudvatsu ca vāriṣu vibhūtayays tadīyānāṃ paryastā yaśasām iva  Ragh ikṣucchāyaniṣādinyas tasya goptur guṇodayam ākumārakathodghātaṃ śāligopyo jagur yaśaḥ  Ragh prasasādodayād ambhaḥ kumbhayoner mahaujasaḥ raghor abhibhavāśaṅki cukṣubhe dviṣatāṃ manaḥ  Ragh madodagrāḥ kakudmantaḥ saritāṃ kūlamudrujāḥ līlākhelam anuprāpur mohakṣās tasya vikramam  Ragh prasavaiḥ saptaparṇānāṃ madagandhibhir āhatāḥ asūyayeva tannāgāḥ saptadhaiva prasusruvuḥ  Ragh saritaḥ kurvatī gādhāḥ pathaś cāśyānakardamān yātrāyai codayām āsa taṃ śakteḥ prathamaṃ śarat  Ragh samyak tasmai ghuto vahnir vājinīrājanāvidhau pradakṣiṇārcir vyājena hasteneva jayaṃ dadau  Ragh sa guptamūlapratyantaḥ śuddhapārṣṇir ayānvitaḥ ṣaḍvidhaṃ balam ādāya pratasthe digjigīṣayā  Ragh avākiran vayovṛddhās taṃ lājaiḥ paurayoṣitaḥ pṛṣatair mandaroddhūtaiḥ kṣīrormaya ivācyutam  Ragh sa yayau prathamaṃ prācīṃ tulyaḥ prācīnabarhiṣā ahitān aniloddhūtais tarjayann iva ketubhiḥ  Ragh rajobhiḥ syandanoddhūtair gajaiś ca ghanasaṃnibhaiḥ bhuvas talam iva vyoma kurvan vyomeva bhūtalam  Ragh pratāpo gre tataḥ śabdaḥ parāgas tadantaram yayau paścād rathādīti catuḥskandheva sā camūḥ  Ragh marupṛṣṭhāny udambhāṃsi nāvyāḥ supratarā nadīḥ vipināni prakāśāni śaktimattvāc cakāra saḥ  Ragh purogaiḥ kaluṣās tasya sahaprasthāyibhiḥ kṛśāḥ paścātprayāyibhiḥ paṅkāś cakrire mārganimnagāḥ  Ragh sa senāṃ mahatīṃ karṣan pūrvasāgaragāminīm babhau harajaṭābhraṣṭāṃ gaṅgām iva bhagīrathaḥ  Ragh tyājitaiḥ phalam utkhātair bhagnaiś ca bahudhā nṛpaiḥ tasyāsīd ulbaṇo mārgaḥ pādapair iva dantinaḥ  Ragh paurastyān evam ākrāmaṃs tāṃs tāñ janapadāñ jayī prāpa tālīvanśyāmam upakañṭhaṃ mahodadheḥ  Ragh anamrāṇāṃ samuddhartus tasmāt sindhurayād iva ātmā saṃrakṣitaḥ suhmair vṛttim āśritya vaitasīm  Ragh vaṅgān utkhāya tarasā netā nausādhanoddhatān nicakhāna jayastambhān gaṅgāsrotontareṣu saḥ  Ragh āpādapadmapraṇatāḥ kalamā iva te raghum phalaiḥ saṃvardhayām āsur utkhātapratirpitāḥ  Ragh sa tīrtvā kapiṣāṃ sainyair baddhadviradasetubhiḥ utkalādarśitapathaḥ kaliṅgābhimukho yayau  Ragh sa pratāpaṃ mahendrasya mūrdhni tīkṣṇaṃ nyaveśayat aṅkuśaṃ dviradasyeva yantā gambhīravedinaḥ  Ragh pratijagrāha kāliṅgas tam astrair gajasādhanaḥ pakṣacchedodyataṃ śakraṃ śilāvarṣīva parvataḥ  Ragh dviṣāṃ viṣahya kākutsthas tatra nārācadurdinam sanmaṅgalasnāta iva pratipede jayaśriyam  Ragh vāyavyāstravinirdhūtāt pakṣāviddhān mahodadheḥ gajānīkāt sa kāliṅgaṃ tārkṣyaḥ sarpam ivādade  Ragh tāmbūlīnāṃ dalais tatra racitāpānabhūmayaḥ nalikerāsavaṃ yodhāḥ śātravaṃ ca papur yaśaḥ  Ragh gṛhītapratimuktasya sa dharmavijayī nṛpaḥ śriyaṃ mahendranāthasya jahāra na tu medinīm  Ragh tato velātaṭenaiva phalavatpūgamālinā agastyācaritām āśām anāśāsyajayo yayau  Ragh sa sainyaparibhogeṇa gajadānasugandhinā kāverīṃ saritāṃ patyuḥ śaṅkanīyām ivākarot  Ragh balair adhuṣitās tasya vijigīṣor gatādhvanaḥ maricodbhrāntahārītā malayādrer upatyakāḥ  Ragh sasañjur aśvakṣuṇṇānām elānām utpatiṣṇavaḥ tulyagandhiṣu mattebhakaṭeṣu phalareṇavaḥ  Ragh ājāneyakhurakṣuṇṇapakvailākṣetrasaṃbhavam vyānaśe sapadi vyoma tripadīchedinām api  Ragh bhogiveṣṭanamārgeṣu candanānāṃ samarpitam nāsrasat kariṇāṃ graivaṃ tripadīchedinām api  Ragh diśi mandāyate tejo dakṣiṇasyāṃ raver api tasyām eva raghoḥ pāṇḍyāḥ pratāpaṃ na viṣehire  Ragh tāmraparṇīsametasya muktāsāraṃ mahodadheḥ te nipatya dadus tasmai yaśaḥ svam iva saṃcitam  Ragh sa nirviśya yathākāmaṃ taṭeṣv ālīnacandanau stanāv iva diśas tasyāḥ śailau malayadardurau  Ragh tasyānīkair visarpadbhir aparāntajayodyataiḥ rāmāstrotsārito py āsīt sahyalagna ivārṇavaḥ  Ragh bhayotsṛṣṭavibhūṣāṇāṃ tena keralayoṣitām alakeṣu camūreṇuś cūrṇapratinidhīkṛtaḥ  Ragh muralāmārutoddhūtam agamat kaitakaṃ rajaḥ tadyodhavārabāṇānām ayatnapaṭavāsatām  Ragh abhyabhūyata vāhānāṃ caratāṃ gātraśiñjitaiḥ varmabhiḥ pavanoddhūtarājatālīvanadvhvanaiḥ  Ragh kharjūrīskandhanaddhānāṃ madodgārtasugandhiṣu kaṭeṣu kariṇāṃ petuḥ puṃnāgebhyaḥ śilīmukhāḥ  Ragh avakāśaṃ kilodanvān rāmāyābhyarthito dadau aparāntamahīpālavyājena raghave karam  Ragh mattebharadanotkīrṇavyaktavikramalakṣaṇam trikūṭam eva tatroccair jayastambhaṃ cakāra saḥ  Ragh pārasīkāṃs tato jetuṃ pratasthe sthalavartmanā indriyākhyān iva ripūṃs tattvajñānena saṃyamī  Ragh yavanīmukhapadmānāṃ sehe madhumadaṃ na saḥ bālātapam ivābjānām akālajaladodayaḥ  Ragh saṃgrāmas tumulas tasya pāścātyair aśvasādhanaiḥ śārṅgakūjitavijñeyapratiyodhe rajasy abhūt  Ragh bhallāpavarjitais teṣāṃ śirobhiḥ śmaśrulair mahīm tastāra saraghāvyāptaiḥ sa kṣaudrapaṭalair iva  Ragh apanītaśirastrāṇāḥ śeṣās taṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ praṇipātapratīkāraḥ saṃrambho hi mahātmanām  Ragh vinayante sma tadyodhā madhubhir vijayaśramam āstīrṇājinaratnāsu drākṣāvalayabhūmiṣu  Ragh tataḥ pratasthe kauberīṃ bhāsvān iva raghur diśam śarair usrair ivodīcyān uddhariṣyam rasān iva  Ragh jitān ajayyas tān eva kṛtvā rathapuraḥsarān mahārṇavam ivaurāgniḥ praviveśottarāpatham  Ragh vinītādhvaśramās tasya sindhutīraveceṣṭanaiḥ dudhuvur vājinaḥ skandhāṃl lagnakuṅkumakesarān  Ragh tatra hūṇāvarodhānāṃ bhartṛśu vyaktavikramam kapolapāṭalādeśi babhūva raghuceṣṭitam  Ragh kāmbojāḥ samare soḍhuṃ tasya vīryam anīśvarāḥ gajālānaparikliṣṭair akṣoṭaiḥ sārdham ānatāḥ  Ragh teṣāṃ sadaśvabhūyiṣṭhās tuṅgā draviṇarāśayaḥ upadā viviśuḥ śaśvan notsekāḥ kosaleśvaram  Ragh tato gaurīguruṃ śailam ārurohāśvasādhanaḥ vardhayann iva tatkūṭān uddhūtair dhātureṇubhiḥ  Ragh śaśaṃsa tulyasattvānāṃ sainyaghoṣe py asaṃbhramam guhāśayānāṃ siṃhānāṃ parivṛtyāvalokitam  Ragh bhūrjeṣu marmarībhūtāḥ kīcakadhvanihetavaḥ gaṅgāśīkariṇo mārge marutas taṃ siṣevire  Ragh viśaśramur namerūṇāṃ chāyāsv adhyāsya sainikāḥ dṛṣado vāsitotsaṅgā niṣaṇṇamṛganābhibhiḥ  Ragh saralāsaktamātaṅgagraiveyasphuritatviṣaḥ āsannoṣadhayo netur naktam asnehadīpikāḥ  Ragh tasyotsṛṣṭanivāseṣu kaṇṭharajjukṣata tvacaḥ gajavarṣma kirātebhyaḥ śaśaṃsur devadāravaḥ  Ragh tatra janyaṃ raghor ghoraṃ pārvatīyair gaṇair abhūt nārācakṣepaṇīyāśmaniṣpeṣotpatitānalam  Ragh śarair utsavasaṃketān sa kṛtvā viratotsavān jayodāharaṇaṃ bāhvor gāpayām āsa kiṃnarān  Ragh paraspareṇa vijñātas teṣūpāyanapāṇiṣu rājñā himavataḥ sāro rājñaḥ sāro himādriṇā  Ragh tatrākṣobhyaṃ yaśorāśiṃ niveśyāvarurobha saḥ paulastyatulitasyādrer ādadhāna iva hriyam  Ragh cakampe tīrṇalauhitye tasmin prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ tadgālānatāṃ prāptaiḥ saha kālāgurudruamaiḥ  Ragh na prasehe sa ruddhārkam adhārāvarṣadurdinam rathavartma rajo py asya kuta eva patākinīm  Ragh tam īśaḥ kāmarūpāṇām atyākhaṇḍalavikramam bheje bhinnakaṭair nāgair anyān uparurodha yaiḥ  Ragh kāmarūpeśvaras tasya hemapīṭhādhidevatām ratnapuṣpopahāreṇa cchāyām ānarca pādayoḥ  Ragh iti jitvā diṣo jiṣṇur nyavartata rathoddhatam rajo viśrāmayan rājñāṃ chattraśūnyeṣu mauliṣu  Ragh sa viśvajitam ājahre yajñaṃ sarvasvadakṣiṇam ādānaṃ hi visargāya sataṃ vārimucām iva  Ragh sattrānte sacivasakhaḥ puraskriyābhir gurvībhiḥ śamitaparājayavyalīkān kākutsthaś ciravirahotsukāvarodhān rājanyān svapuranivṛttaye numene  Ragh yajñānte tam avabhṛthābiṣekapūtaṃ satkāraiḥ śamitaparājayavyalīkān āmantryotsukavanitātpatadvisṛṣṭāḥ svāni svāny avanibhujaḥ purāṇi jagmuḥ  Ragh te rekādhvajakuliśātapatraicihnaṃ samrājaś caraṇayugaṃ prasādalabhyam prasthānapraṇatibhir aṅgulīṣu cakrur maulisrakcyutamakarandareṇugauram  Ragh tam adhvare viśvajiti kṣitīśaṃ niḥśeṣaviśrāṇitakośajātam upāttavidyo gurudakṣinārthī kautsaḥ prapede varatantuśiṣyaḥ  Ragh sa mṛnmaye vītahiraṇmayatvāt pātre nidhāyārgahyam anarghyaśīlaḥ śrutaprakāśaṃ yaśasā prakāśaḥ pratyujjagāmātithim ātitheyaḥ  Ragh tam arcayitvā vidhivad vidhijñas tapodhanaṃ mānadhanāgrayāyī viśāṃpatir viṣṭarabhājam ārāt kṛtāñjaliḥ kṛtyavid ita uvāca  Ragh apy agraṇīr mantrakṛtām ṛṣīṇāṃ kuśāgrabuddhe kuśalī gurus te yatas tvayā jñānam aśeṣam āptam lokena caitanyam ivoṣṇaraśmeḥ  Ragh kāyena vācā manasāpi śaśvad yat saṃbhṛtaṃ vāsavadhairyalopi āpādyate na vyayam antarāyaiḥ kaccin maharṣes trividhaṃ tapas tat  Ragh ādhārabandhapramukhaiḥ prayatnaiḥ saṃvardhitānāṃ sutanirviśeṣam kaccin na vāyvādir upaplavo vaḥ śramacchidaṃ āśramapādapānām  Ragh kriyānimitteṣv api vatsalatvād abhagnakāmā munibhiḥ kuśeṣu tadaṅkaśayyācyutanābhinālā kaccin mṛgīṇām anaghā prasūtiḥ  Ragh nirvartyate yair niyamābhiṣeko yebhyo nivāpāñjalayaḥ pitḥṇām tāny uñchaṣaṣṭhāṅkitasaikatāni śivāni vas tīrthajalāni kaccit  Ragh nīvārapākādi kaḍamgarīyair āmṛśyate jānapadair na kaccit kālopapannātithikalpabhāgaṃ vanyaṃ śarīrasthitisādhanaṃ vaḥ  Ragh api prasannena maharṣiṇā tvaṃ samyag vinīyānumato gṛhāya kālo hy ayaṃ saṃkramituṃ dvitīyaṃ sarvopakārakṣamam āśramaṃ te  Ragh tavārhato nābhigamena tṛptaṃ mano niyogakriyayotsukaṃ me apy ājñayā śāsitur ātmanā vā prāpto si saṃbhāvayituṃ vanān mām  Ragh ity arghyapātrānumitavyayasya raghor udārām api gāṃ niśamya svārthopapattiṃ prati durbalāśas tam ity avocad varatantuśiṣyaḥ  Ragh sarvatra no vārttam avehi rājan nāthe kutas tvavy aśubhaṃ prajānām sūrye tapaty āvaraṇāya dṛṣṭeḥ kalpeta lokasya kathaṃ tamisrā  Ragh bhaktiḥ pratīkṣyeṣu kulocitā te pūrvān mahābhāga tayā tiśeṣe vyatītakālas tv aham abhyupetas tvām arthibhāvād iti me viṣādaḥ  Ragh śarīramātreṇa narendra tiṣṭhann ābhāsi tīrthapratipāditarddhiḥ āraṇyakopāttaphalaprasūtiḥ stambena nīvāra ivāvaśiṣṭaḥ  Ragh sthāne bhavān ekanarādhipaḥ sann akiṃcanatvaṃ makhajaṃ vyanakti paryāyapītasya surair himāṃśoḥ kalākṣayaḥ ślāghyataro hi vṛddheḥ  Ragh tadanyatas tāvad ananyakāryo gurvartham āhartum ahaṃ yatiṣye svasty astu te nirgalitāmbugarbhaṃ śaradghanaṃ nārdati cātako pi  Ragh etāvad uktvā pratiyātukāmaṃ śiṣyaṃ maharṣer nṛpatir niṣidhya kiṃ vastu vidvan gurave pradeyaṃ tvayā kiyad veti tam anvayuṅkta  Ragh tato yathāvadvihitādhvarāya tasmai smayāveśavivarjitāya varṇāśramāṇāṃ gurave sa varṇī vicakṣaṇaḥ prastutam ācacakṣe  Ragh samāptavidyena mayā maharṣir vijñāpito bhūd gurudakṣiṇāyai sa me cirāyāskhalitopacārāṃ tāṃ bhaktim evāgaṇayat purastāt  Ragh nirbandhasaṃjātaruṣārthakārśyam acintayitvā guruṇāham uktaḥ vittasya vidyāparisaṃkhyayā me koṭīṣ catasro daśa cāhareti  Ragh so haṃ saparyāvidhibhājanena matvā bahvantaṃ prabhuśabdaśeṣam abhyutsahe saṃprati noparoddhum alpetaratvāc chrutaniṣkrayasya  Ragh itthaṃ dvijena dvijarākāntir āvedito vedavidāṃ vareṇa enonivṛttendriyavṛttir enaṃ jagāda bhūyo jagadekanāthaḥ  Ragh gurvartham arthī śrutapāradṛśvā raghoḥ sakāśād anavāpya kāmam gato vadāyāntaram ity ayaṃ me mā bhūt parīvādanavāvatāraḥ  Ragh sa tvaṃ praśaste mahite madīye vasaṃś caturtho gnir ivāgnyagāre dvitrāṇy ahāny arhasi soḍhum arhan yāvad yate sādhayituṃ tvadartham  Ragh tatheti tasy āvitathaṃ pratītaḥ pratyagrahīt saṃgaram agrajanmā gām āttasārāṃ raghur apy avekṣya niṣkaṣṭum arthaṃ cakame kuberāt  Ragh vasiṣṭhamantrokṣaṇajāt prabhāvād udanvadākāśamahīdhareṣu marutsakhasyeva balāhakasya gatir vijaghne na hi tadrathasya  Ragh athādhiśiśye prayathaḥ pradoṣe rathaṃ raghuḥ kalpitaśastragarbham sāmantasaṃbhāvanayaiva dhīraḥ kailāsanāthaṃ tarasā jigīṣuḥ  Ragh prātaḥ prayāṇābhimukhāya tasmai savismayāḥ kośagṛhe niyuktāḥ hiraṇmayīṃ kośagṛhasya madhye vṛṣṭiṃ śaśaṃsuḥ patitāṃ nabhastaḥ  Ragh taṃ bhūpatir bhāsurahemarāśiṃ labdhaṃ kuberād abhiyāsyamānāt dideśa kautasya samastam eva pādaṃ sumeror iva vajrabhinnam  Ragh janasya sāketanivāsinas tau dvāv apy abhūtām abhinandyasattvau gurupradeyādhikanīḥspṛho rthī nṛpo rthikāmād adhikapradaś ca  Ragh athoṣṭravāmīśatavāhitārthaṃ prajeṣvaraṃ prītamanā maharṣiḥ spṛṣan kareṇānatapūrvakāyaṃ saṃprasthito vācam uvāca kautsaḥ  Ragh kim atra citraṃ yadi kāmasūr bhūr vṛtte sthitasyādhipateḥ prajānām acintanīyas tu tava prabhāvo manīṣitaṃ dyaur api yena dugdhā  Ragh āśāsyam anyat punaruktabhūtaṃ śreyāṃsi sarvāṇy adhijagmuṣas te putraṃ labhasvātmaguṇānurūpaṃ bhavantam īḍaṃ bhavataḥ piteva  Ragh itthaṃ prayujyāśiṣam agrajanmā rājñe pratīyāya guroḥ sakāśam rājāpi lebhe sutam āśu tasmād ālokam arkād iva jīvalokaḥ  Ragh brāhme muhūrte kila tasya devī kumārakalpaṃ suṣuve kumāram ataḥ pitā brahmaṇa eva nāmnā tam ātmajanmānam ajaṃ cakāra  Ragh rūpaṃ tad ojasvi tad eva vīryaṃ tadaiva naisargikam unnatatvam na kāraṇāt svād bibhide kumāraḥ pravartito dīpa iva pradīpāt  Ragh upāttavidyaṃ vidhivad gurubhyas taṃ yauvanodbhedaviśeṣakāntam śrīr gantukāmāpi guror anujñāṃ dhīreva kanyā pitur ācakāṅkṣa  Ragh atheśvareṇa krathakaiśikānāṃ svayaṃvarārthaṃ svasur indumatyāḥ āptaḥ kumārānayanotsukena bhojena dūto raghave visṛṣṭaḥ  Ragh taṃ ślāghyasaṃbandham asau vicintya dārakriyāyogyadaśaṃ ca putram prasthāpayām āsa sasainyam enam ṛddhāṃ vidarbhādhiparājadhānīm  Ragh tasyopakāryāracitopakārā vanyetarā jānapadopadābhiḥ mārge nivāsā manujendrasūnor babhūvur udyānavihārakalpāḥ  Ragh sa narmadārodhasi śīkarārdrair marudbhir ānartitanaktamāle niveśayām āsa vilaṅghitādhvā klāntaṃ rajodhūsaraketu sainyam  Ragh athopariṣṭād bhramarair bhramadbhiḥ prāk sūcitāntaḥsalilapraveśaḥ nirdhauta dānāmalagaṇḍabhittir yanyaḥ saritto gaja unmamajja  Ragh niḥśeṣavikṣālitadhātunāpi vaprakriyām ṛkṣavatas taṭeṣu nīlordhvarekhāśabalena śaṃsan dantadvayenāśmavikuṇṭhitena  Ragh saṃhāravikṣepalaghukriyeṇa hastena tīrābhimukhaḥ saśabdam babhau sa bhindan bṛhatas taraṅgān vāryargalābhaṅga iva pravṛttaḥ  Ragh sa bhogibhogādhikapīvareṇa hastena tīrābhimukhaḥ saśabdam saṃvardhitārtdhaprahitena dīrghān cikṣepa vārīparighān ivormīn  Ragh śailopamaḥ śaivalamañjarīṇāṃ jālāni karṣann urasā sa paścāt pūrvaṃ tadutpīḍitavārirāśiḥ saritpravāhas taṭam utsasarpa  Ragh kāraṇḍavotsṛṣṭamṛdupratnānāḥ pulindayoṣāmbuvihārakāñcīḥ karṣan sa śaivālalatā nadīṣaḥ skandhāvalagnās taṭam utsasarpa  Ragh tasyaikanāgasya kapolabhittyor jalāvagāhakṣaṇamātraśāntā vanyetarānekapadarśanena punar didīpe madadurdinaśrīḥ  Ragh saptacchadakṣīrakaṭupravāham asahyam āghrāya madaṃ tadīyam vilaṅghitādhoraṇatīvrayatnāḥ senāgajendrā vimukhā babhūvuḥ  Ragh sa cchinnabandhadrutayugyaśūnyaṃ bhagnākṣaparyastarathaṃ kṣaṇena rāmāparitāṇavihastayodhaṃ senāniveśaṃ tumulaṃ cakāra  Ragh tam āpatantaṃ nṛpater avadhyo vanyaḥ karīti śrutavān kumāraḥ nivartayiṣyan viśikhena kumbhe jaghāna nātyāyatakṛṣṭaśārṅgaḥ  Ragh sa viddhamātraḥ kila nāgarūpam utsṛjya tadvismitasainyadṛṣṭaḥ sphuratprabhāmaṇḍalamadhyavarti kāntaṃ vapur vyomacaraṃ prapede  Ragh atha prabhāvopanataiḥ kumāraṃ kalpadrumotthair avakīrya puṣpaiḥ uvāca vāgmī daśanaprabhābhiḥ saṃvardhitoraḥsthalatārahāraḥ  Ragh mataṅgaśāpād avalepamūlād avāptavān asmi mataṅgajatvam avehi gandharvapates tanūjaṃ priyaṃvadaṃ māṃ priyadarśanasya  Ragh sa cānunītaḥ praṇatena paścān mayā maharṣir mṛdutām agacchat uṣṇatvam agnyātapasaṃprayogāc chaityaṃ hi yat sā prakṛtir jalasya  Ragh ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhavo yadā te bhetsyaty ajaḥ kumbham ayomukhena saṃyokṣyase svena vapurmahimnā tadety avocat sa taponidhir mām  Ragh saṃmocitaḥ sattvavatā tvayāhaṃ śāpāc ciraprārthitadarśanena pratipriyaṃ ced bhavato na kuryāṃ vṛthā hi me syāt svapadopalabdhiḥ  Ragh saṃmohanaṃ nāma sakhe mamāstraṃ prayogasaṃhāravibhaktamantram gāndharvam ādhatsva yataḥ prayoktur na cārihiṃsā vijayaś ca haste  Ragh alaṃ hriyā māṃ prati yan muhūrtaṃ dayāparo bhuḥ praharann api tvam tasmād upacchandayati prayojaṃ mayi tvayā na pratiśedharaukṣyam  Ragh tathety upaspṛśya payaḥ pavitraṃ somodhbavāyāḥ sarito nṛsomaḥ udaṅmukhaḥ so stravid astramantraṃ jagrāha tasmān nigṛhītaśāpāt  Ragh evaṃ tayor adhvani daivayogād āseduṣoḥ sakhyam acintyahetu eko yayau caitrarathapadeśān saurājyaramyān aparo vidarbhān  Ragh taṃ tasthivāṃsaṃ nagaropakaṇṭhe tadāgamārūḍhagurupraharṣaḥ pratyujjagāma krathakaiśikendraś candraṃ pravṛddhormir ivormimālī  Ragh praveśya cainaṃ puram agrayāyī nīcais tathopācarad arpitaśrīḥ mene yathā tatra janaḥ sameto vaidarbham āgantum ajaṃ gṛheśam  Ragh tasy ādhikārapuruṣaiḥ praṇataiḥ pradiṣṭāṃ prāgdvāravediviniveśitapūrṇa kumbhām mene yathā tatra janaḥ sameto bālyāt parām iva daśāṃ madano dhyuvāsa  Ragh tatra svayaṃvarasamāhṛtarājalokaṃ kanyālalāma kamanīyam ajasya lipsoḥ bhāvāvabodhakaluṣā dayiteva rātrau nidrā cireṇa nayanābhimukhī babhūva  Ragh taṃ karṇabhūṣaṇanipīḍitapīvarāṃsaṃ śayyottaracchadavimardakṛśāṅgarāgam sūtātmajāḥ savayasaḥ prathitaprabodhaṃprābodhayann uṣasi vāgbhir udāravācaḥ  Ragh rātrir gatā matimatāṃ vara muñca śayyāṃ dhātrā dvidhaiva nanu dhūr jagato vibhaktā tām ekatas tava bibharti gurur vinidras tasyā bhavān aparadhuryapadāvalambī  Ragh nidrāvaśena bhavatāpy anapekṣamāṇā paryutsukatvam abalā niśi khaṇḍiteva lakṣmīr vinodayati yena digantalambī so pi tvadānanaruciṃ vijahāti candraḥ  Ragh tad valgunā yugapadunmiṣitena tāvat sadyaḥ paraparatulām adhirohatāṃ dve praspandamānaparuṣetaratāram antaś cakṣus tava pracalitabhramaraṃ ca padmam  Ragh vṛntāc chlathaṃ harati puṣpam anokahānāṃ saṃsṛjyate sarasijair aruṇāmśubhinnaiḥ svābhāvikaṃ paraguṇena vibhātavāyuḥ saurabhyam īpsur iva te mukhamārutasya  Ragh tāmrodareṣu paitaṃ tarupallaveṣu nirdhauta hāragulikāviśadaṃ himāmbhaḥ ābhāti labdhaparabhāgatayādharoṣṭhe līlāsmitaṃ sadaśanārcir iva tvadīyam  Ragh yāvat pratāpanidhir ākramate na bhānur ahnāya tāvad aruṇena tamo nirastam āyodhanāgrasaratāṃ tvayi vīra yāte kiṃ vā ripūṃs tava guruḥ svayam ucchinatti  Ragh śayyāṃ jahaty ubhayapakṣavinītanidrāḥ stamberamā mukharaśṛṅkhalakarṣiṇas te yeṣāṃ vibhānti taruṇāruṇarāgayogād bhinnādrigairikataṭā iva dantakoṣāḥ  Ragh dīrgheṣv amī niyamitāḥ paṭamaṇḍapeṣu nidrāṃ vihāya vanajākṣa vanāyudeśyāḥ vaktroṣmaṇā malinayanti purogatāni lehyāni saindhavaśilāśakalāni vāhāḥ  Ragh bhavati viralabhaktir mlānapuṣpopahāraḥ svakiraṇpariveṣodhbedaśūnyāḥ pradīpāḥ ayam api ca giraṃ nas tvatprabodhaprayuktām anuvadati śukas te mañjuvāk pañjarasthaḥ  Ragh iti viracitavāgbhir bandiputraiḥ kumāraḥ sapadi vigatanidras talpam ujjhāṃ cakāra madapaṭu ninadadbhir bodhito rājahaṃsaiḥ suragaja iva gāṅgaṃ saikataṃ supratīkaḥ  Ragh atha vidhim avasāyya śāstradṛṣṭaṃ divasamukhocitam añcitākṣipakṣmā kuśalaviracitānukūlaveṣaḥ kṣitipasamājam agāt svayaṃvarastham  Ragh sa tatra mañceṣu manojñaveṣān siṃhāsanasthān upacāravastu vaimānikānāṃ marutām apaśyad ākṛṣṭalīlān naralokapālān  Ragh rater gṛhītānunayena kāmaṃ pratyarpitasvāṅgam iveśvareṇa kākutstham ālokayatāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ mano babhūvendumatīnirāśam  Ragh vaidarbhanirdiṣṭam asau kumāraḥ kḷptena sopānapathena mañcam śilāvibhaṅgair mṛgarājaśāvas tuṅgaṃ nagotsaṅgam ivāruroha  Ragh parārdhyavarṇāstaraṇopapannam āsedivān ratnavad  āsanaṃ saḥ bhūyiṣṭham āsīd upameyakāntir mayūrapṛṣṭhāśrayiṇā guhena  Ragh tāsu śriyā rājaparaṃparāsu prabhāviśeṣodayadurnirīkṣyaḥ sahasradhātmā vyarucad vibhaktaḥ payomucāṃ paṅktiṣu vidyuteva  Ragh teṣāṃ mahārhāsanasaṃsthitānām udāranepathyabhṛtāṃ sa madhye rarāja dhāmnā raghusūnur eva kalpadrumāṇām iva pārijātaḥ  Ragh netravrajāḥ paurajanasya tasmin vihāya sarvān nṛpatīn nipetuḥ madotkaṭe recitapuṣpavṛkṣā gandhadvipe vanya iva dvirephāḥ  Ragh atha stute bandibhir anvayajñaiḥ somārkavaṃśye naradevaloke saṃcārite c āgārusārayonau dhūpe samutsarpati vaijayantīḥ  Ragh puropakaṇṭhopavanāśrayāṇāṃ kalāpinām uddhatanṛtyahetau pradhmātaśaṅkhe parito digantāṃs tūryasvane mūrchati maṅgalārthe  Ragh manuṣyavāhyaṃ caturaśrayānam adhyāsya kanyā parivāraśobhi viveśa mañcāntararājamārgaṃ patiṃvarā kḷptavivāhaveṣā  Ragh tasmin vidhānātiśaye vidhātuḥ kanyāmaye netraśataikalakṣye nipetur antaḥkaraṇair narendrā dehaiḥ sthitāḥ kevalam āsaneṣu  Ragh tāṃ praty abhivyaktamanorathānāṃ mahīpatīnāṃ praṇayāgradūtyaḥ pravālośobhā iva pādapānāṃ śṛṅgāraceṣṭa vividhā babhūvuḥ  Ragh kaścit karābhyām upagūḍhanālam ālolapattrābhihatadvirepham rajobhir antaḥ pariveṣabandhi līlāravindaṃ bhramayāṃ cakāra  Ragh visrastam aṃsād aparo vilāsī ratnānuviddhāṅgadakoṭilagnam prālambam utkṛṣya yathāvakaśaṃ nināya sācīkṛtacāruvaktraḥ  Ragh ākuñcitāgrāṅgulinā tato nyaḥ kiṃcitsamāvarjitanetraśobhaḥ tiryagvisaṃsarpinakhaprabheṇa pādena haimaṃ vililekha pīṭham  Ragh niveśya vāmaṃ bhujam āsanārdhe tatasaṃniveśād adhikonnatāṃsaḥ kaścid vivṛttatrikabhinnahāraḥ suhṛtsamābhāṣaṇatatparo bhūt  Ragh vilāsinīvibhramadantapattram āpāṇḍu raṃ ketakabarham anyaḥ priyāitambocitasaṃniveśair vipāṭayām āsa yuvā nakhāgraiḥ  Ragh kuśeśayātāmratalena kaścit kareṇa rekhādhvajalāñchanena ratnāṅgulīyaprabhayānuviddhān udīrayām āsa salīlam akṣān  Ragh kaścid yathābhāgam avasthite pi svasaṃniveśād vyatilaṅghinīva vajrāṃśugarbhāṅgulirandhram ekaṃ vyāpārayām āsa karaṃ kirīṭe  Ragh tato nṛpāṇāṃ śrutavṛttavaṃśā puṃvat pragalbhā pratihārarakṣī prāk saṃnikarṣaṃ magadheśvarasya nītvā kumārīm avadat sunandā  Ragh asau śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇonmukhānām agādhasattvo magadhapratiṣṭhaḥ rājā prajārañjanalabdhavarṇaḥ paraṃtapo nāma yathārthanāmā  Ragh kāmaṃ ṇrpāḥ santu saharaśo nye rājanvatīm āhur anena bhūmim nakṣatratārāgrahasaṃkulāpi jyotiṣmatī candramasaiva rātriḥ  Ragh kriyāprabandhād ayam adhvarāṇām ajasram āhūtasahasranetraḥ śacyāś ciraṃ pāṇdukapolalambān mandāraśūnyān alakāṃś cakāra  Ragh anena ced icchasi gṛhyamāṇaṃ pāṇiṃ vareṇyena kuru praveśe prāsādavātāyanasaṃśritānāṃ netrotsatvaṃ puṣpapurāṅganānām  Ragh evaṃ tayokte tam avekṣya kiṃcid visraṃsidūrvāṅkamadhūkamālā ṛjupraṇāmakriyayaiva tanvī pratyādideśainam abhāṣamāṇā  Ragh tāṃ saiva vetragrahaṇe niyuktā rājāntaraṃ rājasutāṃ nināya samīraṇottheva taraṅgalekhā padmāntaraṃ mānasarājahaṃsīm  Ragh jagāda cainām ayam aṅganāthaḥ surāṅganāprārthitayauvanaśrīḥ vinītanāgaḥ kila sūtrakārair aindraṃ padaṃ bhūmigato pi bhuṅkte  Ragh anena paryāsayatāsrabindūn muktāphalsthūlatamān staneṣu pratyarpitāḥ śatruvilāsinīnām unmucya sūtreṇa vinaiva hārāḥ  Ragh nisargabhinnāspadam ekasaṃstham asmin dvayaṃ śrīś ca sarasvatī ca kāntyā girā sūnṛtayā ca yogyā tvam eva kalyāṇi tayos tṛtīyā  Ragh athāṅgarājād avatārya cakṣur yāh janyām avadat kumārī nāsau na kāmyo na ca veda samyag draṣṭuṃ na sā bhinnarucir hi lokaḥ  Ragh tataḥ paraṃ duṣprasahaṃ dviṣadbhir nṛpaṃ niyuktā pratihārabhūmau nidarśayām āsa viśeṣadṛśyam induṃ navotthānam ivendumatyai  Ragh avantinātho yam udagrabāhur viśālavakṣās tanuvṛttamadhyaḥ āropya cakrabhrahmam uṣṇatejās tvaṣṭreva yatnollikhito vibhāti  Ragh asya prayāṇeṣu samagraśakter agresarair vājibhir utthitāni kurvanti sāmantaśikhāmaṇīnāṃ prabhāprarohāstamayaṃ rajāṃsi  Ragh asau mahākālaniketanasya vasann adūre kila candramauleḥ tamisrapakṣe pi saha priyābhir jyotsnāvato nirviśati pradoṣān  Ragh anena yūnā saha pārthivena rambhoru kaccin manaso rucis te siprātaraṅgānilakampitāsu vihartum udyānaparaṃparāsu  Ragh tasminn abhidyotitabandhupadme pratāpasaṃśoṣitaśatrupaṅke babandha sā nottamasaukumāryā kumudvatī bhānumatīva bhāvam  Ragh tām agratas tāmarasāntarābhām anūparājasya guṇair anūnām vidhāya sṛṣṭiṃ lalitām vidhātur jagāda bhūyaḥ sudatīṃ sunandā  Ragh saṃgrāmanirviṣṭasahasrabāhur aṣṭadāsadvīpanikhātayūpaḥ ananyasādhāraṇarājaśabdo babhūva yogī kila kārtavīryaḥ  Ragh akāryacintāsamakālam eva prādurbhavaṃś cāpadharaḥ purastāt antaḥśarīreṣv api yaḥ prajānāṃ pratyādideśāvinayaṃ vinetā  Ragh jyābandhaniṣpandabhujena yasya viniśvasadvaktraparaṃpareṇa kārāgṛhe nirjitavāsavena laṅkeśvareṇoṣitam ā prasādāt  Ragh tasyānvaye bhūpatir eṣa jātaḥ pratīpa ity āgamavṛddhasevī yena śriyaḥ saṃśrayadoṣarūḍhaṃ svabhāvalolety ayaśaḥ pramṛśṭam  Ragh āyodhane kṛṣṇagatiṃ sahāyam avāpya yaḥ kṣatriyakālarātrim dhārāṃ śitāṃ rāmaparaśvadhasya saṃbhāvayaty utpalapattrasārām  Ragh asyāṅkalakṣmīr bhava dīrghabāhor māhiṣmatīvapranitambakāñcīm prāsādajālair jalveṇiramyāṃ revāṃ yadi prekṣitum asti kāmaḥ  Ragh tasyāḥ prakāmaṃ priyadarśano pi na sa kṣitīśo rucaye babhūva śaratpramṛṣṭāmbudharoparodhaḥ śaśīva paryāptakalo nalinyāḥ  Ragh sā śūrasendādhipatiṃ suṣeṇam uddiśya lokāntaragītakīrtim ācāraśuddhobhayavaṃśadīpaṃ śuddhāntarakṣyā jagade kumārī  Ragh nīpānvayaḥ pārthiva eṣa vajvā guṇair yam āśritya paraspareṇa siddhāśramaṃ śāntam ivaitya sattvair naisargiko py utsasṛje virodhaḥ  Ragh yasy ātmagehe nayanābhirāmā kāntir himāṃśor iva saṃniviṣṭa harmyāgrasaṃrūḍhatṛṇāṅkureṣu tejo viśahyaṃ ripumandireṣu  Ragh yasyāvarodhastanacandanānāṃ prakṣālanād vārivihārakāle kalindakanyā mathurāṃ gatā pi gaṅgormisaṃsakta jaleva bhāti  Ragh trastena tākrṣyāt kila kāliyena maṇiṃ visṛṣṭaṃ yamunaukasā yaḥ vakṣaḥsthalavyāpirucaṃ dadhānaḥ sakaustubhaṃ hrepayatīva kṛṣnam  Ragh saṃbhāvya bhartāram amuṃ yuvānaṃ mṛdupravālottarapuṣpaśayye vṛndāvane caitrarathād anūne nirviśyatāṃ sundari yuvanaśrīḥ  Ragh adhyāsya cāmbhaḥpṛṣatokṣitāni śaileyagandhīni śilātalāni kalāpināṃ prāvṛṣi paśya nṛtyaṃ kāntāsu govardhanakandarāsu  Ragh nṛpaṃ tam āvartamanojñanābhiḥ sā vyatyagād anyavadhūr bhavitrī mahīdharaṃ mārgavaśād upetaṃ srotovahā sāgaragāminīva  Ragh athāṅgadāśliṣṭabhujaṃ bhujiṣyā hemāṅgadaṃ nāma kaliṅganātham āseduṣīṃ sāditaśatrupakṣaṃ bālām abālendumukhīṃ babhāṣe  Ragh asau mahendrādrisamānasāraḥ patir mahendrasya mahodadheś ca yasya kṣaratsainyagajacchalena yātrāsu yātīva puro mahendraḥ  Ragh jyāghātarekhe subhujo bhujābhyāṃ bibharti yaś cāpabhṛtāṃ purogaḥ ripuśriyāṃ sāñjanabhāṣpaseke bandīkṛṭānām iva paddhatī dve  Ragh raṇe mitatrīṇatayā prakāśaḥ śarāsanajyānikaṣau bhujābhyām viśiṣṭarekhau ripuvikramāgner nirvāṇamārgāv iva yo bibharti  Ragh yam ātmanaḥ sadmani saṃnikṛṣṭo mandradhvanityājitayāmatūryaḥ prāsādavātāyanadṛṣyavīciḥ prabodhayaty arṇava eva suptam  Ragh anena sārdhaṃ viharāmburāśes tīreṣu tālīvanamarmareṣu dvīpānatarānītalavaṅgapuṣpair apākṛtasvedalavā marudbhiḥ  Ragh pralobhitāpy ākṛtilobhanīyā patiṃ purasyorugapūrvanāmnaḥ tasmād apāvartata dūrakṛṣṭā nītyeva lakṣmīḥ pratikūladaivāt  Ragh athādhigamyābhuvarājakalpaṃ patiṃ purasyorugapūrvanāmnaḥ ācārapūtobhayavaṃśadīpaṃ śuddhāntarakṣyā jagade kumārī  Ragh athorākhyasya purasya nāthaṃ dauvārikī devasarūpam itaś cakorākṣi vilokayeti pūrvānuśiṣṭāṃ nijagāda bhojyām  Ragh pāṇḍyo yam aṃsārpitalambahāraḥ kḷptāṅgarāgo haricandanena ābhāti bālātaparaktasānuḥ sanirjharodgāra ivādrirājaḥ  Ragh vindhyasya saṃstambhayitā mahādrer niḥśeṣapītojjhitasindhurājaḥ prītyāśvamedhāvabhṛthārdramūrteḥ sausnātiko yasya bhavaty agastyaḥ  Ragh astraṃ harād āptavatā durāpaṃ yenendralokāva jayāya dṛptaḥ purā janasthānavimardaśaṅkī saṃdhāya laḥkādhipatiḥ pratasthe  Ragh anena pāṇau vidhivad gṛhīte mahākulīnena mahīva gurvī ratnānuviddhārṇavamekhalāyā diśaḥ sapatnī bhava dakṣiṇasyāḥ  Ragh tāmbūlavallīpariṇaddhapūgāsv elālatāliṅgitacandanāsu tamālapattrāstaraṇāsu rantuṃ prasīda śaśvan malayasthalīṣu  Ragh indīvaraśyāmatanaur nṛpo sau tvaṃ rocanāgauraśarīrayaṣṭiḥ anyonyaśobhāparivṛddhaye vāṃ yogas taḍittoyadayor ivāstu  Ragh svasur vidarbhādhipates tadīyo lebhe ntaraṃ cetasi nopadeśaḥ divākarādarśanabaddhakośe nakśatranāthāṃśur ivāravinde  Ragh saṃcāriṇī dīpaśikheva rātrau yaṃ yaṃ vyatīyāya patiṃvarā sā narendramārgāṭṭa iva prapede vivarṇabhāvaṃ sa sa bhūmipālaḥ  Ragh tasyāṃ raghoḥ sūnur upasthitāyāṃ vṛṇīta māṃ neti samākulo bhūt vāmetaraḥ saṃśayam asya bāhuḥ keyūrabandhocchavasitair nunoda  Ragh taṃ prāpya sarvāvayavānavadyaṃ vyāvartatānyopagamāt kumārī na hi praphullaṃ sahakāram etya vṛksāntaraṃ kāṅkṣati ṣaṭpadālī  Ragh tasmin samāveśitacittavṛttim induprabhām indumatīm avekṣya pracakrame vaktum anukramajñā savistaraṃ vākyam idaṃ sunandā  Ragh ikṣvākuvaṃśyaḥ kakudaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ kakutstha ity āhitalakṣaṇo bhūt kākutsthaśabdaṃ yata unnatecchāḥ ślāghyaṃ dadhaty uttarakosalendrāḥ  Ragh mahendram āsthāya mahokṣarūpaṃ yaḥ saṃyati prāptapināki līlaḥ cakāra bāṇair asurāṅganānāṃ gaṇḍasthalīḥ proṣitapattralekhāḥ  Ragh airāvatāsphālanaviślathaṃ yaḥ saṃghaṭṭayann aṅgadam aṅgadena upeyuśaḥ svām api mūrtim agryām ardhāsanaṃ gotrabhido dhitaṣṭhau  Ragh jātaḥ kule tasya kilorukīrtiḥ kulapradīpo nṛpatir dilīpaḥ atiṣṭhad ekonaśatakratutve śakrābhyasūyāvinivṛttaye yaḥ  Ragh yasmin mahīṃ śāsati vāṇinīnāṃ nidrāṃ vihārārdhapathe gatānām vāto pi nāsaraṃsayad aṃśukāni ko lambayed āharaṇāya hastam  Ragh putro raghus tasya padaṃ praśāsti mahākrator viśvajitaḥ prayoktā caturdigāvarjitasaṃbhṛtāṃ yo mṛtpātraśeṣām akarod vibhūtim  Ragh ārūḍham adrīn udadhīn vitīrṇaṃ bhujaṃgamānāṃ vasatiṃ praviṣṭam ūrdhvaṃ gataṃ yasya na cānubandhi yaśaḥ paricchettum iyattayālam  Ragh asau kumāras tam ajo nujātas triviṣṭapasyeva patiṃ jayantaḥ gurvīṃ dhuraṃ yo bhuvanasya pitrā dhuryeṇa damyaḥ sadṛśaṃ bibharti  Ragh kulena kāntyā vayasā navena guṇaiś ca tais tair vinayapradhānaiḥ tvam ātmanas tulyam amuṃ vṛṇīṣva ratnaṃ samāgacchatu kāñcanena  Ragh tataḥ sunandāvacanāvasāne lajjāṃ tanū kṛtya narendrakanyā dṛṣṭyā prasādāmalayā kumāraṃ pratyagrahīt saṃvaraṇasrajeva  Ragh sā yūni tasminn abhilāṣabandhaṃ śaśāka śālīnatayā na vaktum romāñcalakṣyeṇa sa gātrayaṣṭiṃ bhittvā nirākrāmad arālakeśyāḥ  Ragh tathāgatāyāṃ parihāsapūrvaṃ sakhyāṃ sakhī vetradharā babhāṣe ārye vrajāmo nyata ity athaināṃ vadhūr asūyākuṭilaṃ dadarśa  Ragh sā cūrṇagauraṃ raghunandanasya dhātrīkarābhyāṃ karabhopamorūḥ āsañjayām āsa yathāpradeśaṃ kaṇṭhe guṇaṃ mūrtam ivānurāgam  Ragh tayā srajā maṅgalapuṣpamayyā viśālavakṣaḥsthalalambayā saḥ amaṃsta kaṇṭhārpitabāhupāśāṃ vidarbharājāvarajāṃ vareṇyaḥ  Ragh śaśinam upagateyaṃ kaumudī meghamuktaṃ jalanidhim anurūpaṃ iti samaguṇayogaprītayas tatra paurāḥ śravaṇakaṭu nṛpāṇām ekavākyaṃ vivavruḥ  Ragh pramuditavarapakṣam ekatas tat kṣitipatimaṇḍalam anyato vitānam uṣasi sara iva praphullapadmaṃ kumudavanapratipannanidram āsīt  Ragh athopayantrā sadṛśena yuktāṃ skandena sākṣād iva devasenām svasāram ādāya vidarbhanāthaḥ purapraveśābhimukho babhūva  Ragh senāniveśān pṛthivīkṣito pi jagmur vibhātagrahamandabhāsaḥ bhojyāṃ prati vyarthamanorathatvād rūpeṣu veṣeṣu ca sābhyasūyāḥ  Ragh sāṃnidhyayogāt kila tatra śacyāḥ svayaṃvarakṣobhakṛtām abhāvaḥ kākutstham uddiśya samatsaro pi śaśāma tena kṣitipālalokaḥ  Ragh tāvat prakīrṇābhinavopacāram indrāyudhadyotitatoraṇāṅkam varaḥ sa vadhvā saha rājamārgaṃ prāpa dhvajacchāyanivāritoṣṇam  Ragh tatas tadālokanatatparāṇāṃ saudheṣu cāmīkarajālavatsu babhūvur itthaṃ purasundarīṇāṃ tyaktānyakāryāṇi viceṣṭitāni  Ragh ālokamārgaṃ sahasā vrajantyā kayācid udveṣṭanavāntamālyaḥ baddhuṃ na saṃbhāvita eva tāvat kareṇa ruddho pi hi keśapāśaḥ  Ragh prasādhikālambitam agrapādam ākṣipya kācid dravarāgam eva utṣṛṣṛalīlāgatir ā gavākṣād yayau śalākām aparā vahantī  Ragh vilocanaṃ dakṣiṇam añjanena saṃbhāvya tadvañcitavāmanetrā tathaiva vātāyanasaṃnikarṣaṃ yayau śalākām aparā vahantī  Ragh jālāntarapreṣitadṛṣṭir anyā prasthānabhinnāṃ na babandha nīvīm nābhipraviṣṭābharaṇaprabheṇa hastena tasthāv avalambya vāsaḥ  Ragh ardhācitā satvaram utthitāyāḥ pade pade durnimite galantī kasyāścid āsīd raśanā tadānīm aṅguṣṭhamāulārpitasūtraśeṣā  Ragh stanaṃdhayantaṃ tanayaṃ vihāya vilokanāya tvarayā vrajantī saṃprasnutābhyāṃ padavīṃ stanābhyāṃ siṣeca kācit payas ā gavākṣāt  Ragh tāsāṃ mukhair āsavagandhagarbhair vyāptāntarāḥ sāndrakutūhalānām vilolanetrabhramarair gavākṣāḥ sahasrapattrābharaṇā ivāsan  Ragh tā rāghavaṃ dṛṣṭibhir āpibantyo nāryo na jagmur viṣayāntarāṇi tathā hi śeṣendriyavṛttir āsāṃ sarvātmanā cakṣur iva praviṣṭā  Ragh sthāne vṛtā bhūpatibhiḥ parokṣaiḥ svayaṃvaraṃ sādhum amaṃsta bhojyā padmeva nārāyaṇam anyathāsau labheta kāntaṃ katham ātmatulyam  Ragh paraspareṇa spṛhaṇīyaśobhaṃ na ced idaṃ dvandvam ayojayiṣyat asmin dvaye rūpavidhānayatnaḥ patyuḥ prajānāṃ vitatho bhaviṣyat  Ragh ratismarau nūnam imāv abhūtāṃ rājñāṃ sahareṣu tathā hi bālā gateyam ātmapratirūpam eva mano hi janmāntarasaṃgatijñam  Ragh ity udgatāḥ pauravadhūmukhebhyaḥ śṛṇvan kathāḥ śrotasukhāḥ kumāraḥ udbhāsitaṃ maṅgalasaṃvidhābhiḥ saṃbandhinaḥ sadma samāsasāda  Ragh tato vatīryāśu kareṇukāyāḥ sa kāmarūpeśvaradattahastaḥ vaidarbhanirdiṣṭam atho viveśa nārīmanāṃsīva catuṣkam antaḥ  Ragh mahārhasiṃhāsanasaṃsthito sau saratnam arghyaṃ madhuparkamiśram bhojopanītaṃ ca dukūlayugmaṃ jagrāha sārdhaṃ vanitākaṭākṣaiḥ  Ragh dukūlavāsāḥ sa vadhūsamīpaṃ ninye vinītair avarodharakṣaiḥ velāsākśaṃ sphuṭapeharājir navair udanvān iva candrapādaiḥ  Ragh tatrārcito bhojapateḥ purodhā hutvāgnim ājyādibhir agnikalpaḥ tam eva cādhāya vivāhasākṣye vadhūvarau saṃgamayāṃ cakāra  Ragh hastena hastaṃ parigṛhya vadhvāḥ sa rājasūnuḥ sutarāṃ cakāśe anantarāśokalatāpravālaṃ prāpyeva cūtaḥ pratipallavena  Ragh āsīd varaḥ kaṇṭakitaprakoṣṭaḥ svinnāṅguliḥ saṃvavṛte kumārī vṛttis tayoḥ pāṇisamāgamena samaṃ vibhakteva maobhavasya  Ragh tayor apāṅgapratisāritāni kriyāsamāpattivartitāni hrīyantraṇām ānaśire manojñām anyonyalolāni vilocanāni  Ragh pradakṣiṇaprakramaṇāt kṛṣānor udarciṣas tan mithunaṃ cakāśe meror upānteṣv iva vartamānam anyonyasaṃsaktam ahastriyāmam  Ragh nitambagurvī guruṇā prayuktā vadhūr vidhātṛpratimena tena cakāra sā mattacakoranetrā lajjāvatī lājavisargam agnau  Ragh haviḥśamīpallavalājagandhiḥ puṇyaḥ kṛśānor udiyāya dhūmaḥ kapolasaṃsarpiśikhaḥ sa tasyā muhūrtakarṇotpalatāṃ prapede  Ragh tad añjanakledasamākulākṣaṃ pramlānabhījāṅkurakarṇapūram vadhūmukhaṃ pāṭalagaṇḍalekham ācāradhūmagrahaṇād babhūva  Ragh tau snātakair bandhumatā ca rājñā puraṃdhribhiś ca kramaśaḥ prayuktam kanyākumārau kanakāsanasthāv ārdrākṣatāropaṇam anvabhūtām  Ragh iti svasur bhojakulapradīpaḥ saṃpādya pāṇigrahaṇaṃ sa rājā mahīpatīnāṃ pṛthagarhaṇārthaṃ samādideśādhikṛtān adhiśrīḥ  Ragh liṅgair mudaḥ saṃvṛtavikriyās te hradāḥ prasannā iva gūḍhanakrāḥ vaidarbham āmantrya yayus tadīyāṃ pratyarpya pūjām aupdāchalena  Ragh sa rājalokaḥ kṛtapūrvasaṃvid ārambhasiddhau samayopalabhyam ādāsyamānaḥ pramdāmiṣaṃ tad āvṛtya panthānam ajasya tasthau  Ragh bhartāpi tāvat krathakaiṣikānām anuṣṭhitānantarajāvivāhaḥ sattvānurūpāharaṇī kṛtaśrīḥ prāsthāpayad rāghavam anvagāc ca  Ragh tisras trilokī prathitena sārdham ajena mārge vasatīr uṣitvā tasmād apāvartata kuṇḍineśaḥ parvātyaye soma ivoṣṇaraśmeḥ  Ragh pramanyavaḥ prāg api kosalendre pratyekam āttasvatayā babhūvuḥ ato nṛpāś cakṣamire sametāḥ strīratnalābhaṃ na tadātmajasya  Ragh tam udvahantaṃ pathi bhojakanyāṃ rurodha rājanyagaṇaḥ sa dṛptaḥ balipradiṣṭaṃ śriyam ādadānaṃ traivikramaṃ pādam ivendraśatruḥ  Ragh tasyaḥ sa rakṣārtham analpayodham ādiṣya pitryaṃ sacivaṃ kumāraḥ pratyagrahīt pārthivavāhinīṃ tāṃ jyotīrathāṃ śoṇa ivottaraṅgaḥ  Ragh pattiḥ padātiṃ rathinaṃ ratheśas turaṃgasādī turagādhirūḍham yantā gajasyābhyapatad gajasthaṃ tulyapratidvandvi babhūva yuddham  Ragh nadatsu tūryeṣv avibhāvyavāco nodīrayanti sma kulopadeśān bāṇākṣarair eva parasparasya nāmorjitaṃ cāpabhṛtaḥ śaśaṃsuḥ  Ragh utthāpitaḥ saṃyati reṇur aśvaiḥ sāndrīkṛtaḥ syandanavaṃśacakraiḥ cistāritaḥ kuñjarakarṇatālair netrakrameṇoparurodha sūryam  Ragh matsyadhvajā vāyuvaśād vidīrṇair mukhaiḥ pravṛddhadvajinīrajāṃsi babhuḥ pibantaḥ paramārthamatsyāḥ paryāvilānīva navodakāni  Ragh ratho rathāṅgadhvaninā vijajñe vilolaghaṇṭākvaṇitena nāgaḥ svabhartṛnāmagrahaṇād babhūva sāndre rajasy ātmaparāvabodhaḥ  Ragh āvṛṇvato locanamārgam ājau rajondhakārasya vijṛmbhitasya śastrakṣatāśvadvipavīrajanmā bālāruṇo bhūd rudhirapravāhaḥ  Ragh sa cchinnamūlaḥ kṣatajena reṇus tasyopariṣṭāt pavanāvadhūtaḥ aṅgāraśeṣasya hutāśanasya pūrvotthito dhūma ivābabhāse  Ragh prahāramūrchāpagame rathasthān yantḥn upālabhya nivartitāśvāḥ yaiḥ sāditā lakṣitapūrvaketūṃs tān eva sāmarṣatayā nijaghnuḥ  Ragh apy ardhamārge parabāṇalūnā dhanurbhṛtāṃ hastavatāṃ pṛṣatkāḥ saṃprāpur evātmajavānuvṛttyā pūrvārdhabhāgaiḥ phalibhiḥ śaravyam  Ragh ādhoraṇānāṃ gajasaṃnipāte śirāṃsi cakrair niśitaiḥ kṣurāgraiḥ hatāny api āyenanakhāgrakoṭivyāsaktakeśāni cireṇa petuḥ  Ragh pūrvaṃ prahartā na jaghāna bhūyaḥ pratiprahārākṣamam aśvasādī turaṃgamaskandhaniṣaṇṇadehaṃ pratyāśvasantaṃ ripum ācakāṅkṣa  Ragh tanutyajāṃ varmabhṛtāṃ vikośair bṛhatsu danteṣv asibhiḥ patadbhiḥ raṇakṣitiḥ śoṇitamadyakulyā gajā vivignāḥ karaśīkareṇa  Ragh śilīmukhotkṛttaśiraḥphalāḍhyā cyutaiḥ śiratraiś caṣakottareva raṇakṣitiḥ śoṇitamadyakulyā rarāja mṛtyor iva pānabhūmiḥ  Ragh upāntayor niṣkuṣitaṃ vihaṃgair ākṣipya tebhyaḥ piśitapriyāpi keyūrakoṭikṣatatāludeśā śivā bhujacchedam apācakāra  Ragh kaścid dviṣatkhaḍgahṛtottamāṅgaḥ sadyo vimānaprabhutām upetya vāmāṅgasaṃsaktasurāṅganaḥ svaṃ nṛtyat kabandhaṃ samare dadarśa  Ragh anyonyasūtonmathanād abhūtāṃ tāv eva sūtau rathinau ca kaucit vyaśvau gadāvyāyatasaṃprahārau bagnāyudhau bāhuvimardaniṣṭhau  Ragh paraspareṇa kṣatayoḥ prahartror utkrāntavāyvoḥ samakālam eva amartyabhāve pi kayościd āsīd ekāsaraḥprārthitayor vivādaḥ  Ragh vyūhāv ubhau tāv itaretarasmād bhaṅgaṃ jayaṃ cāpatur avyavastham paścātpuromārutayoḥ pravṛddhau paryāyavṛttyeva mahārṇavormī  Ragh pareṇa bhagne pi bale mahaujā yayāv ajaḥ praty arisainyam eva dhūmo nivarteta samīraṇena yato hi kakṣas tata eva vahniḥ  Ragh rathī niṣaṅgī kavacī dhanuṣmān dṛptaḥ sa rājanyakam ekavīraḥ nivārayām āsa mahāvarāhaḥ kalpakṣayoddhūtam ivārṇavāmbhaḥ  Ragh sa dakṣiṇaṃ tūṇamukhena vāmaṃ vyāpārayan hastam alakṣyatājau ākarṇakṛṣṭā sakṛd asya yoddhur maurvīva bāṇān suṣuve riguphnān  Ragh sa roṣadaṣṭādhikalohitoṣṭhair vyaktordhvarekā bhṛkuṭīr vahadbhiḥ tastāra gāṃ bhallanikṛttakaṇṭhair huṃkāragarbhair dviṣatāṃ śirobhiḥ  Ragh sarvair balāṅgair dviradapradhānaiḥ sarvāyudhaiḥ kaṅkaṭabhedibhiś ca sarvaprayatnene ca bhūmipālās tasmin prajahrur yudhi sarva eva  Ragh so stravrajaiś channarathaḥ pareṣāṃ dhvajāgramātreṇa babhūva lakṣyaḥ nīhāramagno dinapūrvabhāgaḥ kiṃcitprakāśena vivasvateva  Ragh priyaṃvadāt prāpam asau kumāraḥ prāyuṅkta rājasv adhirājasūnuḥ gāndharvam astraṃ kusumāstrakāntaḥ prasvāpanaṃ svapanivṛttalaulyaḥ  Ragh tato dhanuṣkarṣaṇamūḍhahastam ekāṃsaparyastaśirastrajālam tasthau dhvajastambhaniṣaṇṇadehaṃ nidrāvidheyaṃ naradevasainyam  Ragh tataḥ priyopāttarase dharoṣṭhe niveśya dadhmau jalaṃ kumāraḥ yena svahastārjitam ekavīraḥ piban yaśo mūrtam ivābhāse  Ragh śaṅkhasvanābhijñatayā nivṛttās taṃ sannaśatruṃ dadṛśuḥ svayodhāḥ nimīlitānām iva paṅkajānāṃ madhye sphurantaṃ pratimāśaśāṅkam  Ragh saśoṇitais tena śilīmukhāgrair nikṣepitāḥ ketuṣu pārthivānām yaśo hṛtam saṃprati rāghaveṇa na jīvitaṃ vaḥ kṛpayeti varṇāḥ  Ragh sa cāpakoṭīnihitaikabāhuḥ śirastaniṣkarṣaṇabhinnamuliḥ lalāṭabaddhaśramavāribindur bhītāṃ priyām etya vaco babhāṣe  Ragh itaḥ parān arbhakahāryaśastrān vaidarbhi paśyānumatā mayāsi evaṃvidhenāhavaceṣṭitena tvaṃ prārthyase hastagatā mamabhiḥ  Ragh tasyāḥ pratidvandvibhavād viṣādāt sadyo vimuktaṃ mukham ābabhāse niśvāsabāṣpāpagamāt prapannaḥ prasādam ātmīyam ivātmadarṣāḥ  Ragh hṛṣṭāpi sā hrīvijitā na sākṣād vāgbhiḥ sakhīnāṃ priyam abhyanandat sthalī navāmbhaḥpṛṣatābhivṛṣṭā mayūrakekābhir ivābhravṛndam  Ragh iti śirasi sa vāmaṃ pādam ādhāya rājñām udavahad anavadyāṃ tām avadyād apetah rathaturagarajobhis tasya rūkṣālakāgrā samaravijayalaṣmīḥ saiva mūrtā babhūva  Ragh prathamaparigatārthas taṃ raghuḥ saṃnivṛttaṃ vijayinam abhinandya ślāghyajāyāsametam tadupahitakuṭumbaḥ śāntimārgotusko bhūn na hi sati kuladhurye sūryavaṃśyā gṛhāya  Ragh atha tasya vivāhakautukaṃ lalitaṃ bibhrata eva pārthivaḥ vasudhām api hastagāminīm akarod indumatīm ivāparām  Ragh duritair api kartum ātmasāt prayatante nṛpasūnavo hi yat tad upasthitam agrahīd ajaḥ pitur ājñeti na bhogatṛṣṇayā  Ragh anubhūya vasiṣṭhasaṃbhṛtaiḥ salilais tena sahābhiṣecanam viśadocchavasitena medinī kathayām āsa kṛtārthatām iva  Ragh sa babhūva durāsadaḥ parair guruṇātharvavidā kṛtakriyaḥ pavanāgnisamāgamo hy ayaṃ sahitaṃ brahma yad astratejasā  Ragh raghum eva nivṛttayauvanaṃ tam amanyanta naveśvaraṃ prajāḥ sa hi tasya na kevalāṃ śriyaṃ pratipede sakalān guṇān api  Ragh adhikaṃ śuśubhe śubhaṃyunā dvitayena dvayam eva saṃgatam padam ṛddham ajena paitṛkaṃ vinayenāsya navaṃ ca yauvanam  Ragh sadayaṃ bubhuje mahābhujaḥ sahasodvegam iyaṃ vrajed iti aciropanatāṃ sa medinīṃ navapāṇigrahaṇāṃ vadhūm iva  Ragh aham eva mato mahīpater iti sarvaḥ prakṛtiṣv acintayat udadher iva nimagāśateṣv abhavan nāsya vimānanā kvacit  Ragh na kharo na ca bhūyasā mṛduḥ pavamānaḥ pṛthivīruhān iva sa puraskṛtamadhyamakramo namayām āsa nṛpān anuddharan  Ragh atha vīksya raghuḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ prakṛtiṣv ātmajam ātmavat tayā viṣayeṣu vināśadharmasu tridivasteṣv api niḥspṛho bhavat  Ragh guṇavatsutaropitaśriyaḥ pariṇāme hi dilīpavaṃśajāḥ padavīṃ taruvalkavāsasāṃ prayatāḥ saṃyamināṃ prapedire  Ragh tam araṇyasamāśrayonmukhaṃ śirasā veṣṭanaśobhinā sutaḥ pitaraṃ praṇipatya pādayor aparityāgam ayācatātmanaḥ  Ragh raghur aśrumukhasya tasya tat kṛtavān īpsitam ātmajapriyaḥ na tu sarpa iva tvacaṃ punaḥ pratipede vyapavarjitāṃ śriyam  Ragh sa kīlaśramam antyam āśrito nivasann āvasathe purād bahiḥ samupāsyata putrabhogyayā snūṣayevāvikṛtendriyaḥ śriyā  Ragh praśamasthitapūrvapārthivaṃ kulam abhyudyata nūtaneśvaram nabhasā nibhṛtendunā tulām uditārkeṇa samāruroha tat  Ragh yatipārthivaliṅgadhāriṇau dadṛśate raghurāghavau janaiḥ apavargamahodayārthayor bhuvam aṃśāv iva dharmayor gatau  Ragh ajitādhigamāya mantribhir yuyuje nītiviśaradair ajaḥ anapāyipadopalabdhaye raghur āptaiḥ samiyāya yogibhiḥ  Ragh samayujayta bhūpatir yuvā sacivaiḥ pratyaham arthasiddhaye apunarjananopattaye prayayāḥ saṃyamibhir manīṣibhiḥ  Ragh nṛpatiḥ prakṛtīr avekṣitum vyavahārāsanam ādade yuvā paricetum upāṃśu dhāraṇāṃ kuśapūtaṃ pravayās tu viṣṭaram  Ragh anuraṇjayituṃ prajāḥ prabhur vyahārāsanam ādade navaḥ aparaḥ śuciviṣṭarasthitaḥ paricetuṃ yatate sma dhāraṇāḥ  Ragh anayat prabhuśaktisaṃpadā vaśam eko nṛpatīn anantarān aparaḥ praṇidhānayogyayā marutaḥ pañca śarīragocarān  Ragh nayacakṣur ajo didṛkṣayā pararandhrasya tatāna maṇḍale hṛdaye samaropayan manaḥ paramaṃ jyotir avekṣituṃ raghuḥ  Ragh akarod acireśvaraḥ kṣitau dviṣadārambhaphalāni bhasmasāt aparo dahane svakarmaṇāṃ vavṛte jñānamayena vahninā  Ragh paṇabandhamukhān guṇān ajaḥ ṣaḍ upāyuṅkta samīkṣya tatphalam raghur apy ajayad guṇatrayaṃ prakṛtisthaṃ samaloṣṭakāñcanaḥ  Ragh na navaḥ prabhur ā phalodayāt sthirakarmā virarāma karmaṇaḥ na ca yogavidher navetaraḥ sthiradhīr ā paramātmadarśanāt  Ragh iti śatruṣu cendriyeṣu ca pratiṣiddhaprasareṣu jāgratau prasitāv udayāpavargayor ubhayīṃ siddhim ubhāv avāpatuḥ  Ragh atha kāścid ajavyapekṣayā gamayitvā samdarśanaḥ samāḥ tamasaḥ param āpad avyayaṃ puruṣaṃ yogasamādhinā raghuḥ  Ragh śutadehavisarjanaḥ pituś ciram aśrūṇi vimucya rāghavaḥ vidadhe vidhim asya naiṣṭhikaṃ yatibhiḥ sārdham anagnim agnicit  Ragh akarot sa tadaurdhvadaihikaṃ pitṛbhaktyā pitṛkāryakalpavit na hi tena pathā tanutyajas tanayāvarjitapiṇḍakāṅkṣiṇaḥ  Ragh sa parārdhyagater aśocyatāṃ pitur uddiśya sadarthavedibhiḥ śamitādhir adhijyakārmukaḥ kṛtavān apratiśāsanaṃ jagat  Ragh kṣitir indumatī ca bhāminī patim āsādya tam agryapauruṣam prathamā bahuratnasūr abhūd aparā vīram ajījanat sutam  Ragh daśarāsmiśatopamadyutiṃ yaśasā dikṣu daśav api śrutam daśapūrvarathaṃ yam ākhyayā daśakaṇṭhāriguruṃ vidur budhāḥ  Ragh ṛṣidevagaṇasvadhābhujāṃ śrutayāgaprasvaiḥ sa pārthivaḥ anṛṇatvam upeyivān babhau paridher mukta ivoṣṇadīdhitiḥ  Ragh balam ārtabhayopaśāntaye viduṣāṃ saṃnataye bahu śrutam vasu tasya na kevalaṃ guṇavattāpi paraprayojanā  Ragh sa kadācid aveṣitaprajaḥ saha devyā vijahāra suprajāḥ nagaropavane śacīsakho marutāṃ pālayiteva nandane  Ragh atha rodhasi dakṣiṇodadheḥ śrita gokarṇaniketam īśvaram upavīṇayituṃ yayau raver udagāvṛttipathena nāradaḥ  Ragh kusumair grathitām apārthivaiḥ srajam ātodyaśironiveśitām aharat kila tasya vegavān adhivāsaspṛhayeva mārutaḥ  Ragh bhramaraiḥ kusumānusāribhiḥ parikīrṇā parivādinī muneḥ dadṛśe pavanāvalepajaṃ sṛjatī bāṣpam ivāñjanāvilam  Ragh abhibhūya vibhūtim ārtavīṃ madhugandhātiśayena vīrudhām nṛpater amarasrag āpa sā dayitorustanakoṭisusthitim  Ragh kṣaṇamātrasakhīṃ sujātayoḥ stanayos tām avalokya vihalā nimimīla narottamapriyā hṛtacandrā tamaseva kaumudī  Ragh vapuṣā karaṇojjhitena sā nipatantī patim apy apātayat nanu tailaniṣekabindunā saha dīpārcir upaiti medinīm  Ragh samam eva narādhipena sā gurusaṃmohaviluptacetanā gurusaṃmohaviluptacetanā navadīpārcir iva kṣites talam  Ragh ubhayor api pārśvavartināṃ tumu lenārtaraveṇa vejitāḥ vihagāḥ kamalākarālayāḥ samaduḥkhā iva tatra cukruśuḥ  Ragh nṛpater vyajanādibhis tamo nunude sā tu tathaiva saṃsthitā pratikāravidhānam āyuṣaḥ sati śeṣe hi phalāya kalpate  Ragh pratiyojayitavyavallakīsamavasthām atha sattvaviplavāt sa nināya nitāntavatsalaḥ parigṛhyocitam aṅkam aṅganām  Ragh sa nināya nitāntavatsalaḥ parivṛttaprathamacchaviṃ kṣaṇāt saliloddhṛtapadminīnibhāṃ dayitām aṅkam udaśulocanaḥ  Ragh sa nināya nitāntavatsalaḥ karaṇāpāyavibhinnavarṇayā samalakṣyata bibhrad āvilāṃ mṛgalekhām uṣasīva candramāḥ  Ragh vilalāpa sa bāṣpagadgadaṃ sahajām apy apahāya dhīratām abhitaptam ayo pi mārdavaṃ bhajate kaiva kathā śarīriṣu  Ragh kusumāny api gātrasaṃgamāt prabhavanty āyur apohituṃ yadi na bhaviṣyati hanta sādhanaṃ kim ivānayat prahariṣyato vidheḥ  Ragh atha vā mṛdu vastu hiṃsituṃ mṛdunaivārabhate prajāntakaḥ himasekavipattir atra me nalinī pūrvanidarśanaṃ matā  Ragh srag iyaṃ yadi jīvitāpahā hṛdaye kiṃ nihitā na hanti mām viṣam apy amṛtaṃ kvacid bhaved amṛtaṃ vā viṣam īśvarecchayā  Ragh atha vā mama bhāgyaviplavād aśaniḥ kalpita eṣa vedhasā yad anena tarur na pātitas kṣapitā tadviṭapāśritalatā  Ragh kṛtavaty asi nāvadhīraṇām aparādhhe pi yadā ciraṃ mayi katham ekapade nirāgasaṃ janam ābhāṣyam imaṃ na manyase  Ragh dhruvam asmi śaṭhaḥ śucismite vidhitaḥ kaitavavatsalas tava paralokam asaṃnivṛttaye yad anāpṛcchya gatāsi mām itaḥ  Ragh dayitāṃ yadi tāvad anvagād vinivṛttaṃ kim idaṃ tayā vinā sahatāṃ hatajīvitaṃ mama prabalām ātmakṛtena vedanām  Ragh surataśramasaṃbhṛto mukhe dhriyate svedalavodgamo pi te atha cāstamitā sy aho bata dhig imāṃ dehabhṛtām asāratām  Ragh surataśramavāribindavo na hi tāvad viramanti te mukhe katham astamitā sy aho bata dhig imām dehavatām asāratām  Ragh manasāpi na vipriyaṃ mayā kṛtapūrvaṃ tava kiṃ jahāsi mām nanu śabdapatiḥ kṣiter ahaṃ tvayi me bhāvanibandhanā ratiḥ  Ragh kusumotkacitān valīmataś calayan bhṛṅgarucas tavālakān karabhoru karoti mārutas tvadupāvartanśaṅki me manaḥ  Ragh tad apohitum arhasi priye pratibodhena viṣādam āṣu me jvalitena guhāgataṃ tamas tuhinādrer iva natam oṣadhiḥ  Ragh idam ucchvasitālakaṃ mukhaṃ viśrāntakathaṃ dunoti mām niśi suptam ivaikapaṅkajaṃ viratābhyantaraṣaṭpadasvanam  Ragh śaśinaṃ punar eti śārvarī dayitā dvandvacaraṃ patatriṇam iti tau virhāntarakṣamau katham atyantagatā na māṃ daheḥ  Ragh navapallavasaṃstare pi te mṛdu dūyeta yad aṅgam arpitam tad idaṃ viṣahiṣyate kathaṃ vada vāmoru citādhirohaṇam  Ragh iyam apratibodhaśāyinīṃ raśanā tvāṃ prathamā rahaḥsakhī gativibhramasāda nīravā na śucā nānumṛteva lakṣyte  Ragh kalam anyabhṛtāsu bhāṣitaṃ kalahaṃsīṣu gataṃ madālasaṃ pṛṭatīṣu vilolam īkṣitaṃ pavanādhūtalatāsu vibhramaḥ  Ragh tridivotsukayāpy avekṣya māṃ nihitāḥ satyam amī guṇās tvayā virahe tava me guruvyathaṃ hṛdayaṃ na tv avalambituṃ kṣamāḥ  Ragh mithunaṃ parikalpitaṃ tvayā sahakāraḥ phalinī ca nanv imau avidhāya vivāhasatkriyām anayor gamyata ivy asāṃpratam  Ragh kusumaṃ kṛtadohadas tvayā yad aśoko yam udīrayiṣyati alakābharaṇaṃ kathaṃ nu tat tava neṣyāmi nivāpalālyatām  Ragh smarateva saśabdanūpuraṃ caraṇānugraham anyadurlabham amunā kusumāśruvarṣiṇā tvam aśokena sugātri śocyase  Ragh tava niḥśvasitānukāribhir bakulair ardhacitāṃ samaṃ mayā asamāpya vilāsamekhalāṃ kim idaṃ kiṃnarakaṇṭhi supyate  Ragh samaduḥkhasukhaḥ sakhījanaḥ pratipaccandranibho yam ātmajaḥ aham ekarasas tathāpi te vyavasāyaḥ pratipattiniṣṭhuraḥ  Ragh dhṛtir astamitā ratiś cyutā virataṃ geyam ṛtur nirutsavaḥ gatam ābharaṇaprayojanaṃ pariśūnyaṃ śayanīyam adya me  Ragh gṛhiṇī sacivaḥ sakhī mithaḥ priyaśiṣyā lalite kalāvidhau karuṇāvimukhena mṛtyunā haratā tvāṃ vada kiṃ na me hṛtam  Ragh madirākṣi madānanārpitaṃ madhu pītvā rasavat kathaṃ nu me anupāsyasi bāṣpadūṣitaṃ paralokopanataṃ jalāñjalim  Ragh vibhave pi sati tvayā vinā sukham etāvad ajasya gaṇyatām ahṛtasya vilobhanāntarair mama sarve viṣayās tadāśrayāḥ  Ragh vilapann iti kosalādhipaḥ karuṇārthagrathitaṃ priyāṃ prati akarot pṛthivīruhān api srutaśākhārasabhāṣpadurdinān  Ragh atha tasya kathaṃcid aṅkataḥ svajanas tām apanīya sundarīṃ visasarja kṛtāntyamaṇḍanām analāy āgurucandanadihase  Ragh pramadām anu saṃsthitaḥ śucā nṛpatiḥ sann iti vācyadarśanāt na cakāra śarīram agnisāt saha devyā na tu jīvitāśayā  Ragh atha tena daśāhataḥ pare guṇaśeṣāṃ upadiṣya gehinīm viduṣā vidhayo maharddhayaḥ pura evopavane samāpitāḥ  Ragh sa viveśa purīṃ tayā vinā kṣaṇadāpāyaśaśāṅkadarśanaḥ parivāham ivāvalokayan svaśucaḥ pauravadhūmukhāśruṣu  Ragh atha taṃ savanāya diṣitaḥ praṇidhānād gurur āśramasthitaḥ abhiṣaṅgajaḍaṃ vijajñivān iti śiṣyeṇa kilānvabodhayat  Ragh asamāptavidhir yato munis tava vidvān api tāpakāraṇam na bhavantam upasthitaḥ svayaṃ prakṛtau sthāpayituṃ kṛtasthitiḥ  Ragh mayi tasya suvṛtta vartate laghusaṃdeśapadā sarasvatī śṛṇu viśrutasattvasāra tāṃ hṛdi cainām upadhātum arhasi  Ragh puruṣasya padeṣv ajanmanaḥ samatītaṃ ca bhavac ca bhāvi ca sa hi niṣpratighena cakṣuṣā tritayaṃ jñānamayena paśyati  Ragh carataḥ kila duścaraṃ tapas tṛṇabindoḥ pariśaṅkitaḥ purā prajighāya samādhibedinīṃ harir asmai hariṇīṃ surāṅganām  Ragh sa tapaḥpratibandhamanyunā pramukhāviṣkṛtacāruvibhramām aśapad bhava mānuṣīti tāṃ śamavelāpralayormiṇā muniḥ  Ragh bhagavan paravān ayaṃ janaḥ pratikūlācaritaṃ kṣamasva me iti copanatāṃ kṣitipṛśaṃ vivaśā śāpanivṛttikāraṇam  Ragh krathakaiśikavaṃśasaṃbhavā tava bhūtvā mahiṣī cirāya sā upalabdhavatī divaś cyutaṃ vivaśā śāpanivṛttikāraṇam  Ragh tad alaṃ tadapāyacintayā vipad utpattimatām upasthitā vasudheyam avekṣyatāṃ tvayā vasumatyā hi nṛpāḥ kalatriṇaḥ  Ragh udaye madavācyam ujjhatā śrutam āviṣkṛtam ātmavattayā manasas tad upasthite jvare punar aklībatayā prakāśyatāṃ  Ragh rudatā kuta eva sā punar bhavatā nānumṛtāpi labhyate paralokajuṣāṃ svakarmabhir gatayo bhinnapathā hi dehinām  Ragh ruditena na sā nivartate nṛpa tat tāvad anrthakaṃ tava na bhavān anusaṃsthito pi tāṃ labhate karmavaśā hi dehinaḥ  Ragh apaśokamanāḥ kuṭumbinīm anugṛhṇīṣva nivāpadattibhiḥ svajanāśru kilātrisaṃtataṃ dahati pretam iti pracakṣate  Ragh maraṇaṃ prakṛtiḥ śarīriṇāṃ vikṛtir jīvitam ucyate budhaiḥ kṣaṇam apy avatiṣṭhate śvasan yadi jantur nanu lābhavān asau  Ragh avagacchati mūḍhacetanaḥ priyanāśaṃ hṛdi śalyam arpitam sthiradhīs tu tad eva manyate kuśaladvāratayā samuddhṛtam  Ragh avagacchati mūḍhacetanaḥ śruta dhṛtasaṃyogaviparyayau yadā virahaḥ kim ivānutāpayed vada bāhyair viṣayair vipaścitam  Ragh na pṛthagjanavac chuco vaśaṃ vaśinām uttama gantum arhasi drumasānumatāṃ kim antaraṃ yadi vāyau dvitaye pi te calāḥ  Ragh sa tatheti vinetur udāramateḥ pratigṛhya vaco visasarja munim tad alabdhapadaṃ hṛdi śokaghane pratiyātam ivāntikam asya guroḥ  Ragh tenāṣṭau parigamitāḥ samāḥ kathaṃcid bālatvād avitathasūnṛtena sūnoḥ sādṛśyapratikṛtidarśanaiḥ priyāyāḥ svapneṣu kṣaṇikasamāgamtosavaiś ca  Ragh tasya prasahya hṛdayaṃ kila śokaśaṅkuḥ plakṣapraroha iva saudhatalaṃ bibheda prāṇāntahetum api taṃ bhiṣajām asādhyaṃ lābhaṃ priyānugamane tvarayā sa mene  Ragh samyagvinītam atha varmaharaṃ kumāram ādiśya rakṣaṇavidhau vidhivat prajānām rogopasṛṣṭatanudurvasatiṃ mumukṣuḥ prāyopaveśanamatir nṛpatir babhūva  Ragh tīrthe toyavyatikarabhave jahnukanyāsaryvor dehatyāgād amaragaṇanālekhyam āsādya sadyaḥ pūrvākārādhikatararucā saṃgataḥ kāntayāsau līlāgāreṣv aramata punar nandanābhyantareṣu  Ragh pitur anantaram uttarkosalān samadhigamya samādhijitendriyaḥ daśarathaḥ praśaśāsa mahāratho yamavatām avatāṃ ca dhuri sthitaḥ  Ragh adhigataṃ vidhivad yad apālayat prakṛtimaṇḍalam ātmakulocitam abhavad asya tato guṇavattaraṃ sanagaraṃ nagarandhrakaraujasaḥ  Ragh ubhayam eva vadanti manīṣiṇaḥ samayavarṣitayā kṛtakarmaṇām valaniṣūdanam arthpatiṃ ca taṃ śramanudaṃ manudaṇḍaharānvayam  Ragh janapade na gadaḥ padam ādadhāv abhibhavaḥ kuta eva sapatnajaḥ kṣitir abhūt phalavaty ajanandane śamarate maratejasi pārthive  Ragh daśadigantajitā raghuṇā yathā śriyam apuṣyad ajena tataḥ param tam adhigamya tathaiva punar babhau na na mahī nam ahīnaparākramam  Ragh samatayā vasuvṛṭivisarjanair niyamanād asatāṃ ca narādhipaḥ anuyayau yamapuṇyajaneśvarau savaruṇāv aruṇāgrasaraṃ rucā  Ragh na mṛgayābhiratir na durodaraṃ na ca śaśipratimābharaṇaṃ madhu tam udayāya na vā navayauvanā priyatamā yatamānam apāharā  Ragh na kṛpaṇā prabhavaty api vāsave na vitathā parihāsakathāsv api na ca sapatnajaneṣv api tena vāg aparuṣā paruṣākṣaram īritā  Ragh udayam astamayaṃ ca raghūdvahād ubhayam ānaśire vasudhādhipāḥ sa hi nideśam alaṅghayatām abhūt suhṛd ayohṛdayaḥ pratigarjatām  Ragh ajayad ekarathena sa medinīm udadhinemim adhijyaśarāsanaḥ jayam aghoṣayad asya tu kevalaṃ gajavatī javatīrahayā camūḥ  Ragh jaghananirviṣayīkṛtamekhalān anucitāśruviluptaviśeṣakān sa ripudāragaṇān akarod balād analakān alakādhipavikramaḥ  Ragh avanim ekarathena varūthinā jitavataḥ kila tasya dhanurbhṛtaḥ vijayadundubhitāṃ yayur arṇavā ghanaravā naravāhanasaṃpadaḥ  Ragh śamitapakṣabalaḥ śitakoṭinā śikhariṇāṃ kuliśena puraṃdaraḥ sa sāravṛṣṭimucā dhanuṣā dviṣāṃ svanavatā navatāmarasānanaḥ  Ragh sphuritakoṭisahasramarīcinā samacinot kuliśena harir yaśaḥ sa dhanuṣā yudhi sāyakavarṣiṇā svanavatā navatāmarasānanaḥ  Ragh caraṇayor nakharāgasamṛddhibhir mukuṭaratnamarīcibhir aspṛśan sa dhanuṣā yudhi sāyakavarṣiṇā śatamakhaṃ tam akhaṇḍitapauruṣam  Ragh nivavṛte sa mahārṇavarodhasaḥ sacivakāritabālasutāñjalīn samanukampya sapatnaparigrahān analakān alakānavamāṃ purīm  Ragh upagato pi ca maṇḍalanābhitām anuditānyasitātapavāraṇaḥ ajitam asti nṛpāspadam ity abhūd analaso nalasomasamadyutiḥ  Ragh kratuṣu tena visarjitamaulinā bhujasamāhṛtadigvasunā kṛtāḥ kanakayūpasamucchrayaśobhino vitamasā tamasārasyūtaṭāḥ  Ragh ajinadaṇḍabhṛtaṃ kuśamekhalāṃ yatagiraṃ mṛgaśṛṅgaparigrahām adhivasaṃs tanum adhvaradīkṣitām asambhāsam abhāsayad īśvaraḥ  Ragh avabhṛtaprayato niyatendriyaḥ surasamājasamākramaṇocitaḥ namayati sma sa kevalam unnataṃ vanamuce namucer araye śiraḥ  Ragh tam apahāya kakutsthakulodbhavaṃ puruṣam ātmabhuvaṃ ca pativratā nṛpatim anyam asevata devatā sakamalā kam alāghavam arthiṣu  Ragh sa kila saṃyugamūrdhni sahāyatāṃ maghavataḥ pratipadya mahārathaḥ svabhujavīryam agāpayad ucchritaṃ suravadhūr avadhūtabhayāḥ śaraiḥ  Ragh asakṛd ekarathena tarasvinā harihayāgrasareṇa dhanurbhṛtā dinakarābhimukhā raṇareṇavo rurudhire rudhireṇa suradviṣām  Ragh tam alabhanta patiṃ patidevatāḥ śikhariṇāṃ iva sāgaram āpagāḥ magadhakosalakekayaśasināṃ duhitaro hitaropitamārgaṇam  Ragh priyatamābhir asau tiṛbhir babhau tisṛbhir eva bhuvaṃ saha śaktibhiḥ upagato vininīṣur iva prajā harihayo rihayogavicakṣaṇaḥ  Ragh atha samāvavṛte kusumair navais tam iva sevitum ekanarādhipam yamakuberjaleśvaravajriṇāṃ samadhuraṃ madhur añcitavikramam  Ragh jigamiṣur dhanadādhyuṣitāṃ diśaṃ rathayujā parivartitavāhanaḥ dinamukhāni ravir himanirgrahair vimalayan malayaṃ nagam atyajat  Ragh himavivarṇitacandanapallavaṃ virahayan malayādrim udaṅmukhaḥ vihagayoḥ kṛpayeva śanair yayau ravir aharvirahadhruvabhedayoḥ  Ragh kusumajanma tato navapallavās tadanu ṣaṭpadakokilakūjitam iti yathākramam āvirabhūn madhur drumavatīm avatīrya vanasthalīm  Ragh surabhisaṃgamajaṃ vanamālayā navapalāśam adhāryata bhaṅguram ramaṇadattam ivārdranakhakṣataṃ pramadayā madayāpitalajjayā  Ragh upahitaṃ śiśirāpagamaśriyā mukulajālam aśobhata kiṃśuke praṇayinīva nakhakṣatamaṇḍanaṃ pramadayā madayāpitalajjayā  Ragh parabhṛtā madanakṣatacetasāṃ priyasakhī laghuvāg iva yoṣitām priyatamān akarot kalahāntare mṛduravā duravāpasamāgamān  Ragh vraṇagurupramadādharaduḥsahaṃ jaghananirviṣayīkṛtamekhalam na khalu tāvad aśeṣam apohituṃ ravir alaṃ viralaṃ kṛtavān himam  Ragh viśadacandrakaraṃ sukhamārutaṃ kusumitadrumam unmadakokilam tad upabhogarasaṃ himavarṣiṇaḥ param ṛtor viralaṃ kṛtavān himam  Ragh abhinayān paricetum ivodyatā malayamārutakampitapallavā amadayat sahakāralatā manaḥ sakalikā kalikāmajitām api  Ragh nayaguṇopacitām iva bhūpateḥ sadupakāraphalāṃ śriyam arthinaḥ abhiyayuḥ saraso madhusaṃbhṛtāṃ kamalinīm alinīrapatriṇaḥ  Ragh daśanacandrikayā vyabhāsitaṃ hasitam āsavagandhi madhor iva bakulapuṣpam asevyata ṣaṭpadaiḥ śucirasaṃ cirasaṃcitam īpsubhiḥ  Ragh kusumam eva na kevalam ārtavaṃ navam aśokataroḥ smaradīpanam kisalayaprasavo pi vilāsināṃ madayitā dayitāśravaṇārpitaḥ  Ragh viracitā madhunopavanśriyām abhinavā iva pattraviśeṣakāḥ madhulihāṃ madhudānaviśāradāḥ kurabakā ravakāraṇatāṃ yayuḥ  Ragh suvadanāvadanāsavasaṃbhṛtas tadanuvādiguṇaḥ kusumodgamaḥ madhukarair akaron madhulolupair bakulam ākulam āyatapaṅktibhiḥ  Ragh suvadanāvadanāsavasaṃbhṛtas tadanuvādiguṇaḥ kusumodgamaḥ iti dayāta ivābhavad āyatā na rajanī rajanīśavatī madhau  Ragh prathamam anyabhṛtābhir udīritāḥ praviralā iva mugdhavadhūkathāḥ surabhigandhiṣu śuśruvire giraḥ kusumitāsu mitā vanarājiṣu  Ragh śrutisukhabhramarasvanagītayaḥ kusumakomaladantaruco babhuḥ upavanāntalatāḥ pavanāhataiḥ kisalayaiḥ salayair iva pāṇibhiḥ  Ragh lalitavibhramabandhavicakṣaṇaṃ surabhigandhaparājitakesaram patiṣu nirviviśur madhum aṅganāḥ smarasakhaṃ rasakhaṇḍanavarjitam  Ragh tilakamastakaharmyakṛtāspadaiḥ kusumamadhvanuṣaṅgasugandhibhiḥ kalam agīyata bhṛṅgavilāsināṃ smarayutair ayutair abalāsakhaiḥ  Ragh śuśubhire smitacārutarānanāḥ striya iva ślathaśiñjitamekhalāḥ vikacatāmarasā gṛhadīrghikā madakalodakalolavihaṃgamāḥ  Ragh laghayati sma na patyaparādhajaṃ na sahakāratarus taruṇīdhṛtam kusumito namito libhir unmadaiḥ smarasamādhisamādhikaroṣitam  Ragh upayayau tanutāṃ madhukhaṇḍitā himakarodayapāṇḍumukhacchaviḥ sadṛśam iṣṭasamāgamanirvṛtiṃ vanitayā nitayā rajanīvadhūḥ  Ragh apatuṣāratayā viśadaprabhaiḥ suratarāga pariśramanodibhiḥ kusumacāpam atejayad aṃśubhir himakaro makarojitaketanam  Ragh hutahutāśanadīpti vanśriyaḥ pratinidhiḥ kanakābharaṇasya yat yuvatayaḥ kusumaṃ dadhur āhitaṃ tad alake dalakesarapeśalam  Ragh alibhir añjanabindumaoharaiḥ kusumapaṅktinipātibhir aṅkitaḥ na khalu śobahayit sma vanasthalīṃ na tilakas tilakaḥ pramadām iva  Ragh amadayan madghugandhasanāthayā kisalayādharasaṃgatayā manaḥ kusumasaṃbhṭtayā navamallikā smitarucā tarucāruvilāsinī  Ragh analasānyabhṛtā nalasān manaḥ kamaladhūlibhṛtā maruteritā kusumabhāranatādhvagayoṣitām asamaśokam aśokalatā karot  Ragh aruṇarāganiṣedhibhir aṃśukaiḥ śravaṇalabdhapadaiś ca yavāṅkuraiḥ parabhṛtāvirutaiś ca vilāsinaḥ smarabalair abalaikarasāḥ kṛtāḥ  Ragh upacitāvayavā śucibhiḥ kaṇair alikadambakayogam upeyuṣī sadṛśakāntir alakṣyata mañjarī tilakajā lakajālakamauktikaiḥ  Ragh dhvajapaṭaṃ madanasya dhanurbhṛtaś chavikaraṃ mukhacūrṇam ṛtuśriyaḥ kusumakesarareṇum alivrajāḥ sapavanopavanotthitam anvayuḥ  Ragh anubhavan navadolam ṛtūtsavaṃ paṭur pai priyakaṇṭhajigṛkṣayā anayad āsanarajjuparigrahe bhujalatāṃ jaḍatām abalājanaḥ  Ragh tyajata mānam alaṃ bata bigrahair na punar eti gataṃ caturaṃ vayaḥ parabhṛtābhir itīva nivedite smaramate ramate sma vadhūjanaḥ  Ragh atha yathāsukham ārtavam utsavaṃ samanubhūya vilāsavatīsakhaḥ narapatiś cakame mṛgayāratiṃ sa madhumanmadhumanmathasaṃnibhaḥ  Ragh paricayaṃ calakṣyanipātane bhayaruṣoś ca tadiṅgitabodhanam śramajayāt praguṇāṃ ca karoty asau tanum ato numataḥ sacivair yayau  Ragh mṛgavanopagamakṣamaveṣabhṛd vipulakaṇṭhaniṣaktaśarāsanaḥ gaganam aśvakhuroddhuta reṇubhir nṛsavitā savitānam ivākarot  Ragh grathitamaulir asau vanamālayā taru palāśasavarṇatanucchadaḥ turagavalganacaṇcalakuṇḍalo viruruce ruruceṣṭitabhūmiṣu  Ragh tanulatāviniveśitavigrahā bhramarasaṃkramitekṣaṇavṛttayaḥ dadṛṣur adhvani taṃ vanadevatāḥ sunayanaṃ nayananditakosalam  Ragh śvagaṇvāgurikaiḥ prathamāsthitaṃ vyapagatānaladasyu viveśa saḥ sthiraturaṃgamabhūmi nipānavan mṛgavayogavayopacitaṃ vanam  Ragh atha nabhasya iva tridaśāyudhaṃ kanakapiṅgataḍidguṇasaṃyutam dhanur radhijyam anādhir upādade naravaro ravaroṣitakesarī  Ragh tasya stanapraṇayibhir muhur eṇaśāvair vyāhanyamānahariṇīgamanaṃ purastāt āvirbabhūva kuśagarbhamukhaṃ mṛgāṇāṃ yūthaṃ tadagrasaragarvitakṛṣnasāram  Ragh tat prārthitaṃ javanvājigatena rājñā tūṇīmukhoddhṛtaśareṇa viśīrṇapaṅkti śyāmīcakāra vanam ākuladṛśṭipātair vateritotpaladalaprakarair ivāmbhaḥ  Ragh lakṣyīkṛtasya hariṇasya hariprabhāvaḥ prekṣya sthitāṃ sahacarīṃ vyavadhāya deham ākarṇakṛṣṭam api kāmitayā sa dhanvī bāṇaṃ kṛpāmṛdhumanāḥ pratisaṃjahāra  Ragh tasyāpareṣv api mṛgeṣu śarān mumukṣoḥ karṇāntam etya bibhide nibiḍo pi muṣṭiḥ trāsātimātracaṭulaiḥ smarayatsu netraiḥ prauḍhapriyānayanavibhramaceṣṭitāni  Ragh uttasthuṣaḥ śiśirapalvalapaṅkamadhyān mustāprarohakavalāvayavānukīrṇam jagrāha sa drutavarāhakulasya mārgaṃ suvyaktam ārdrapadapaṅktibhir āyatābhiḥ  Ragh taṃ vāhanād avanatottarakāyam īṣad vidhyantam uddhatasaṭāḥ pratihantum īṣuḥ nātmānam asya vividuḥ sahasā varāhā vṛkeṣu viddham iṣubhir jaghanāśrayeṣu  Ragh tenābhighātarabhasasya vikṛṣya pattrī vanyasya netravivare mahiṣasya muktaḥ nirbhidya vigraham aśoṇitaliptapuṅkhas taṃ pātayāṃ prathamam āsa papāta paścāt  Ragh prāyo viṣāṇaparimoṣalaghūttamāṅgān khaḍgāṃś cakāra nṛpatir niśitaiḥ kṣurapraiḥ śṛṇgaṃ sa dṛptavinayādhikṛtaḥ pareṣām abhyucchritaṃ na mamṛṣe na tu dīrgham āyuḥ  Ragh vyāghrān abhīr abhimukhopatitān guhābhyaḥ phullāsanāgraviṭapān iva vāyurugṇān śikṣāviśeṣalaghuhastatayā nimeṣāt tūṇīcakāra śarapūritavaktrarandhrān  Ragh nirghātograiḥ kuñjalīnāñ jighāṃsur jyānirghoṣaiḥ kṣobhayām āsa siṃhān nūnaṃ teṣām abhyasūyāparo bhūd vīryodagre rājaśabde mṛgeṣu  Ragh tān hatvā gajakulabaddhatīvravairān kākutsthaḥ kuṭilanakhāgralagnamuktān ātmānaṃ raṇakṛtakarmaṇāṃ gajānām ānṛṇyaṃ gatam iva mārgaṇair amaṃsta  Ragh tān hatvā gajakulabaddhatīvravairān kākutsthaḥ kuṭilanakhāgralagnamuktān ātmānaṃ raṇakṛtakarmaṇāṃ gajānām ānṛṇyaṃ gatam iva mārgaṇair amaṃsta  Ragh camarān paritaḥ pravartitāśvaḥ kvacid ākarṇavikṛṣṭabhallavarṣī nṛpatīn iva tān viyojya sadyaḥ sitavālavyajanair jagāma śāntim  Ragh api turagasamīpād utpatantaṃ mayūraṃ na sa rucirakalāpaṃ bāṇalakṣyī cakāra sapadi gatamanaskaś citramālyānukīrṇe rativigalitabandhe keśapāśe priyāyāḥ  Ragh tasya karkaśavihārsaṃbhavaṃ svedam ānanavilagnajālakam ācacāma satuṣāraśīkaro bhinnapallavapuṭo vanānilaḥ  Ragh iti vismṛtānyakaraṇīyam ātmanaḥ sacivāvalambitadhuraṃ narādhipam parivṛddharāgam anubhandhasevayā mṛgayā jahāra catureva kāminī  Ragh sa lalitakusumapravālaśayyāṃ jvalitamahauṣadhidīpikāsanāthām narapatir ativāhayāṃ babhūva kvacid asametaparicchadas triyāmām  Ragh uṣasi sa gajayūthakarṇatālaiḥ paṭupaṭadhavanibhir vinītanidraḥ aramata madhurāṇi tatra śṛṇvan vihagavikūjitabandimaṅgalāni  Ragh atha jātu ruror gṛhītavartmā vipine pārśvacarair alakṣyamāṇaḥ śramaphenamucā tapasvigāḍhāṃ tamasāṃ prāpa nadīṃ turaṃgameṇa  Ragh kumbhapūraṇabhavaḥ paṭur uccair uccacāra nando mbhasi tasyāḥ tatra sa dviradabṛṃhitaśaṅkī śabdapātinam iṣuṃ visasarja  Ragh nṛpateḥ pratiṣiddham eva tat kṛtavān paṅktiratho vilaṅghya yat apathe padam arpayanti hi śrutavanto pi rajonimīlitāḥ  Ragh hā tāteti kranditam ākarṇya viṣaṇṇas tasyānviṣyan vetasagūḍhaṃ prabhavaṃ saḥ śalyaprotaṃ prekṣya sakumbhaṃ muniputraṃ tāpād antaḥśalya ivāsīt kśitipo pi  Ragh tenāvatīrya turagāt prathitāngvayena pṛṣṭānvayaḥ sa jalakumbhaniṣaṇṇadehaḥ tasmai dvijetaratapasvisutaṃ skhaladbhir ātmānam akṣarapadaiḥ kathayāṃ babhūva  Ragh taccoditaḥ ca tam anuddhrṛtaśalyam eva pitroḥ sakāśam avasannadṛśor nināya tābhyāṃ tathāgatam upetya tam ekaputram ajñānataḥ svacaritaṃ nṛpatiḥ śaśaṃsa  Ragh tau daṃpatī bahu vilapya śiśoḥ prahartrā śalyaṃ nikhātam udahārayatām urastaḥ so bhūt parāsur atha bhūmipatiṃ śaśāpa hastārpitair nayanvāribhir eva vṛddhaḥ  Ragh diṣṭāntam āpsyati bhavān api putraśokād ante vayasy
