aham iveti tam uktavantam ākrāntapūrvam iva muktaviṣaṃ bhujaṃgaṃ provāca kosalapatiḥ prathamāparāddhaḥ  Ragh śāpo py adṛṣṭatanayānanapadmaśobhe sānugraho bhagavatā mayi pātito yam kṛṣyāṃ dahann api khalu kṣitim indhaneddho bījaprarohajananīṃ jvalanaḥ karoti  Ragh itthaṃ gate gataghṛṇaḥ kim ayaṃ vidhattāṃ vadhyas tavety abhitite vasudhādhipena edhān hutāśanavataḥ sa munir yayāce putraṃ parāsum anugantumanāḥ sadāraḥ  Ragh prātānugaḥ sapadi śāsanam asya rājā saṃpādya pātakaviluptadhṛtir nivṛttaḥ antarniviṣṭapadam ātmavināśahetuṃ śāpaṃ dadhaj jvalanam aurvam ivāmburāśiḥ  Ragh tadartham arthajñagate gatatrapaḥ kim eṣa te vadhyajano nusiṣṭhatu sa vahnisaṃskāram ayācatātmanaḥ sadārasūnor vidadhe ca tan nṛpaḥ  RaghA sameyivān raghuvṛṣabhaḥ svasainikaiḥ svamandiraṃ śithiladhṛtir nivartitaḥ manogataṃ guruṃ ṛṣiśāpam udvahan kṣayānalaṃ jaladhir ivāntakāspadam  RaghB pṛthivīṃ śāsatas tasya pākaśāsanatejasaḥ kiṃcidūnam anūnarddheḥ śaradām ayutaṃ yayau  Ragh na copalebhe pūrveṣām ṛṇanirmokṣasādhanam sutābhidhānaṃ sa jyotiḥ śaradām ayutaṃ yayau  Ragh manor vaṃśaś ciraṃ tasminn anabhivyaktasaṃtatiḥ nimajjya punar utthāsyan nadaḥ śoṇa ivābhavat  Ragh atiṣṭhat pratyayāpekṣasaṃtatiḥ sa ciraṃ nṛpaḥ prāṅ manthād anabhivyaktaratnotpattir ivārṇavaḥ  Ragh ṛṣyaśṛṅgādayas tasya santaḥ saṃtānakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ārebhire jitātmānaḥ putrīyām iṣṭim ṛtvijaḥ  Ragh tasminn avasare devāḥ paulastyopaplutā harim abhijagmur nidāghārtāś chāyāvṛkṣam ivādhvagāḥ  Ragh te ca prāpur udanvataṃ bubudhe cādipūruṣaḥ avyākṣepo bhaviṣyantyāḥ kāryasiddher hi lakṣaṇam  Ragh bhogibhogādanāsīnaṃ dadṛśus taṃ divaukasaḥ tatphaṇāmaṇḍalodarcirmaṇidyotitavigraham  Ragh śriyaḥ padmaniṣaṇṇāyāḥ kṣaumāntaritamekhale aṅke nikṣiptacaraṇam āstīrṇakarapallave  Ragh prabuddhapuṇḍarīkākṣaṃ bālātapanibhāṃśukam divasaṃ śāradam iva prārambhasukhadarśanam  Ragh prabhānuliptaśrīvatsaṃ lakṣmīvibhramadarpaṇam kautsubhākhyam apāṃ sāraṃ bibhrāṇaṃ bṛhatorasā  Ragh bāhubhir viṭapākārair divyābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ āvirbhūtam apāṃ madhye pārijātam ivāparam  Ragh daityastrīgaṇḍalekhānāṃ madarāgavilopibhiḥ hetibhiś cetanāvadbhir udīritajayasvanam  Ragh muktaśeṣavirodhena kuliśavraṇalakṣmaṇā upasthitaṃ prāñjalinā vinītena garutmatā  Ragh yoganidrāntaviśadaiḥ pāvanair avalokanaiḥ bhṛgvādīn anugṛhṇantaṃ saukha śāyanikān ṛṣīn  Ragh praṇipatya surās tasmai śamayitre suradviṣām athainaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ stutyam avāṅmanasagocaram  Ragh namo viśvasṛje pūrvaṃ viśvaṃ tadanu bibhrate atha viśvasya saṃhartre tubhyaṃ tredhāsthitātmane  Ragh rasāntarāṇy ekarasaṃ yathā divyaṃ payo śnute deśe deśe guṇeṣv evam avasthās tvam avikriyaḥ  Ragh ameyo mitalokas tvam anarthī prārthanāvahaḥ ajito jiṣṇur atyantam avyakto vyaktakāraṇam  Ragh ekaḥ kāraṇatas tāṃ tām avasthāṃ pratipadyase nānātvaṃ rāgasaṃyogāt sphaṭikasyeva te smṛtam  Ragh hṛdayastham anāsannam akāmaṃ tvāṃ tapasvinam dayālum anaghaspṛṣṭaṃ purāṇam ajaraṃ viduḥ  Ragh sarvajñas tvam avijñātaḥ sarvayonis tvam ātmabhūḥ sarvaprabhur anīśas tvam ekas tvaṃ sarvarūpabhāk  Ragh saptasāmopagītaṃ tvāṃ saptārṇavajaleśayam saptārcirmukham ācakhyuḥ saptalokaikasaṃśrayam  Ragh caturvargaphalaṃ jñānaṃ kālāvasthā caturyugā caturvarṇamayo lokas tvattaḥ sarvaṃ caturmukhāt  Ragh abhyāsanigṛhītena manasā hṛdayāśrayam jyotirmayaṃ vicinvanti yoginas tvāṃ vimuktaye  Ragh ajasya gṛhṇato janma nirīhasya hatadviṣaḥ svapato jāgarūkasya yāthātmyaṃ veda kas tava  Ragh śabdādīn viṣayān bhoktuṃ carituṃ duścaraṃ tapaḥ paryāpto si prajāḥ pātum audāsīnyena vartitum  Ragh bahudhāpy āgamair bhinnāḥ panthānaḥ siddhihetavaḥ tvayy eva nipatanty oghā jāhnavīyā ivārṇave  Ragh tvayy āveśitacittānāṃ tvatsamarpitakarmaṇām gatis tvaṃ vītarāgāṇām abhūyaḥsaṃnivṛttaye  Ragh pratyakṣo py aparicchedyo mahyādir mahimā tava āptavāganumānābhyāṃ sādhyaṃ tvāṃ prati kā kathā  Ragh kevalaṃ smaraṇenaiva punāsi puruṣaṃ yataḥ anena vṛttayaḥ śeṣā niveditaphalās tvayi  Ragh udadher iva ratnāni tejāṃsīva vivasvataḥ stutibhyo vyatiricyante dūreṇa caritāni te  Ragh anavāptam avāptavyaṃ na te kiṃcana vidyate lokānugraha evaiko hetus te janmakaramaṇoḥ  Ragh mahimānaṃ yad utkīrtya tava saṃhriyate vacaḥ śrameṇa tad aśaktyā vā na guṇānām iyattayā  Ragh iti prasādayām āsus tava saṃhriyate vacaḥ bhūtārthavyāhṛtiḥ sā hi na stutiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  Ragh tasmai kuśalasaṃpraśnavyañjitaprītaye surāḥ bhayam apralayodvelād ācakhyur nairṛtodadheḥ  Ragh atha velāsamāsannaśailarandhrānunādinā svareṇovāca bhagavān paribhūtārṇavadhvaniḥ  Ragh purāṇasya kaves tasya varṇasthānasamīritā babhūva kṛtasaṃskārā caritārthaiva bhāratī  Ragh babhau sa daśanajyotsnā sā vibhor vadanodgatā niryātaśeṣā caraṇād gaṅgevordhvapravartinī  Ragh jāne vo rakṣasākrāntāv anubhāvaparākramau aṅgināṃ tamasevobhau guṇau prathmamadhyamau  Ragh viditaṃ tapyamānaṃ ca tena me bhuvantrayam akāmopanateneva sādhor hṛdayam enasā  Ragh kāryeṣu caikakāryatvād abhyarthyo smi na vajriṇā svayam eva hi vāto gneḥ sārathyaṃ pratipadyate  Ragh svāsidhārāparihṛtaḥ kāmaṃ cakrasya tena me sthāpito daśamo mūrdhā lavyāṃśa iva rakṣasā  Ragh sraṣṭur varātisargāt tu mayā tasya durātmanaḥ atyārūḍhaṃ ripoḥ soḍhaṃ candaneva bhoginaḥ  Ragh dhātāraṃ tapasā prītaṃ yayāce sa hi rākṣasaḥ daivāt sargād avadhyatvaṃ martyeṣv āsthāparāṅmukhaḥ  Ragh so haṃ dāśarathir bhūtvā raṇabhūmer balikṣamam kariṣyāmi śarais tīkṣṇais tacchiraḥkamaloccayam  Ragh acirād vajvabhir bhāgaṃ kalpitaṃ vidhivat punaḥ māyāvibhir anālīḍham ādāsyadhve miśācaraiḥ  Ragh vaimānikāḥ puṇyakṛtas tyajantu marutāṃ pathi puṣpakālokasaṃkṣobhaṃ meghāvaraṇatatparāḥ  Ragh moṣyadhve svargabandīnāṃ veṇībandhān adūṣitān śāpayantritapaulastyabalātkārakacagrahaiḥ  Ragh rāvaṇāvagrahaklāntam iti vāgamṛtena saḥ abhivṛṣya marutsasyaṃ kṛṣṇameghas tirodadhe  Ragh puruhūtaprabhṛtayaḥ surakāryodyataṃ surāḥ aṃśair anuyayur viṣṇuṃ puṣpair vāyum iva drumāḥ  Ragh atha tasya viśāṃpatyur ante kāmyasya karmaṇaḥ puruṣaḥ prababhūvāgner vismayena sahartvijām  Ragh hemapātragataṃ dorbhyām ādadhānaḥ payaścarum anupraveśād ādyasya puṃsas tenāpi durvaham  Ragh prājāpatyopanītaṃ tad annaṃ pratyagrahīn nṛpaḥ vṛṣeva payasāṃ sāram āviṣkṛtam udanvatā  Ragh anena kathitā rājño guṇās tasyānyadurlabhāḥ prasūtiṃ cakame tasmiṃs trailokyaprabhavo pi yat  Ragh sa tejo vaiśnavaṃ patnyor vibheje carusaṃjñitam dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ pratyagram aharpatir ivātapam  Ragh arcitā tasya kausalyā priyā kekayavaṃśajā ataḥ saṃbhāvitāṃ tābhyāṃ sumitrām aicchad īśvaraḥ  Ragh te bahujñasya cittajñe patnyau patyur mahīṣitaḥ caror ardhārdhabhāgābhyāṃ tām ayojayatām ubhe  Ragh sāpi praṇayavaty āsīt sapatnyor ubhayor api bhramarī vāraṇasyeva madanisyandalekhayoḥ  Ragh tābhir garbhaḥ prajābhūtyai dadhre devāṃśasambhavaḥ saurībhir iva nāḍībhir amṛtākhyābhir ammayaḥ  Ragh samam āpannasattvās tā rejur āpāṇḍuratviṣaḥ antargataphalārambhāḥ sasyānām iva saṃpadaḥ  Ragh guptaṃ dadṛśur ātmānaṃ sarvāḥ svapneṣu vāmanaiḥ jalajāsigadāśārṅgacakralāñchitamūrtibhiḥ  Ragh hemapakṣaprabhājālaṃ gagane ca vitanvatā uhyante sma suparṇena vegākṛṣṭapayomucā  Ragh bibhratyā kaustubhaṃ nyāsaṃ stanāntaravilambinam paryupāsyanta lakṣmyā ca padmavyajanahastayā  Ragh kṛtābhiṣekair divyāyāṃ trisrotasi ca saptabhiḥ brahma rṣibhiḥ paraṃ brahma gṛṇadhbir upatasthire  Ragh tābhyas tathāvidhān svapnāñ chrutvā prīto hi pārthivaḥ mene parārdhyam ātmānaṃ gurutvena jagdguroḥ  Ragh vibhaktātmā vibhus tāsām ekaḥ kuṣiṣv anekadhā uvāsa pratimācandraḥ prasannānām apām iva  Ragh athāgramahiṣī rājñaḥ prasūtisamaye satī putraṃ tamopahaṃ lebhe naktaṃ jyotir ivauṣadhiḥ  Ragh rāma ity abhirāmeṇa tenāpratima tejasā nāmadheyaṃ guruś cakre jagatprathamamaṅgalam  Ragh raghuvaṃśapradīpena tenāpratima tejasā rakṣāgṛhagatā dīpāḥ pratyādiṣṭa ivābhavan  Ragh śayyāgatena rāmeṇa mātā śātodarī babhau saikatāmbhojabalinā jāhnavīva śaratkṛśā  Ragh kaikeyyās tanayo jajñe bharato nāma śīlavān janayitrīm alaṃcakre yaḥ praśraya iva śriyam  Ragh sutau lakṣmaṇaśatrughnau sumitrā suṣuve yamau samyagāgamitā vidyā prabodhavinayāv iva  Ragh nirdoṣam abhavat sarvam āviṣkṛtaguṇaṃ jagat anvagād iva hi svargo gāṃ gataṃ puruṣottamam  Ragh tasyodaye caturmūrteḥ paulastyacakiteśvarāḥ virajaskair nabhasvadbhir diśa ucchvasitā iva  Ragh kṛśānur apadhūmatvāt prasannatvāt prabhākaraḥ rakṣiviprakṛtāv āstām apaviddhaśucāv iva  Ragh daśānanakirīṭebhyas tatkṣaṇaṃ rākṣasaśriyaḥ maṇivyājena paryastāḥ pṛthivyām aśrubindavaḥ  Ragh putrajanmapraveśyānāṃ tūryāṇām tasya putriṇaḥ ārambhaṃ prathamaṃ cakrur devadhundubhayo divi  Ragh saṃtānakamayī vṛṣṭir bhavane cāsya petuṣī samaṅgalopacārāṇāṃ saivādiracanābhavat  Ragh kumārāḥ kṛtasaṃskārās te dhātristanya pāyinaḥ ānandenāgrajeneva samaṃ vavṛdhire pituḥ  Ragh svābhāvikaṃ vinītatvaṃ teṣaṃ vinayakarmaṇā mumūrcha sahajaṃ tejo haviṣeva havirbhujām  Ragh parasparāviruddhās te tad raghor anaghaṃ kulam alam uddyotayām āsur devāraṇyam ivartavaḥ  Ragh samāne pi hi saubhrātre yathobhau rāmalakṣmaṇau tathā bharataśatrughnau prītyā dvandvaṃ babhūvatuḥ  Ragh teṣāṃ dvayor dvayor aikyaṃ bibhide na kadācana yathā vāyuvibhāvasvor yathā candrasamudrayoḥ  Ragh te prajānāṃ prajānāthās tejasā praśrayeṇa ca mano jahrur nidāghānte śyāmābhrā divasā iva  Ragh sa caturdhā babhau vyastaḥ prasavaḥ pṛthivīpateḥ dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇām avatāra ivāṅgabhāk  Ragh guṇair ārādhayām āsus te guruṃ guruvatsalāḥ tam eva caturnateśaṃ ratnair iva mahārṇavāḥ  Ragh suragaja iva dantair bhagnadaityāsidhārair naya iva paṇabandhavyaktayogair upāyaiḥ harir iva yugadīrghair dorbhir aṃṣais tadīyaiḥ patir avanipatīnāṃ taiś cakāśe  Ragh kauśikena sa kila kṣitīśvaro rāmam adhvaravighātaśāntaye kākapakṣadharam etya yācitas tejasāṃ hi na vayaḥ samīkṣyate  Ragh kṛcchralabdham api labdhavarṇabhāk taṃ dideśa munaye salakṣmaṇam apy asupraṇayināṃ raghoḥ kule na vyahanyata kadācid arthitā  Ragh yāvad ādiśati pārthivas tayor nirgamāya puramārgasatkriyām tāvad āśu vidadhe marutsakhaiḥ sā sapuṣpajalavarṣibhir ghanaiḥ  Ragh tau nideśakaraṇodyatau pitur dhanvinau caraṇayor nipetatuḥ bhūpater api tayoḥ pravatsyator namrayor upari bāṣpabindavaḥ  Ragh tau pitur nayanajena vāriṇā kiṃcidukṣitaśikhaṇḍakāv ubhau dhanvinau tam ṛṣim anvagacchatāṃ pauradṛṣṭikṛtamārgatoraṇau  Ragh lakṣmaṇānucaram eva rāghavaṃ netum aicchad ṛṣir ity asau nṛpaḥ āśiṣaṃ prayuyuje na vāhinīṃ sā hi rakṣaṇavidhau tayoḥ kṣamā  Ragh rejatuś ca sutarāṃ mahaujasaḥ kauśikasya padavīm anudrutau uttarāṃ prati diśaṃ vivasvataḥ prasthitasya madhumādhavāv iva  Ragh mātṛvargacaraṇaspṛṣau munes tau prapadya padavīṃ mahaujasaḥ rejatur gativaśāt pravartinau bhāskarasya madhumādhavāv iva  Ragh vīcilolabhujayos tayor gataṃ śaiśavāc capalam apy aśobhata toyadāgama ivoddhyabhidyayor nāmadheyasadṛśaṃ viceṣṭitam  Ragh tau balātibalayoḥ prabhāvato vidyayoḥ pathi munipradiṣṭayoḥ mamlatur na maṇikuṭṭimocitau mātṛpārśvaparivartināv iva  Ragh pūrvavṛttakathitaiḥ purāvidaḥ sānujaḥ pitṛsakhasya rāghavaḥ uhyamāna iva vāhanocitaḥ pādacāram api na vyabhāvayat  Ragh tau sarāṃsi rasavadbhir ambubhiḥ kūjitaiḥ śrutisukhaiḥ patatriṇaḥ vāyavaḥ surabhipuṣpareṇubhiś chāyayā ca jaladāḥ siṣevire  Ragh nāmbhasāṃ kamalaśobhināṃ tathā śākhināṃ na ca pariśramacchidām darśanena laghunā yathā tayoḥ prītim āpur ubhayos tapasvinaḥ  Ragh sthāṇudagdhavapuṣas tapovanaṃ prāpya dāśarathir āttakārmukaḥ vigraheṇa madanasya cāruṇā so bhavat pratinidhir na karmaṇā  Ragh tau suketusutayā khilīkṛte kauśikād viditaśāpayā pathi ninyatuḥ sthalaniveśitātaṭanī līlayaiva dhanuṣī adhijyatām  Ragh jyāniniādam atha gṛhṇatī tayoḥ prādurāsa bahūlakṣapā chaviḥ tāḍakā calakapālakuṇḍalā kālikeva nibiḍā balākinī  Ragh tīvravegadhutamārgavṛkṣayā pretacīvaravasā svanograyā abhyabhāvi bharatāgrajas tayā vātyayeva pitṛkānanotthayā  Ragh udyataikabhujayaṣṭim āyatīṃ śroṇilambipuruṣāntramekhalām tāṃ vilokya vanitāvadhe ghṛṇāṃ pattriṇā saha mumoca rāghavaḥ  Ragh yac cakāra vivaraṃ śilāghane tāḍakorasi sa rāmasāyakaḥ apraviṣṭaviṣayasya rakṣasāṃ dvāratām agamad antakasya tat  Ragh bāṇabhinnahṛdayā nipetuṣī sā svakānabhuvaṃ na kevalām viṣṭapatrayaparājayasthirāṃ rāvaṇaśriyam api vyakampayat  Ragh rāmamanmathaśareṇa tāḍitā duḥsahena dṛdaye niśācarī gandhavadrudhiracandanokṣitā jīviteśavasatiṃ jagāma sā  Ragh nairṛtaghnam atha mantravan muneḥ prāpad astram avadānatoṣitāt jyotir indhanaipāti bhāskarāt sūryakānta iva tāḍakāntakaḥ  Ragh vāmanāśramapadaṃ tataḥ paraṃ pāvanaṃ śruam ṛṣer upeyivān unmanāḥ prathamajanmaceṣṭitāny asmarann api babhūva rāghavaḥ  Ragh āsasāda munir ātmanas tataḥ śiṣyavargaparikalpitārhaṇam baddhapallavapuṭāñjalidrumaṃ darśanonmukha mṛgaṃ tapovanam  Ragh tatra dīkṣitam ṛṣiṃ rakaṣatur vighnato daśarathātmajau śaraiḥ lokam andhatamasāt kramoditau raśāmibhiḥ śaśidivākarāv iva  Ragh vīkṣya vedim atha raktabindubhir bandhujīvapṛthubhiḥ pradūṣitām saṃbhramo bhavad apoḍhakarmaṇām ṛtvijāṃ cyutavikaṅkatasrucām  Ragh unmukhaḥ sapadi lakṣmaṇāgrajo bāṇam āśrayamukhāt samuddharan rakṣasāṃ balam apaśyad ambare gṛdhrapakṣapavaneritadhvajam  Ragh tatra yāv adhipatī makhadviṣāṃ tau śaravyam akarot sa netarān kiṃ mahoragavisarpivikramo rājileṣu garuḍaḥ pravartate  Ragh so stram ugrajavam astrakovidaḥ saṃdadhe dhanuṣi vāyudaivatam tena śailagurum apy apātayat pāṇḍupattram iva tāḍakāsutam  Ragh yaḥ subāhur iti rākṣaso paras tatra tatra visasarpa māyayā taṃ kṣurapraśakalīkṛtām kṛtī pattriṇāṃ vyabhajad āśramād bahiḥ  Ragh ity apāstamakhavighnayos tayoḥ sāṃyugīnam abhinandya vikramam ṛtvijaḥ kulapater yathākramaṃ vāgyatasya niravartayan kriyāḥ  Ragh tau praṇāmacalakākapakṣakau bhrātarāv abhṛthāpluto muniḥ āśiṣām anupadaṃ samaspṛśad darbhapāṭitatalena pāṇinā  Ragh taṃ nyamantrayata saṃbhṛtakratur maithilaḥ sa mighilāṃ vrajan vaśī rāghavāv api nināya bibhratau taddhanuḥśravaṇajaṃ kutūhalam  Ragh taiḥ śiveṣu vasatir gatādhvabhiḥ sāyam āśramataruṣv agṛhyata yeṣu dīrghatapasaḥ parigraho vāsavakṣaṇakalatratāṃ yayau  Ragh pratyapadyata cirāya yat punaś cāru gautamavadhūḥ śilāmayī svaṃ vapuḥ sa kila kilibiṣacchidāṃ rāmapādarajasām anugrahaḥ  Ragh rāghavānvitam upasthitaṃ muniṃ taṃ niśamya janako janeśvaraḥ arthakāmasahitaṃ saparyayā dehabaddham iva dharmam abhyagāt  Ragh tau videhanagarīnivāsināṃ gāṃ gatāv iva divaḥ punarvasū manyate sma pibatāṃ vilocanaiḥ pakṣmapātam api vañcanāṃ manaḥ  Ragh yūpavaty avasite kiryāvidhau kālavit kuśikavaṃśavardhanaḥ rāmam iṣvasanadarśanotsukaṃ maithilāya kathayāṃ bvabhūva saḥ  Ragh tasya vīkṣya lalitaṃ vapuḥ śiśoḥ pārthivaḥ prathitavaṃśajanmanaḥ svaṃ vicintya ca dhanur durānamaṃ pīḍito duhiṭśulkasaṃsthayā  Ragh abravīc ca bhagavan mataṅgajair yad bṛhadbhir api karma duṣkaram tatra nāham anumantum utsahe moghavṛtti kalabhasya ceṣṭitam  Ragh hrepitā hi bahavo nareśvarās tena tāta dhanuṣā dhanurbhṛtaḥ jyānighātakaṭhinatvaco bhujān svān vidhūya dhig iti pratasthire  Ragh pratyuvāca tam ṛṣir niśamyatāṃ sārato yam atha vā kṛtaṃ girā cāpa eva bhavato bhaviṣyati vyaktaśaktir aśanir girāv iva  Ragh evam āptavacanāt sa pauruṣaṃ kākapakṣakadhare pi rāghave śraddadhe tridaśagopamātrake dāhaśaktim iva kṛṣṇavartmani  Ragh vyādideśa gaṇaḥ sapārśvagān karmukābharaṇāya maithilaḥ taijasaya dhanuṣaḥ pravṛttaye toyadān iva sahasralocanaḥ  Ragh tat prasuptabhujagendrabhīṣaṇaṃ vīkṣya dāśarathir ādade dhanuḥ vidrutakratumṛgānausāriṇaṃ yena bāṇam asṛjad vṛṣadhvajaḥ  Ragh ātatajyam akarot sa saṃsadā vismayastimitanetram īkṣitaḥ śailasāram api nātiyatnataḥ puṣpacāpam iva peśalaṃ smaraḥ  Ragh bhajyamānam atimātrakarṣaṇāt tena vajraparuṣasvanaṃ dhanuḥ bhārgavāya dṛḍhamanyave punaḥ kṣatram udyatam iti nyavedayat  Ragh dṛṣṭasāram atha rudrakārmuke vīryaśulkam abhinandya maithilaḥ rāghavāya tanayām ayonijāṃ rūpiṇīṃ śriyam iva nyavedayat  Ragh maithilaḥ sapadi satyasaṃgaro rāghavāya tanayām ayonijāṃ saṃnidhau dyutimatas taponidher agnisākṣika ivātisṛṣṭavān  Ragh prāhiṇoc ca mahitaṃ mahādyutiḥ kosalādhipataye purodhasam bhṛtyabhāvi duhituḥ parigrahād diśyatāṃ kulam idaṃ nimer iti  Ragh utsukaś ca sutadārakarmaṇā so bhavad gurur upāgataś ca tam gautamasya tanayo nukūlavāk prārthitaṃ hi sukṛtām akālahṛt  Ragh anviyeṣa sadṛśīṃ sa ca snuṣāṃ prāpa cainam anukūlavāg dvijaḥ sadya eva sukṛtāṃ hi pacyate kalpavṛkṣaphala dharmi kāṅkṣitam  Ragh tasya kalpitapuraskriyāvidheḥ śuśruvān vacanam agrajanmanaḥ uccacāla valabhitasakho vaśī sainyareṇumuṣitārkadīdhitiḥ  Ragh āsasāda mithilāṃ sa veṣṭayan piḍitopavanapādapāṃ balaiḥ prītirodham asahiṣṭa sā purī strīva kāntaparibhogam āyatam  Ragh tau sametya samayasthitāv ubhau bhūpatī varuṇavāsavopamau kanyakātanayakautukakriyāṃ svaprabhāvasadṛśīṃ vitenatuḥ  Ragh pārthivīm udavahad raghūdvaho lakṣmaṇas tadanujām athormilām yau tayor avarajau varaujasau tau kuśadhvajasute sumadhyame  Ragh te caturthasahitās trayo babhuḥ sūnavo navavadhūparigrahāḥ sāmadānavidhibhedavigrahāḥ siddhimanta iva tasya bhūpateḥ  Ragh tā narādhipasutā nṛpātmajais te ca tābhir agaman kṛtārthatām so bhavad varavadhūsamāgamaḥ pratyayaprakṛtiyogsaṃnibhaḥ  Ragh evam āttaratir ātmasaṃbhavāṃs tān niveśya caturo pi tatra saḥ adhvasu triṣu visṛṣṭamaithilaḥ svāṃ purīṃ daśaratho nyavartata  Ragh tasya jātu marutaḥ pratīpagā vartmasu dhavjatarupramāthinaḥ cikliśur bhṛśatayā varūthinīm uttaṭā iva nadīrayāḥ sthalīm  Ragh lakṣyate sma tadanantaraṃ ravir baddhabhīmapairveṣamaṇḍalaḥ vainateyaśamitasya bhogino bhogaveṣṭita iva cyuto maṇiḥ  Ragh śyenapakṣaparidhūsarālakāḥ sāṃdhyamegharudhirārdravāsasaḥ aṅganā iva rajasvalā diśo no babhūvur avalokanakṣamāḥ  Ragh bhāskaraś ca diśam adhyuvāsa yāṃ tāṃ śritāḥ pratibhayaṃ vavāśire kṣatraśoṇitapitṛkriyocitaṃ codayantya iva bhārgavaṃ śivāḥ  Ragh tat pratīpapavanādi vaikṛtaṃ prekṣya śāntim adhikṛtya kṛtyavit anvayuṅkta gurum īśvaraḥ kṣiteḥ svantam ity alaghayat sa tadvyathām  Ragh tejasaḥ sapadi rāśir utthitaḥ prādurāsa kila vāhinīmukhe yaḥ pramṛjya nayanāni sainikair lakṣaṇīyapuruṣākṛtiś cirāt  Ragh pitryam aṃśam upavītalakṣaṇaṃ mātṛkaṃ ca dhanur ūrjitaṃ dadhat yaḥ sasoma iva gharmadīdhitiḥ sadvijihva iva candanadrumaḥ  Ragh yena roṣaparuṣātmanaḥ pituḥ śāsane sthibhido pi tasthuṣā vepamānajananīśiraśchidā prāg ajīyata ghṛṇā tato mahī  Ragh akṣabhījavalayena nibabhau dakṣiṇaśravaṇasaṃsthitena yaḥ kṣatriyāntakaraṇaikaviṃśater vyājapūrvagaṇanām ivodvahan  Ragh taṃ pitur vadhabhavena manyunā rājavaṃśanidhanāya dīkṣitam bālasūnur avalokya bhārgavaṃ svāṃ daśāṃ ca viṣasāda pārthivaḥ  Ragh rāmanāma iti tulyam ātmaje vartamānam ahite ca dāruṇe hṛdyam asya bhayadāyi cābhavad ratnajātam iva hārasarpayoḥ  Ragh arghyam arghyam iti vādinaṃ nṛpaṃ so navekṣya bharatāgrajo yataḥ kṣatrakopadahanārciṣaṃ tataḥ saṃdadhe dṛśam udagratārakām  Ragh tena kārmukaniṣaktamuṣṭinā rāghavo vigatabhīḥ purogataḥ aṅgulīvivaracāriṇaṃ śaraṃ kurvatā nijagade yuyutsunā  Ragh kṣatrajātam apakāri vairi me tan nihatya bahuśaḥ śamaṃ gataḥ suptasarpa iva daṇḍaghaṭṭanād roṣito smi tava vikramaśravāt  Ragh maithilasya dhanur anyapārthivais tvaṃ kilānamitapūrvam akṣaṇoḥ tan niśamya bahavatā samarthaye vīryaśṛṅgam iva bhagnam ātmanaḥ  Ragh anyadā jagati rāma ity ayaṃ śabda uccarita eva mām agāt vrīḍam āvahati me sa saṃprati vyastavṛttir udayonmukhe tvayi  Ragh bibhrato stram acale py akuṇṭhitaṃ dvau matau mama ripū samāgasau homadhenuharaṇāc ca haihayas tvaṃ ca irtim apahartum udyataḥ  Ragh kṣatriyāntakaraṇo pi vikramas tena mām avati nājite tvayi pāvakasya mahimā sa gaṇyate kakṣavaj jvalati sāgare pi yaḥ  Ragh viddhi cāttabalam ojasā harer aiśvaraṃ dhanur abhāji yat tvayā khātamūlam anilo nadīrayaiḥ pātayaty api mṛdus taṭadrumam  Ragh tan madīyam idam āyudhaṃ jyayā saṃgamayya saśaraṃ vikṛṣyatām tiṣṭhatu pradhanam evam apy ahaṃ tulyabāhutarasā jitas tvayā  Ragh kātaro si yadi vodgatārciṣā tarjitaḥ paraśudhārayā mama jyānighātakaṭhināṅgulir vṛthā badhyatām abhayayācanāñjaliḥ  Ragh evam uktavati bhīmadarśane bhārgave smitavikampitādharaḥ taddhanurgrahaṇam eva rāghavaḥ pratyapadyata samartham uttaram  Ragh pūrvajanmadhanuṣā samāgataḥ so timātralaghudarśano bhavat kevalo pi subhago navāmbudaḥ kiṃ punas tridaśacāpalāñchitaḥ  Ragh tena bhūminihitaikakoṭi tat kārmukaṃ ca balinādhiropitam niṣprabhaś ca ripur āsa bhūbhṛtāṃ dhūmaśeṣa iva dhūmaketanaḥ  Ragh tāv ubhāv api parasparasthitau vardhamānaparihīnatejasau paśyati sma janatā dinātyaye pārvaṇau śaśidivākarāv iva  Ragh taṃ kṛpāmṛdur avekṣya bhārgavaṃ rāghavaḥ skhalitavīryam ātmani svaṃ ca saṃhitam amogham āśugaṃ vyājahāra harasūnasaṃnibhaḥ  Ragh na prahartum alam asmi nidayaṃ vipra ity abhibhavaty api tvayi śaṃṣa kiṃ gatim anena pattriṇā hanmi lokam uta te makhārjitam  Ragh pratyuvāca tam ṛṣir na tattvatas tvāṃ na vedmi puruṣaṃ purātanam gāṃ gatasya tava dhāma vaiṣṇavaṃ kopito hy asi mayā didṛkṣuṇā  Ragh bhasmasāt kṛtavataḥ pitṛdviṣaḥ pātrasāc ca vasudhāṃ sasāgarām āhito jayaviparyayo pi me ślāghya eva parameṣṭhinā tvayā  Ragh tad gatiṃ matimatāṃ varepsitāṃ puṇyatīrthagamanāya rakṣa me pīḍayiṣyati na māṃ khilīkṛtā svargapaddhatir abhogalolupam  Ragh pratyapadyata tatheti rāghavaḥ prāṅmukhaś ca visasarja sāyakam bhārgavasya sukṛto pi so bhavat svargamārgaparigho duratyayaḥ  Ragh rāghavo pi caraṇau taponidheḥ kṣamyatām iti vadan samaspṛṣat nirjiteṣu tarasā tarasvināṃ śatruṣu praṇatir eva kīrtaye  Ragh rājasatvam avadhūya mātṛkaṃ pitryam asmi gamitaḥ śamaṃ yadā nanv aninditaphalo mama tvayā nigraho py ayam anugrahīkṛtaḥ  Ragh sādhu yāmy aham avighnam astu te devakāryam upapādayiṣyataḥ ūcivān iti vacaḥ salakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajam ṛṣis tirodadhe  Ragh svaṃ niveśya kila dhāma rāghave vaiṣṇavaṃ viditaviṣṇutejasi svastidānam adhikṛtya cākṣayaṃ bhārgavo tha nijam āśramaṃ yayau  Ragh tasmin gate vijayinaṃ parirabhya rāmaṃ snehād amanyata pitā punar eva jātam tasyābhavat kṣaṇaśucaḥ paritoṣalābhaḥ kakṣāgnilaṅghitataror iva vṛṣṭipātaḥ  Ragh atha pathi gamayitvā kḷparamyopakārye katicid avanipālaḥ śarvarīḥ śarvakalpah puram aviśad ayodhyāṃ maithilīdarśanīnāṃ kuvalayitagavākṣāṃ locanair aṅganānām  Ragh nirviṣṭaviṣayasnehaḥ sa daśāntam upeyivān āsīd āsannanirvāṇaḥ pradīpārcir ivoṣasi  Ragh taṃ karṇamūlam āgatya rāme śrīr nasyatām iti kaikeyīśaṅkayevāha palitacchadmanā jarā  Ragh sā paurān paurakāntasya rāmasyābhyudayaśrutiḥ pratyekaṃ hlādayāṃ cakre kulyevodyānapādapān  Ragh tasyābhiṣekasaṃbhāraṃ kalpitaṃ krūraniścayā dūṣayām āsa kaikeyī śokoṣṇaiḥ pārthivāśrubhiḥ  Ragh sā kilāśvāsitā caṇḍī bhartrā tatsaṃśrutau varau udvavāmendrasiktā bhūr bilamagnāv ivoragau  Ragh tayoś caturdaśaikena rāmaṃ prāvrājayat samāḥ dvitīyena sutasyaicchad vaidhavyaikaphalāṃ śriyam  Ragh pitrā dattāṃ rudan rāmaḥ prāṅ mahīṃ pratyapadyata paścād vanāya gaccheti tadājñāṃ mudito grahīt  Ragh dadhato maṅgalakṣaume vasānasya ca valkale dadṛśur vismitās tasya mukharāgaṃ samaṃ janāḥ  Ragh sa sītālakṣmaṇasakhaḥ satyād gurum alopayan viveśa daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ pratyekaṃ ca satāṃ manaḥ  Ragh rājāpi tadviyogārtaḥ smṛtvā śāpaṃ svakarmajam śarīratyāgamātreṇa śuddhilābham amanyata  Ragh viproṣitakumāraṃ tad rājyam astamiteśvaram randhrānveṣaṇadakṣāṇāṃ dviṣām āmiṣatāṃ yayau  Ragh athānāthāḥ prakṛtayo mātṛbandhunivāsinam maulair ānāyayām āsur bhartaṃ stambhitāśrubhiḥ  Ragh śrutvā tathāvidhaṃ mṛtyuṃ kaikeyītanayaḥ pituḥ mātur na kevalaṃ svasyāḥ śriyo py āsīt parāṅmukhaḥ  Ragh sasainyaś cānvagād rāmaṃ darśitān āśramālayaiḥ tasya paśyan sasaumitrer udaśrur vasatidrumān  Ragh citrakūṭavanasthaṃ ca kathitasvargatir guroḥ lakṣmyā nimantrayāṃ cakre tam anucchiṣṭasaṃpadā  Ragh sa hi prathamaje tasminn akṛtaśrīparigrahe parivettāram ātmānaṃ mene svīkaraṇād bhuvaḥ  Ragh tam aśakyam apākraṣṭuṃ nirdeśāt svargiṇaḥ pituḥ yayāce pāduke paścāt kartuṃ rājyādhidevate  Ragh sa visṛṣṭas tathety uktvā bhrātrā naivāviśat purīm nandigrāmagatas tasya rājyaṃ nyāsam ivābhunak  Ragh dṛḍhabhaktir iti jyeṣṭhe rājyatṛṣṇāparāṅmukhaḥ mātuḥ pāpasya śuddhyarthaṃ prāyaścittam ivākarot  Ragh rāmo pi saha vaidehyā vane vanyena vartayan cacāra sānujaḥ śānto vṛddhekṣvākuvrataṃ yuvā  Ragh prabhāvastambhitacchāyam āśritaḥ sa vanaspatim kadācid aṅke sītāyāḥ śiśye kiṃcid iva śramāt  Ragh aindriḥ kila nakhais tasyā vidadāra stanau dvijaḥ priyopabhogacihneṣu paurobhāgyam ivācaran  Ragh mṛgamāṃsaṃ tataḥ sītāṃ rakṣantīm ātape dhṛtam pakṣatuṇḍanakhāghātair babādhe vāyaso balāt  Ragh tasminn āsthad iṣīkāstraṃ rāmo rāmāvabhodhitaḥ ātmānaṃ mumuce tasmād ekanetravyayena saḥ  Ragh rāmas tv āsannadeśatvād bharatāgamanaṃ punaḥ āśaṅkyotsukasāraṅgāṃ citrakūṭasthalīṃ jahau  Ragh prayayāv ātitheyeṣu vasann ṛṣikuleṣu saḥ dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ṛkṣeṣu vārṣikeṣv iva bhāskaraḥ  Ragh babhau tam anugacchantī videhādhipateḥ sutā pratiṣiddhāpi kaikeyyā lakṣmīr iva guṇonmukhī  Ragh anusūyātisṛṣṭena puṇyagandhena kānanam sā cakārāṅgarāgeṇa puṣpoccalita ṣaṭpadam  Ragh saṃdhyābhrakapiṣas tatra virādho nāma rākṣasaḥ atiṣṭhan mārgam āvṛtya rāmasyendor iva grahaḥ  Ragh sa jaharā tayor madhye maithilīṃ lokaśoṣaṇaḥ nabhonabhasyayor vṛṣṭim avagraha ivāntare  Ragh taṃ viniṣpiṣya kākutsthau purā dūṣayati shtalīm gandhenāśucinā ceti vasudhāyāṃ nicakhnatuḥ  Ragh pañcavaṭyāṃ tato rāmaḥ śāsanāt kumbhajanmanaḥ anapoṣhasthitis tasthau vindhyādriḥ prakṛtāv iva  Ragh rāvaṇāvarajā tatra rāghavaṃ madanāturā abhipede nidāghārtā vyālīva malayadrumam  Ragh sā sītāsaṃnidhāv eva taṃ vavre kathitānvayā atyārūḍho hi nārīṇām akālajño maobhavaḥ  Ragh kalatravān ahaṃ bāle kanīyāṃsaṃ bhajasva me iti rāmo vṛṣasyantīṃ vṛṣaskandhaḥ śaśāsa tām  Ragh jyeṣṭhābhigamanāt pūrvaṃ tenāpy anabhinanditā sābhūd rāmāśrayā bhūyo nadīvobhayakūlabhāk  Ragh saṃrambhaṃ maithilīhāsaḥ kṣaṇaṃ saumyāṃ nināya tām nivātastimitāṃ velāṃ candrodaya ivodadheḥ  Ragh phalam asyopahāsasya sadyaḥ prāpsyasi paśya mām mṛgyaḥ paribhavo vyāghryām ity avehi tvayā kṛtam  Ragh ity uktvā maithilīṃ bhartur aṅke nirviśatīṃ bhayāt rūpaṃ śūrpaṇakhānāmnaḥ sadṛśaṃ pratyapadyata  Ragh lakṣmaṇaḥ prathamaṃ śrutvā kokilāmañjubhāṣiṇīm śivāghorasvanāṃ paścād bubudhe vikṛteti tām  Ragh parṇaśālām atha kṣipraṃ vidhṛtāsiḥ praviśya saḥ vairūpyapaunaruktyena bhīṣaṇāṃ tām ayojayat  Ragh sā vakranakhadhāriṇyā veṇukarkaśaparvayā aṅkuśākārayāṅgulyā tāv atarjayad ambare  Ragh prāpya cāśu jansthānaṃ kharādibhyas tathāvidham rāmopakramam ācakhyau rakṣaḥparibhavaṃ navam  Ragh mukhāvayavalūṇāṃ tāṃ nairṛtā yat purodadhuḥ rāmābhiyāyināṃ teṣāṃ tad evābhūd amaṅgalam  Ragh udāyudhān āpatatas tān dṛptān prekṣya rāghavaḥ nidadhe vijayāśaṃsāṃ cāpe sītāṃ ca lakṣmaṇe  Ragh eko dāśarathī rāmo yātudhānāḥ sahasraśaḥ te tu yāvanta evājau tāvāṃś ca dadṛśe sa taiḥ  Ragh asajjanena kākutsthaḥ prayuktam atha dūṣaṇam na cakṣame śubhācāraḥ sa dūṣaṇam ivātmanaḥ  Ragh taṃ śaraiḥ pratijagrāha kharatiśirasau ca saḥ khramaśas te punas tasya cāpāt samam ivodyayuḥ  Ragh tais trayāṇāṃ śitair bāṇair yathāpūrvaviśuddhibhiḥ āyur dehātigaiḥ pītaṃ rudhiraṃ tu patatribhiḥ  Ragh tasmin rāmaśarotkṛtte bale mahati rakṣasām utthitaṃ dadṛśe nyac ca kabandhebhyo na kiṃcana  Ragh sā bāṇavarṣiṇaṃ rāmaṃ yodhayitvā suradviṣām aprabodhāya suṣvāpa gṛdhracchāye varūthinī  Ragh rāghavāstravidīrṇānāṃ rāvaṇaṃ prati rakṣasām teṣāṃ śūrpaṇakhaivaikā duṣpratvṛttiharābhavat  Ragh nigrahāt svasur āptānāṃ vadhāc ca dhanadānujaḥ rāmeṇa nihataṃ mene padaṃ daśasu mūrdhasu  Ragh rakṣasā mṛgarūpeṇa vañcayitvā sa rāghavau jaharā sītāṃ pakṣīndraprayāsakṣaṇavighnitaḥ  Ragh tau sītānveṣiṇau gṛdhraṃ lūnapakṣam apaśyatām prāṇair daśarathaprīter anṛṇaṃ kaṇṭhavartibhiḥ  Ragh sa rāvaṇahṛtāṃ tābhyāṃ vacasācaṣṭa maithilīm ātmanaḥ sumahat karma vraṇair āvedya saṃsthitaḥ  Ragh tayos rāvaṇahṛtāṃ tābhyāṃ pitṛvyāpattiśokayoḥ pitarīvāgnisaṃskārāt parā vavṛtire kriyāḥ  Ragh vadhanirdhūtaśāpasya kabandhasyopadeśataḥ mumūrcha sakhyaṃ rāmasya samānavyasane harau  Ragh sa hatvā vālinaṃ vīras tatpade cirakāṅkṣite dhātoḥ sthāna ivādeśaṃ sugrīvaṃ saṃnyaveśayat  Ragh itas tataś ca vaidehīm anveṣṭuṃ bhartṛcoditāḥ kapayaś cerur ārtasya rāmasyeva manorathāḥ  Ragh pravṛttāv upalabdhāyāṃ tasyāḥ saṃpātidarśanāt mārutiḥ sāgaraṃ tīrṇaḥ saṃsāram iva nirmamaḥ  Ragh dṛṣṭā vicinvatā tena laṅkāyāṃ rākṣasīvṛtā jānakī viṣavallībhiḥ parīteva mahauṣadhiḥ  Ragh tasyai bhartur abhijñāmam aṅgulīyaṃ dadau kapiḥ pratyudgatam ivānuṣṇais tadānandāśrubhindubhiḥ  Ragh nirvāpya priyasaṃdeśaiḥ sītām akṣavadhoddhataḥ sa dadāha purīṃ laṅkāṃ kṣaṇasoḍhārinigrahaḥ  Ragh pratyabhijñānaratnaṃ ca rāmāyādarśayat kṛtī hṛdayaṃ svayam āyātaṃ vaidehyā iva mūrtimat  Ragh sa prāpa hṛdayanyastamaṇiparśanimīlitaḥ apayodharasaṃsargaṃ priyāliṅgananirvṛtim  Ragh śrutvā rāmaḥ priyodantaṃ mene tatsaṃgamotsukaḥ mahārṇavaparikṣepaṃ laṅkāyāḥ parikhālaghum  Ragh sa pratasthe rināśāya harisainyair anudrutaḥ na kevalaṃ dharāpṛṣṭhe vyomni saṃbādhavartibhiḥ  Ragh nirviṣṭam udadheḥ kūle taṃ prapede vibhīṣaṇaḥ snehād rākṣasalakṣmyeva buddhim ādiśya coditaḥ  Ragh tasmai niśācaraiśvaryaṃ pratiśuśrāva rāghavaḥ kāle khalu samārabdhāḥ phalaṃ badhnanti nītayaḥ  Ragh sa setuṃ bandhayām āsa plavagair lavaṇāmbhasi rasātalād ivonmagnaṃ śeṣaṃ svapnāya śārṅgiṇaḥ  Ragh tenottīrya pathā laṅkāṃ rodhayām āsa piṅgalaiḥ dvitīyaṃ hemaprākāraṃ kurvadbhir iva vānaraiḥ  Ragh raṇaḥ pravavṛte tatra bhīmaḥ plavagarakṣasām digvijṛmbhitakākutsthapaulastyajayaghoṣaṇaḥ  Ragh pādapāviddhaparighaḥ śilāniṣpiṣṭamudgaraḥ atiśastranakhanyāsaḥ śailarugṇa mataṅgajaḥ  Ragh atha rāmaśiraśchedadarśanodbhrāntacetanām sītāṃ māyeti śaṃsantī trijaṭā samajīvayat  Ragh kāmaṃ jīvati me nātha iti sā vijahau śucam prāṅ matvā satyam asyāntaṃ jīvitāsmīti lajjitā  Ragh garuḍāpātaviśliṣṭameghanādāstrabandhanaḥ dāśarathyoḥ kṣaṇakleśaḥ svapnavṛtta ivābhavat  Ragh tato bibheda paulastyaḥ śaktyā vakṣasi lakṣmaṇam rāmas tv anāhato py āsīd vidīrṇahṛdayaḥ śucā  Ragh sa mārutisamānītamahauṣadhihatavyathaḥ laṅkāstrīṇāṃ punaś cakre vilāpācāryakaṃ śaraiḥ  Ragh sa nādaṃ meghanādasya dhanuś cendrāyudhaprabham meghasyeva śaratkālo na kiṃcit paryaśeṣayat  Ragh kleśena mahatā nidrāṃ tyājitaṃ raṇadurjayam rāvaṇaḥ preṣayām āsa yuddhāyānujam ātmanaḥ  RaghA jaghāna sa tadādeśāt kapīn ugrān anekaśaḥ viveśa ca purīṃ laṅkāṃ samādāya harīśvaram  RaghB kumbhakarṇaḥ kapīndreṇa tulyāvasthaḥ svasuḥ kṛtaḥ rurodha rāmaṃ śṛṅgīva ṭaṅkacchinnamanaḥśilaḥ  Ragh akāle bodhito bhrātrā priyasvapno vṛthā bhavān rāmeṣubhir itīvāsau dīrghanidrāṃ praveśitaḥ  Ragh itarāṇy api rakṣāṃsi petur vānarakoṭiṣu rajāṃsi samarotthāni
