anyonyapāvanam abhūd ubhayaṃ sametya  Ragh krośārdhaṃ prakṛtipuraḥsareṇa gatvā kākutsthaḥ stimitajavena puṣpakeṇa śatrughnaprativihitopakāryam āryaḥ sāketopavanam udāram adhyuvāsa  Ragh uttiṣṭha vatse nanu sānujo sau daśāntaraṃ tatra samaṃ prapanne apaśyatāṃ dāśarathī jananyau chedād ivopaghnataror vratatyau  Ragh ubhāv ubhābhyāṃ praṇatau hatārī yathākramaṃ vikramaśobhinau tau vispaṣṭam asrāndhatayā na dṛṣṭau jñātau sutasparśasukhopalambhāt  Ragh ānandajaḥ śokajam aśru bāṣpas tayor aśītaṃ śiśiro bibheda gaṅgāsarayvor jalam uṣṇatpataṃ himādrinisyanda ivāvatīrṇaḥ  Ragh te putrayor nairṛtaśastramārgān ārdrān ivāṅge sadayaṃ spṛśantyau apīpsitaṃ kṣatrakulāṅganānāṃ na vīrasūśabdam akāmayetām  Ragh kleśāvahā bhartur alakṣaṇāhaṃ sīteti nāma svam udīrayantī svargapratiṣṭhasya guror mahiṣyāv abhaktibhedena vadhūr vavande  Ragh uttiṣṭha vatse nanu sānujo sau vṛttena bhartā śucinā tavaiva kṛcchraṃ mahat tīrṇa iti priyārhāṃ tām ūcatus te priyam apy amithyā  Ragh athābhiṣekaṃ raghuvaṃśaketoḥ prārabdham ānandajalair jananyoḥ nirvartayām āsur amātyavṛddhās tīrthāhṛtaiḥ kāñcanakumbhatoyaiḥ  Ragh saritsamudrān sarasīś ca gatvā rakṣaḥkapīndrair upapāditāni tasyāpatan mūrdhni jalāni jiṣṇor vindhyasya meghaprabhavā ivāpaḥ  Ragh tapasviveṣakriyayāpi tāvad yaḥ prekṣaṇīyaḥ sutarāṃ babhūva rājendranepathyavidhānaśobhā rasyoditāsīt punaruktadoṣā  Ragh sa maularakṣoharimiśrasainyas tūryasvanānanditapauravargaḥ viveṣa saudhodgatalājavarṣām uttoraṇām anvayarājadhānīm  Ragh saumitriṇā sāvarajena mandam ādhūtavālavyajano rathasthaḥ dhṛtātapatro bharatena sākṣād upāyasaṃghāta iva pravṛddhaḥ  Ragh prāsādakālāgurudhūmarājis tasyāḥ puro vāyuvaśena bhinnā vanān nivṛttena raghūdvahena muktā svayaṃ veṇir ivābhāse  Ragh śvaśrūjanānuṣṭhitacāruveṣāṃ karṇīrathasthāṃ raghuvīrapatnīm prāsādavātāyanadṛśyabandhaiḥ sāketanāryo ñjalibhiḥ praṇemuḥ  Ragh sphuratprabhāmaṇḍalam ānusūyaṃ sā bibhratī śāśvatam aṅgarāgam rarāja śuddheti punaḥ svapuryai saṃdarśita vahnigateva bhartrā  Ragh veśmāni rāmaḥ paribarhavanti viśrāṇya sauhārdhanidhiḥ suhṛdbyaḥ bāṣpāyamāṇo balimanniketam ālekhyaśeṣasya pitur viveśa  Ragh kṛtāñjalis tatra yad amba satyān nābhraśyata svargaphalād gurur naḥ tac cintyamānaṃ sukṛtaṃ taveti jahāra lajjāṃ bharatasya mātuḥ  Ragh tathā ca sugrīvavibhīśaṇādīn upācarat kṛtrimasaṃvidhābhiḥ saṃkalpamātroditasiddhayas te krāntā yathā cetasi vismayena  Ragh sabhājanāyopagatān sa divyān munīn puraskṛtya hatasya śatroḥ śuśrāva tebhyaḥ prabhavādi vṛttaṃ svavikrame gauravam ādadhānam  Ragh pratiprayāteṣu tapodhaneṣu sukhād avijñātagatārdhamāsān sītāsvahastopahṛtāgryapūjān rakṣaḥkapīndrān visasarja rāmaḥ  Ragh tac cātmacintāsulabhaṃ vimānaṃ hṛtaṃ surāreḥ saha jīvitena kailāsanāthodvahanāya bhūyaḥ puṣpaṃ divaḥ puṣpakam anvamaṃsta  Ragh pitur niyogād vanavāsam evaṃ nistīrya rāmaḥ pratipannarājyaḥ dharmārthakāmeṣu samāṃ prapede yathā tathaivāvarajeṣu vṛttim  Ragh sarvāsu mātṛṣv api vatsalatvāt sa nirviśeṣapratipattir āsīt ṣaḍānanāpītapayodharāsu netā camūnām iva kṛttikāsu  Ragh tenārthavāṃl lobhaparāṅmukhena tena ghnatā vighnabhayaṃ kriyāvān tenāsa lokaḥ pitṛmān vinetrā tenaiva śokāpanudena putrī  Ragh sa paurakāryāṇi samīkṣya kāle reme videhādhipater duhitrā upasthitaś cāru vapus tadīyaṃ kṛtvopabhogotsukayeva lakṣmyā  Ragh tayor yathāprārthitam indriyārthān āseduṣoḥ sadmasu citravatsu prāptāni duḥkhāny api daṇḍakeṣu saṃcintyamānāni sukhāny abhūvan  Ragh athādhikasnigdhavilocanena mukhena sītā śarapāṇḍureṇa ānandayitrī pariṇetur āsīd anakṣaravyañjitadohadena  Ragh tām aṅkam āropya kṛśāṅgayaṣṭiṃ varṇāntarākrāntapayodharāgrām vilajjamānāṃ rahasi pratītaḥ prapraccha rāmāṃ ramaṇo bhilāṣam  Ragh sā daṣṭanīvārabalīnihiṃsraiḥ saṃbaddha vaikhānasakanyakāni iyeṣa bhūyaḥ kuśavanti gantuṃ bhāgīrathītīratapovanāni  Ragh tasyai pratiśrutya raghupravīras tad īpsitaṃ pārśvacarānuyātaḥ ālokayiṣyan muditām ayodhyāṃ prāsādam abhraṃliham āruroha  Ragh ṛddhāpaṇaṃ rājapathaṃ sa paśyan vigāhyamānāṃ sarayūṃ ca naubhiḥ vilāsibhiś cādhyuṣitāni pauraiḥ puropakaṇṭhopavanāni reme  Ragh sa kiṃvadantīṃ vadatāṃ purogaḥ svaṛttam uddiśya viśuddhavṛttaḥ sarpādhirājorubhujo pasarpaṃ papraccha bhadraṃ vijitāribhadraḥ  Ragh nirbandhapṛṣṭaḥ sa jagāda sarvaṃ stuvanti paurāś caritaṃ tvadīyam anyatra rakṣobhavanoṣitāyāḥ parigrahān mānavadeva devyāḥ  Ragh kalatranindāguruṇā kilaivam abhyāhataṃ kīrtiviparyayeṇa ayoghanenāya ivābhitaptaṃ vaidehibandhor hṛdayaṃ vidadre  Ragh kim ātmanirvādakathām upekṣe jāyām adoṣām uta saṃtyajāmi ity ekapakṣāśrayaviklavatvād āsīt sa dolācalacittavṛttiḥ  Ragh niścitya cānanyanivṛtti vācyaṃ tyāgena patnyāḥ parimārṣṭum aicchat api svadehāt kim utendriyārthād yaśodhanānāṃ hi yaśo garīyaḥ  Ragh sa saṃnipātyāvarajān hataujās tadvikriyādarśanaluptaharṣān kaulīnam ātmāśrayam ācacakṣe tebhyaḥ punaś cedam uvāca vākyam  Ragh rājarṣivaṃśasya raviprasūter upasthitaḥ paśyata kīdṛśo yam mattaḥ sadācāraśuceḥ kalaṅkaḥ payodavātād iva darpaṇasya  Ragh paureṣu so haṃ vahulībhavantam apāṃ taraṅgeṣv iva tailabindum soḍhuṃ na tatpūrvam avarṇam īśe ālānikaṃ sthāṇum iva dviependraḥ  Ragh tasyāpanodāya phalapravṛttāv upasthitāyām api nirvyapekṣaḥ tyakṣyāmi vaidehasutāṃ purastāt samudranemiṃ pitur ājñayeva  Ragh avaimi cainām anagheti kiṃ tu lokāpavādo balavān mato me chāyā hi bhūmeḥ śaśino malatvenāropitā śuddhimataḥ prajābhiḥ  Ragh rakṣovadhānto na ca me prayāso vyarthaḥ sa vairapratimocanāya amarṣaṇaḥ śoṇitakāṅkṣayā kiṃ padā spṛśantaṃ daśati dvijihvaḥ  Ragh tad eṣa sargaḥ karuṇārdracittair na me bhavadbhiḥ pratiṣedhanīyaḥ yady arthitā nirhṛtavācyaśalyān prāṇān mayā dhārayituṃ ciraṃ vaḥ  Ragh ity uktavantaṃ janakātmajāyāṃ nitāntarūkṣābhiniveśam īśam na kaścana bhrātṛṣu teṣu śakto niṣeddhum āsīd anuvartituṃ vā  Ragh sa lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmaṇapūrvajanmā vilokya lokatrayagītakīrtiḥ saumyeti cābhāṣya yathārthabhāṣī sthitaṃ nideśe pṛthag ādideśa  Ragh prajāvatī dohadaśaṃsinī te tapovaneṣu spṛhayālur eva saumyeti cābhāṣya yathārthabhāṣī prāpayya vālmīkipadaṃ tyajainām  Ragh sa śuśruvān mātari bhārgaveṇa pitur niyogāt prahṛtam dviṣadvat pratyagrahīd agrajaśāsanaṃ tad ājñā gurūṇāṃ hy avicāraṇīyā  Ragh athānukūlaśravaṇapratītām atrasnubhir yuktadhuraṃ turaṃgaiḥ rathaṃ sumantra pratipannaraśmim āropya vaidehasutāṃ pratasthe  Ragh sā nīyamānā rucirān pradeśān priyaṃkaro me priya ity anandat nābuddha kalpadrumatāṃ vihāya jātaṃ tam ātmany asipattravṛkṣam  Ragh jugūha tasyāḥ pathi lakṣmaṇo yat savyetareṇa sphuratā tad akṣṇā ākhyātam asyai guru bhāvi duḥkham atyantaluptapriyadarśanena  Ragh sā durnimittopagatād viṣādāt sadyaḥ parimlānamukhāravindā rājñaḥ śivaṃ sāvarajasya bhūyād ity āśaśaṃse karaṇair abāhyaiḥ  Ragh guror niyogād vanitāṃ vanānte sādhvīṃ sumitrātanayo vihāsyan avāryatevotthitavīcihastair jahnor duhitrā shitayā purastāt  Ragh rathāt sa yantrā nigṛhītavāhāt tāṃ bhrātṛhyāyāṃ puline vatārya gaṅgāṃ niṣādāhṛtanauviśeṣas tatāra saṃdhām iva satyasaṃdhaḥ  Ragh atha vyavasthāpitavāk kathaṃcit saumitrir antargatabāṣpakaṇṭhaḥ autpātiko megha ivāśmavarṣaṃ mahīpateḥ śāsanam ujjagāra  Ragh tato bhiṣaṅgānilavipraviddhā prabhraśyamānābharaṇasprasūnā svamūrtilābhaprakṛtiṃ dharitrīṃ lateva sītā sahasā jagāma  Ragh ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhavaḥ kathaṃ tvāṃ tyajed akasmāt patir āryavṛttaḥ iti kṣitiḥ saṃśayiteva tasyai dadau praveśaṃ jananī na tāvat  Ragh sā luptasaṃjñā na viveda duḥkhaṃ pratyāgatāsuḥ samatapyatāntaḥ tasyāḥ sumitrātmajayatnalabdho mohād abhūt kaṣṭataraḥ prabodhaḥ  Ragh na cāvadad bhartur avarṇam āryā nirākariṣṇor vṛjinād ṛte pi ātmānam eva sthiraduḥkhabājaṃ punaḥ punar duṣkṛtinaṃ nininda  Ragh āśvāsya rāmāvarajaḥ satīṃ tām ākhyātavālmīkiniketamārgaḥ nighnasya me bhartṛnideśaraukṣyaṃ devi kṣamasveti babhūva namraḥ  Ragh sītā samutthāpya jagāda vākyaṃ prītāsmi te saumyacirāya jīva viḍaujasā viṣṇur ivāgrajena bhrātrā yad itthaṃ paravān asi tvam  Ragh śvaśrūjanaṃ sarvam anukrameṇa vijñāpaya prāpitamatpraṇāmaḥ prajāniśekaṃ mayi vartamānaṃ sūnor anudhyāyata cetaseti  Ragh vācyas tvayā madvacanāt sa rājā vahnau viśuddhām api yat samakṣam māṃ lokavādaśravaṇād ahāsīḥ śrutasya kiṃ tat sadṛśaṃ kulasya  Ragh kalyāṇabuddher atha vā tavāyaṃ na kāmacāro mayi śaṅkanīyaḥ mamaiva janmāntarapātakānāṃ vipākavisphūrjathur aprasahyaḥ  Ragh upasthitāṃ pūrvam apāsya lakṣmīṃ vanaṃ mayā sārdham asi prapannaḥ tad āspadaṃ prāpya tayātiroṣāt soḍhāsmi na tvadbhavane vasantī  Ragh niśācaropaplutabhartṛkāṇāṃ tapasvinīnāṃ bhavataḥ prasādāt bhūtvā śaraṇyā śaraṇārtham anyāṃ kathaṃ prapatsye tvayi dīpyamāne  Ragh kiṃ vā tavātyantaviyogamoghe kuryām upekṣāṃ hatajīvite smin syād rakṣaṇīyaṃ yadi me na tejas tvadīyam antargatam antarāyaḥ  Ragh sāhaṃ tapaḥ sūryaniviṣṭadṛṣṭir ūrdhvaṃ prasūtes caritum yatiṣye tathā yathā me jananāntare pi tvam eva bhartā na ca viprayogaḥ  Ragh nṛpasya varṇāśramarakṣaṇaṃ yat sa eva dharmo manunā praṇītaḥ nirvāsitāpy evam atas tvayāhaṃ tapasvisāmānyam avekṣaṇīyā  Ragh tatheti tasyāḥ pratigṛhya vācaṃ rāmānuje dṛśṭipathaṃ vyatīte sā muktakaṇṭhaṃ vyasanātibhārāc cakranda vignā kurarīva bhūyaḥ  Ragh nṛtyaṃ mayūrāḥ kusumāni vṛkṣā darbhān upāttān vijahur hariṇyaḥ tasyāḥ prapanne samaduḥkhabhāvam atyantam āsīd ruditaṃ vane pi  Ragh tām abhyagacchad ruditānusārī kaviḥ kuśedhmāharaṇāya yātaḥ niṣādaviddhāṇḍajadarśanotthaḥ ślokatvam āpadyata yasya śokaḥ  Ragh tam aśru netrāvaraṇaṃ pramṛjya sītā vilāpād viratā vavande tasyai munir dohadaliṅgadarśī dāśvān supurtrāśiṣam ity uvāca  Ragh jāne viṣṛśṭāṃ praṇidhānatas tvāṃ mithyāpavādakṣubhitena bhartrā tan mā vyathiṣṭhā viṣayāntarasthaṃ prāptāsi vaidehi pitur niketam  Ragh uthkātalokatrayakaṇṭake pi satyapratijñe py avikatthane pi tvāṃ praty akasmāt kaluṣapravṛttāv asty eva manyur bharatāgraje me  Ragh tavendukīrtiḥ śvaśuraḥ sakhā me satāṃ bhavocchedakaraḥ pitā te dhuri sthitā tvaṃ patidevatānāṃ kiṃ tan na yenāsi mamānukampyā  Ragh tapasvisaṃsargavinitatsattve tapovane vītabhayā vasāsmin ito bhaviṣyaty anaghaprasūter apatyasaṃskāramayo vidhis te  Ragh aśūnyatīrāṃ munisaṃniveśais tamopahantrīṃ tamasāṃ vigāhya tatsaikatotsaṅgabalikriyābhiḥ saṃpatsyate te manasaḥ prasādaḥ  Ragh puṣpaṃ phalaṃ cārtavam āharantyo bījaṃ ca bāleyam akṛṣṭarohi vinodayiṣyanti navābhiṣaṅgām udāravāco munikanyakās tvām  Ragh payoghaṭair āśramabālavṛkṣān saṃvardhayantī svabalānurūpaiḥ asaṃśayaṃ prāk tanayopapatteḥ stanaṃdhayaprītim avāpsyasi tvam  Ragh anugrahapratyabhinandinīṃ tāṃ vālmīkir ādāya dayārdracetāḥ sāyaṃ mṛgādhyāsitavedipārśvaṃ svam āśramaṃ śāntamṛgaṃ nināya  Ragh tām arpayām āsa ca śokadīnāṃ tadāgamaprītiṣu tāpasīṣu nirviṣṭasārāṃ pitṛbhir himāṃśor antyāṃ kalāṃ darśa ivauṣadhīṣu  Ragh tā iṅgudīsnehakṛtapradīpam āstīrṇamedhyājinatalpam antaḥ tasyai saparyānupadaṃ dinānte nivāsahetor uṭajaṃ viteruḥ  Ragh tatrābhiṣekaprayatā vasantī prayuktapūjā vidhinātithibhyaḥ vanyena sā valkalinī śarīraṃ patyuḥ prajāsaṃtataye babhāra  Ragh api prabhuḥ sānuśayo dhunā syāt kim utsukaḥ śakrajito pi hantā śaśaṃsa sītāparidevanāntam anuṣṭhitaṃ śāsanam agrajāya  Ragh babhūva rāmaḥ sahasā sabāṣpas tuṣāravarṣīva sahasyacandraḥ kaulīnabhītena gṛhān nirastā na tena vaidehasutā manastaḥ  Ragh nigṛhya śokaṃ svayam eva dhīmān varṇāśramāvekṣaṇajāgarūkaḥ sa bhrātṛsādhāraṇabhogam ṛddhaṃ rājyaṃ rajoriktamanāḥ śaśāsa  Ragh tām ekabhāryāṃ parivādabhīroḥ sādhvīm api tyaktavato nṛpasya vakṣasy asaṃghaṭṭasukhaṃ vasantī reje sapatnīrahiteva lakṣmīḥ  Ragh sītāṃ hitvā daśamukharipur nopayema yad anyāṃ tasyā eva pratikṛtisakho yat kratūn ājahāra vṛttāntena śravaṇaviṣayaprāpiṇā tena bhartuḥ sā durvāraṃ katham api parityāgaduḥkhaṃ viṣehe  Ragh kṛtasītāparityāgaḥ sa ratnākaramekhalām bubhūje pṛthivīpālaḥ pṛthivīm eva kevalām  Ragh lavaṇena viluptejyās tāmisreṇa tam abhyayuḥ munayo yamunābhājaḥ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇārthinaḥ  Ragh avekṣya rāmaṃ te tasmin na prajahruḥ svatejasā trāṇābhāve hi śāpāstrāḥ kurvanti tapaso vyayam  Ragh pratiśuśrāva kākutsthas tebhyo vighnapratikriyām dharmasaṃrakṣaṇāyaiva pravṛttir bhuvi śārṅgiṇaḥ  Ragh te rāmāya vadhopāyam ācakhyur vibudhaviṣaḥ durjayo lavaṇaḥ śūlī viśūlaḥ prārthyatām iti  Ragh ādideśātha śatrughnaṃ teṣāṃ kṣemāya rāghavaḥ kariṣyann iva nāmāsya yathārtham arinigrahāt  Ragh yaḥ kaścana raghūṇāṃ hi param ekaḥ paraṃtapaḥ apavāda ivotsargaṃ vyāvartayitum īśvaraḥ  Ragh agrajena prayuktāśīs tadā dāśarathī rathī yayau vanstahliḥ paśyan puṣpitāḥ surabhīr abhīḥ  Ragh rāmādeśād anupadaṃ senāṅgaṃ tasya siddhaye paścād adhyayanārthasya dhātor adhir ivābhavat  Ragh ādiṣṭavartmā munibhiḥ sa gacchaṃs tapatāṃ varaḥ virarāja rathapṛṣṭhair vālakhilyair ivāṃśumān  Ragh tasya mārgavaśād ekā babhūva vasatir yataḥ rathasvanotkaṇṭhamṛge vālmīkīye tapovane  Ragh tam ṛṣiḥ pūjayām āsa kumāraṃ klāntavāhanam tapaḥprabhāvasiddhābhir viśeṣapratipattibhiḥ  Ragh tasyām evāsya yāminyām antarvatnī prajāvatī sutāv asūta saṃpannau kośadaṇḍāv iva kṣitiḥ  Ragh saṃtānaśravaṇād bhrātuḥ saumitriḥ saumanasyavān prāñjalir munim āmantrya prātar yuktaratho yayau  Ragh sa ca prāpa madhūpaghnaṃ kumbhīnasyāś ca kukṣijaḥ vanāt karam ivādāya sattvarāśim upasthitaḥ  Ragh dhūmadhūmro vasāghandhī jvālābabhruśiroruhaḥ kravyādgaṇaparīvāraś citāgnir iva jaṅgamaḥ  Ragh apaśulaṃ tam āsādya lavaṇaṃ lakṣmaṇānujaḥ rurodha saṃmukhīno hi jayo randhraprahāriṇām  Ragh nātiparyāptam ālakṣya matkukṣer adya bhojanam diṣṭyā tvam asi me dhātrā bhīgtenevopapāditaḥ  Ragh iti saṃtarjya śatrughnaṃ rākṣasas tajjighāṃsayā prāṃśum utpāṭayām āsa mustāstambam iva drumam  Ragh saumitrer niśitair bāṇair antarā śakalīkṛtaḥ gātraṃ puṣparajaḥ prāpa na śākhī nairṛteritaḥ  Ragh vināśāt tasya vṛkṣasya rakṣas tasmai mahopalam prajighāya kṛtāntasya muṣṭiṃ pṛthag iva sthitam  Ragh aindram astram upādāya śatrughnena sa tāḍitaḥ sikatābhyo pi hi parāṃ prapede paramāṇutām  Ragh dakṣiṇaṃ doṣam udyamya rākṣasas tam upādravat ekatāla ivopātapavanaprerito giriḥ  Ragh kārṣnena pattrinā śatruḥ sa bhinnarhṛdayaḥ patan ānināya bhuvaḥ kampaṃ jahārāśramavāsinām  Ragh vayasāṃ paṅktayaḥ petur hatasyopari rakṣasaḥ tatpratidvandino mūrdhni divyāḥ kusumavṛṣṭayaḥ  Ragh sa hatvā lavaṇaṃ vīras tadā mene mahaujasaḥ bhrātuḥ sodaryam ātmānam indrajidvadhaśobhinaḥ  Ragh tasya saṃstūyamānasya caritārthais tapasvibhiḥ śuśubhe vikramodagraṃ vrīḍayāvanataṃ śiraḥ  Ragh upakūlaṃ sa kālindyāḥ purīṃ pauruṣabhūṣaṇaḥ nirmame nirmamo rtheṣu mathurāṃ madhurākṛtiḥ  Ragh yā saurājyaprakāśābhir babhau pauravibhūtibhiḥ svargābhiṣyandavamanaṃ kṛtvevopaniveśitā  Ragh tatra saudhagataḥ paśyan yamunāṃ cakravākinīm hema bhaktimatīṃ bhūmeḥ praveṇīm iva pripiye  Ragh sakhā daśarathasyātha janakasya ca mantrakṛt saṃcaskārobhayaprītyā maithileyau yathāvidhi  Ragh sa tau kuśalavonmṛṣṭagarbhakledau tadākhyayā kaviḥ kuśalavāv eva cakāra kila nāmataḥ  Ragh sāṅgaṃ ca vedam adhyāpya kiṃcidutkrāntaśaiśavau svakṛtiṃ gāpayām āsa kaviprathamapaddhatim  Ragh rāmasya madhuraṃ vṛttaṃ gāyantau mātur agrataḥ tadviyogavyathāṃ kiṃcic chithilīcakratuḥ sutau  Ragh itare pi raghor vaṃśyās trayas tretāgnitejasaḥ tadyogāt pativatnīṣu patnīṣv āsan dvisūnavaḥ  Ragh śatrughātini śatrughnaḥ subāhau ca bahuśrute mathurāvidiśe sūnvor nidadhe pūrvajotsukaḥ  Ragh bhūyas tapovyayo mā bhūd vālmīker iti so tyagāt maithilītanayodgītaniṣpandamṛgam āśramam  Ragh vaśī viveśa cāyodhyāṃ rathyāsaṃskāraśobhinīm lavaṇasya vadhāt paurair atigauravam īkṣitaḥ  Ragh sa dadarśa sabhāmadhye sabhāsadbhir upasthitam rāmaṃ sītāparityāgād asāmaṇyapatiṃ bhuvaḥ  Ragh tam abhyanandat praṇataṃ lavaṇāntakam agrajaḥ kālanemivadhāt prītas turāṣāḍ iva śārṅgiṇam  Ragh sa pṛṣṭaḥ sarvato vārttām ākhyād rājñe na saṃtatim pratyarpayiṣyataḥ kāle kaver ādyasya śāsanāt  Ragh atha jānapado vipraḥ śiśum aprāptayauvanam avatāry āṅkaśayyāsthaṃ dvāri cakranda bhūpateḥ  Ragh śocanīyāsi vasudhe yā tvaṃ daśarathāc cyutā rāmahastam anuprāpya kaṣṭāt kaṣṭataraṃ gatā  Ragh śrutvā tasya śuco hetuṃ goptā jihrāya rāghavaḥ na hy akālabhavo mṛtyur ikṣvākupadam aspṛśat  Ragh sa muhūrtaṃ sahasveti dvijam āśvāsya duḥkhitam yānaṃ sasmāra kauberaṃ vaivasvatajigīṣayā  Ragh āttaśastras tad adhyāsya pratisthaḥ sa raghūdvahaḥ uccacāra puras tasya gūḍharūpā sarasvatī  Ragh rājan prajāsu te kaścid apacāraḥ pravartate tam anviṣya praśamayer bhavitāsi tataḥ kṛtī  Ragh ity āptavacanād rāmo vineṣyan varṇavikriyām diśaḥ papāta pattreṇa veganiṣkampaketunā  Ragh atha dhūmābhitāmrākṣaṃ vṛkṣākhāvalambinam dadarśa kaṃcid aikśvākas tapasyantam adhomukham  Ragh pṛṣṭanāmānvayo rājñā sa kilācaṣṭa dhūmapaḥ ātmānaṃ śambukaṃ nāma śūdraṃ surapadārthinam  Ragh tapasy anadhikāritvāt prajānāṃ tam aghāvaham śīrṣacchedyaṃ paricchidya niyantā śastram ādade  Ragh sa tadvaktraṃ himakliṣṭakiñjalkam iva paṅkajam jyotiṣkaṇāhataśmaśru kaṇṭhanālād apāharat  Ragh kṛtaṇḍaḥ svayam rājñā lebhe śūdraḥ satāṃ gatim tapasā duścareṇāpi na svamārgavilaṅghinā  Ragh raghunātho py agastyena mārgasaṃdarśitātmanā mahaujasā saṃyuyuje śaratkāla ivendunā  Ragh kumbhayonir alaṃkāraṃ tasmai divyaparigraham dadau dattaṃ samudreṇa pītenevātmaniṣkrayam  Ragh taṃ dadhan maithilīkaṇṭhanirvyāpāreṇa bāhunā paścān nivavṛte rāmaḥ prāk parāsur dvijātmajaḥ  Ragh tasya pūrvoditāṃ nindāṃ dvijaḥ putrasamāgataḥ stutyā nivartayām āsa trātur vaivasvatād api  Ragh tam adhvarāya muktāśvaṃ rakṣaḥkapinareśvarāḥ meghāḥ sasyam ivāmbhobhir abhyavarṣann upāyanaiḥ  Ragh digbhyo nimantritāś cainam abhijagmur maharṣayaḥ na bhaumāny eva dhiṣṇyāni hitvā jyotirmayāny api  Ragh upaśalyaniviṣṭais taiś caturdvāramukhī babhau ayodhyā sṛṣṭalokeva sadyaḥ paitāmahī tanuḥ  Ragh ślāghyas tyāgo pi vaidehyāḥ patyuḥ prāgvaṃśavāsinaḥ ananyahāneḥ tasyāsīt saiva jāyā hiraṇmayī  Ragh vidher adhikasaṃbhāras tataḥ pravavṛte makhaḥ āsan yatra kriyāvighnā rākṣasā eva rakṣiṇaḥ  Ragh atha prācetasopajñaṃ rāmāyaṇam itas tataḥ maithileyau kuśalavau jagatur gurucoditau  Ragh vṛttaṃ rāmasya vālmīkeḥ kṛtis tau kiṃnarasvanau kiṃ tad yena mano hartum alaṃ syātāṃ na śṛṇvatām  Ragh rūpe gīte ca mādhuryam tayos tajjñair niveditam dadarśa sānujo rāmaḥ śuśrāva ca kutūhalī  Ragh tadgītaśravaṇaikāgrā saṃsad aśrumukhī babhau himanisyandinī prātar nivāgteva vanasthalī  Ragh vayoveṣavisaṃvādi rāmasya ca tayoś ca sā janatā prekṣya sādṛśyaṃ nākśikampaṃ vyatiṣṭhata  Ragh ubhayor na tathā lokaḥ prāvīṇyena visiṣmiye nṛpateḥ prītidāneṣu vītaspṛhatayā yathā  Ragh geye kena vinītau vāṃ kasya ceyaṃ kaveḥ kṛtiḥ iti rājñā svayaṃ pṛṣṭau tau vālmīkim aśaṃsatām  Ragh atha sāvarajo rāmaḥ prācetasam upeyivān urikrtyātmano dehaṃ rājyam asmai nyavedayat  Ragh sa tāv ākhyāya rāmāya maithileyau tad ātmajau kaviḥ kāruṇiko vavre sītāyāḥ saṃparigraham  Ragh tāta śuddhā samakṣaṃ naḥ snuṣā te jātavedasi daurātmyād rakṣasas tāṃ tu nātratyāḥ śraddadhuḥ prajāḥ  Ragh tāḥ svacāritram uddiśya pratyāyayatu maithilī tataḥ putravatīm enāṃ pratipatsye tadājñayā  Ragh iti pratiśrute rājñā jānakīm āsramān muniḥ śiṣyair ānāyayām āsa svasiddhiṃ niyamair iva  Ragh anyedyur atha kākutsthaḥ saṃnipātya puraukasaḥ kavim āhvāyayām āsa prastutapratipattaye  Ragh svarasaṃskāravatyeva putrābhyāṃ saha sītayā ṛcevodarciṣaṃ sūryaṃ rāmaṃ munir upasthitaḥ  Ragh kāṣāyaparivītena svapadārpitacakṣuṣā kavim āhvāyayām āsa śāntena vapuṣaiva sā  Ragh janās tadālokapathāt pratisaṃhṛtacakṣuṣaḥ tasthus te vāṅmukhāḥ sarve phalitā iva sālayaḥ  Ragh tāṃ dṛṣṭiviṣaye bhartur munir āsthitaviṣṭaraḥ kuru niḥsaṃśayaṃ vatse svavṛtte lokam ity aśāt  Ragh atha vālmīkśiṣyeṇa puṇyam āvarjitaṃ payaḥ ācamyodīrayām āsa sītā satyāṃ sarasvatīm  Ragh vāṅmanaḥkarmabhiḥ patyau vyabhicāro yathā na me tathā viśvaṃbhare devi mām antardhātum arhasi  Ragh evam ukte tayā sādhvyā randhrāt sadyobhavād bhuvaḥ śātahradam iva jyotiḥ prabhāmaṇḍalam udyayau  Ragh tatra nāgaphaṇotkṣiptasiṃhāsananiṣeduṣī samudraraśanā sākṣāt prādurāsīd vasuṃdharā  Ragh sā sītām aṅkam āropya bhartari prahitekṣaṇām mā meti vyāharaty eva tasmin pātālam abhyagāt  Ragh dharāyāṃ tasya saṃrambhaṃ sītāpratyarpaṇaiṣiṇaiḥ gurur vidhibalāpekṣī śamayāṃ āsa dhanvinaḥ  Ragh ṛṣīn visṛjya yajñānte suhṛdaś ca puraskṛtān rāmaḥ sītāgataṃ snehaṃ nidadhe tadapatyayoḥ  Ragh yudhājitas tu saṃdeśāt sa deśa sindhunāmakam dadau dattaprabhāvāya bharatāya dhṛtaprajaḥ  Ragh bharatas tatra gandharvān yudhi nijitya kevalam ātodyaṃ grāhayām āsa samatyājayad āyudham  Ragh sa takṣapuṣkalau putrau rājadhānyos tadākhyayoḥ abhiṣicyābhiṣekārhau rāmāntikam agāt punaḥ  Ragh aṅgadaṃ candraketuṃ ca lakṣmaṇo py ātmasaṃbhavau śāsanād raghunāthasya cakre kārāpatheśāvarau  Ragh ity āropitaputrās te jananīnāṃ janeśvarāḥ bhartṛlokaprapannānāṃ nivāpān vidadhuḥ kramāt  Ragh upetya muniveṣo tha kālaḥ provāca rāghavam rahaḥsaṃvādinau pāsyed āvāṃ yas taṃ tyajer iti  Ragh tatheti pratipannāya vivṛtātmā nṛpāya saḥ ācakhyau divam adhyāsva śāsanāt parameṣṭhinaḥ  Ragh vidvān api tayor dvāḥstahaḥ samayaṃ lakṣmaṇo bhinat bhīto durvāsasaḥ śāpād rāmasaṃdarśanārthinaḥ  Ragh sa gatvā sarayūtīraṃ dehatyāgena yogavit cakāra vitathāṃ bhrātuḥ pratijñāṃ pūrvajanmanaḥ  Ragh tasminn ātmacaturbhāge prāṅ nākam adhitasthuṣi rāghavaḥ śithilaṃ tasthau bhuvi dharmas tripād iva  Ragh sa niveśya kuśāvatyāṃ ripunāgāṅkuṣaṃ kuśam śarāvatyāṃ satāṃ sūktair janitāśrulavaṃ lavam  Ragh udak pratasthe sthiradhīḥ sānujo gnipuraḥsaraḥ anvitaḥ pativātsalyād gṛhavarjam ayodhyayā  Ragh jagṛhus tasya cittajñāḥ padavīṃ harirākṣasāḥ kadambamukulasthūlair abhivṛṣṭaṃ prajāśrubhiḥ  Ragh upasthitavimānena tena bhaktānukampinā cakre tridivaniḥṣreṇiḥ sarayūr anuyāyinām  Ragh yad gopratarakalpo bhut saṃmardas tatra majjatām atas tadākhyayā tīrthaṃ pāvanaṃ bhuvi paprathe  Ragh sa vibhur vibudhāṃśeṣu pratipannātmamūrtiṣu tridaśībhūtapaurāṇāṃ svargāntaram akalpayat  Ragh nirvartyaivaṃ daśamukhaśiraśchedakāryaṃ surāṇāṃ viṣvaksenaḥ svatanum aviśat sarvalokapratiṣṭhām laṅkānāthaṃ pavanatanayaṃ cobhayaṃ sthāpayitvā kīrtistambhadvayam iva girau dakṣiṇe cottare ca  Ragh athetare sapta raghupravīrā jyeṣṭhaṃ purojanmatayā juṇaiś ca cakruḥ kuśaṃ ratnaviśeṣabhājaṃ saubhrātram eṣāṃ hi kulānusāri  Ragh te setuvārttāgajabandhamukhyair abhyucchritāḥ karmabhir apy avandhyaiḥ anyonyadeśapravibhāgasīmāṃ velāṃ samudrā iva na vyatīyuḥ  Ragh caturbhujāṃśaprabhavaḥ sa teṣāṃ dānapravṛtter anupāratānām suradvipānām iva sāmayonir bhinno ṣṭhadā viprasasāra vaṃśaḥ  Ragh athārdharātre stimitapradīpe śayyāgṛhe suptajane prabuddhaḥ kuśaḥ pravāsasthakalatraveṣām adṛṣṭapūrvāṃ vanitām apaśyat  Ragh sā sādhusādhāraṇapārthivarddheḥ sthitvā purastāt puruhūtabhāsaḥ jetuḥ pareṣāṃ jayaśabdapūrvaṃ tasyāñjaliṃ bandhumato babandha  Ragh athānupoḍhārgalam apy agāraṃ chāyām ivādarśatalaṃ praviṣṭām savismayo dāśarathes tanūjaḥ provāca pūrvārdhaviṣṛṭatalpaḥ  Ragh labhdāntarā sāvaraṇe pi gehe yogaprabhāvo na ca lakṣyate te bibharṣi cākāram anirvṛtānāṃ mṛṇālinī haimam ivoparāgam  Ragh kā tvaṃ śubhe kasya parigraho vā kiṃ vā madabhyāgamakāraṇaṃ te ācakṣva matvā vaśināṃ raghūṇāṃ manaḥ parastrīvimukhapravṛtti  Ragh tam abravīt sā guruṇā navadyā yā nītapaurā svapadonmukhena tasyāḥ puraḥ saṃprati vītanāthāṃ jānīhi rājann adhidevatāṃ mām  Ragh vasaukasārām abhibhūya sāhaṃ saurājyabaddhotsavayā vibhūtyā samagraśaktau tvayi sūryavaṃṣye sati prapannā karuṇām avasthām  Ragh viśīrṇatalpāṭṭaśato niveśaḥ paryastaśālaḥ prabhuṇā vinā me viḍambayaty astanimagnasūryaṃ dināntam ugrānilabhinnamegham  Ragh niśāsu bhāsvatkalanūpurāṇāṃ yaḥ saṃcaro bhūd abhisārikāṇām nadanmukholkāvicitāmiṣābhiḥ sa vāhyate rājapathaḥ śivābhiḥ  Ragh āsphālitaṃ yat pramadākarāgrair mṛdaṅgadhīradhvanim anvagacchat vanyair idānīṃ mahiṣais tad ambhaḥ śṛṅgāhataṃ krośati dīrghikāṇām  Ragh citradvipāḥ padmavanāvatīrṇāḥ kareṇubhir dattamṛṇālabhaṅgāḥ nakhāṅkuśāghātavibhinnakumbhāḥ saṃrabdhasiṃhaprahṛtaṃ vahanti  Ragh stambheṣu yoṣitpratiyātanānām utkrāntavarṇakramadhūsarāṇām stanottarīyāṇi bhavanti saṅgān nirmokapaṭṭāḥ phaṇibhir vimuktāḥ  Ragh kālāntaraśyāmasudheṣu naktam itas tato rūḍhatṛṇāṅkureṣu ta eva muktāguṇaśuddhayo pi harmyeṣu mūrchanti na candrapādāḥ  Ragh āvarjya śākhāḥ sadayaṃ ca yāsāṃ puṣpāṇy upāttāni vilāsinībhiḥ vanyaiḥ pulindair iva vānarais tāḥ kliśyanta udyānalatā madīyāḥ  Ragh rātrāv anāviṣkṛtadīpabhāsaḥ kāntāmukhaśrīviyutā divāpi tiraskriyante kṛmitantujālair vicchinnadhūmaprasarā gavākṣāḥ  Ragh balikriyāvarjitasaikatāni snānīyasaṃsargam anāpanuvanti upāntavānīragṛhāṇi dṛṣṭvā śūnyāni dūye sarayūjalāni  Ragh tad arhasīmāṃ vasatiṃ visṛjya mām abhyupaituṃ kularājadhānīm hitvā tanuṃ kāraṇamānuṣīṃ tāṃ yathā gurus te paramātmamūrtim  Ragh tatheti tasyāḥ praṇayaṃ pratītaḥ pratyagrahīt prāgraharo raghūṇām pūr apy abhivyaktamukhaprasādā śarīrabandhena tirobabhūva  Ragh tad adbhutaṃ saṃsadi rārtrivṛttaṃ prātar dvijebhyo nṛpatiḥ śaśaṃsa śrutvā ta enaṃ kularājadhānyā sākṣāt patitve vṛtam abhayanandan  Ragh kuśāvatīṃ śrotriyasāt sa kṛtvā yātrānukūle hani sāvarodhaḥ anudruto vāyur ivābhravṛndaiḥ sainyair ayodhyābhimukhaḥ pratasthe  Ragh sā ketumālopavanā bṛhadbhir vihāraśailānugateva nāgaiḥ senā rathodāragṛhā prayāṇe tasyābhavaj jaṅgamarājadhānī  Ragh tenātapatrāmalamaṇḍalena prasthāpitaḥ pūrvanivāsabhūmim babhau balaughaḥ śaśinoditena velām udanvān iva nīyamānaḥ  Ragh tasya prayātasya varūthinīnāṃ pīḍām aparyāptavatīva soḍhum vasuṃdharā viṣṇupadaṃ dvitīyam adhyāruroheva rajaśchalena  Ragh udyacchamānā gamanāya paścāt puro niveśe pathi ca vrajantī sā yatra senā dadṛṣe nṛpasya tatraiva sāmagryamatiṃ cakāra  Ragh tasya dvipānāṃ madavārisekāt khurābhighātāc ca turaṃgamāṇām reṇuḥ prapede pathi paṅkabhāvaṃ paṅko pi reṇutvam iyāya netuḥ  Ragh mārgaiṣiṇī sā kaṭakāntareṣu vaindhyeṣu senā bahudhā vibhinnā cakāra reveva mahāvirāvā baddhapratiśrunti guhāmukhāni  Ragh sa dhātubhedāruṇayānanemiḥ prabhuḥ prayāṇadhvanimiśratūryaḥ vyalaṅghayad vindhyam upāyanāni paśyan pulindair upapāditāni  Ragh tīrthe tadīye gajasetubandhāt pratīpagām uttarato sya gaṅgām ayatnavālagvyajanībabhūvur haṃsā nabholaṅghanalolakpakṣāḥ  Ragh sa pūrvajānāṃ kapilena roṣād bhasmāvaśeṣīkṛtavigrahāṇām surālayaprāptinimittam ambhas traisrotasaṃ naululitaṃ vavande  Ragh ity adhvanaḥ kaiścid ahobhir ante kūlaṃ samāsādya kuśaḥ sarayvāḥ vedipratiṣṭhān vitatādhvarāṇāṃ yūpān apaśyac chataśo raghūṇām  Ragh ādhūya śākhāḥ kusumadrumāṇāṃ spṛṣṭvā ca śītān sarayūtaraṅgān taṃ klāntasainyaṃ kularājadhānyāḥ pratyujjagāmopavanāntavāyuḥ  Ragh athopaśalye ripumagnaśalyas tasyāḥ puraḥ paursakhaḥ sa rājā kuladhvajas tāni caladhvajāni niveśayām āsa balī balāni  Ragh tāṃ śilpisaṃghāḥ prabhuṇā niyuktās tathāgatāṃ saṃbhṛtasādhanatvāt puraṃ navīcakrur apāṃ visargān meghā nidāghaglapitām ivorvīm  Ragh tataḥ saparyāṃ sapaśūpahārāṃ puraḥ parārdhyapratimāgṛhāyāḥ upoṣitair vāstuvidhānavidbhir nirvartayām āsa raghupavīraḥ  Ragh tasyāḥ sa rājopapadaṃ niśāntaṃ kāmīva kāntāhṛdayaṃ praviśya yathārham anyair anujīvilokaṃ saṃbhāvayām āsa gṛhais tadīyaiḥ  Ragh sā mandurāsaṃśrayibhis turaṃgaiḥ śālāvidhistambhagataiś ca nāgaiḥ pūr ābabhāse vipaṇisthapaṇyā sarvāṅganaddhābharaṇeva nārī  Ragh vasan sa tasyāṃ vasatau raghūṇāṃ purāṇaśobhām adhiropitāyām na maithileyaḥ spṛhayāṃ babhūva bhartre divo nāpy alakeśvarāya  Ragh athāsya ratnagrathitottarīyam ekāntapāṇḍustanalambihāram niḥśvāsahāryāṃśukam ājagāma gharmaḥ priyā veṣam ivopadeṣṭum  Ragh agastyacihnād ayanāt samīpaṃ dig uttarā bhāsvati saṃnivṛtte ānandaśītam iva bhāṣpavṛṣṭiṃ himasrutiṃ haimavatīṃ sasarja  Ragh pravṛddhatāpo divaso timātram atyartham eva kṣaṇadā ca tanvī ubhau virodhakriyayā vibhinnau jāyāpatī sānuśayāv ivāstām  Ragh dine dine śaivalavanty adhastāt sopānaparvāṇi vimuñcad ambhaḥ uddaṇḍapadmaṃ gṛhadīrghikāṇāṃ nārīnitambadvayasaṃ babhūva  Ragh vaneṣu sāyanatanamallikānāṃ vijṛmbhaṇodgandhiṣu kuḍ maleṣu pratyekanikṣiptapadaḥ saśabdaṃ saṃkhyām ivaiṣāṃ bhramaraś cakāra  Ragh svedānuviddhārdranakhakṣatāṅke saṃdaṣṭabhūyiṣṭhaśikhaṃ kapole cyutaṃ na karṇād api kāminīnāṃ śirīṣapuṣpaṃ sahasā papāta  Ragh yantrapravāhaiḥ śiśiraiḥ parītān rasena dhautān malayodbhavasya śilāviśeṣān adhiśayya ninyur dhārāgṛheṣv ātapam ṛddhimantaḥ  Ragh snānārdramukteṣv anudhūpavāsaṃ vinyastasāyantanamallikeṣu kāmo vasantātyayamandavīryaḥ keśeṣu lebhe balam aṅganānām  Ragh āpiñjarā baddharajaḥkaṇatvān mañjary udārāśuśubhe rjunasya dagdhvāpi dehaṃ giriśena roṣāt khaṇḍīkṛtā jyeva manobhvasya  Ragh manojñagandhaṃ sahakārabhaṅgaṃ purāṇasīdhuṃ navapāṭalaṃ ca saṃbadhnatā kāijaneṣu doṣāḥ sarve nidāghāvadhinā pramṛṣṭāḥ  Ragh janasya tasmin samaye vigāḍhe babhūvatur dvau saviśeṣakāntau tāpāpanodakṣamapāda sa codayastho nṛpatiḥ śaśī ca  Ragh athormilolonmadarājahaṃse rodholatāpuṣpavahe sarayvāḥ vihartum icchā vanitāsakhasya tasyāmbhasi grīṣmasukhe babhūva  Ragh sa tīrabhūmau vihitopakāryām ānāyibhis tām apakṛṣṭanakrām vigāhituṃ śrīmahimānurūpaṃ pracakrame cakradharaprabhāvaḥ  Ragh sā tīrasopānapathāvatārād anyonyakeyūravighaṭṭinībhiḥ sanūpurakṣobhapadābhir āsīd udvignahaṃsā sarid aṅganābhiḥ  Ragh parasparābhyukṣaṇatatparāṇāṃ tāsāṃ nṛpo majjanarāgadarśī nausaṃśrayaḥ pārśvagatāṃ kirātīm upāttavālavyajanāṃ babhāṣe  Ragh paśyāvarodhaiḥ śataśo madīyair vigāhyamāno galitāṅgarāgaiḥ saṃdhyodayaḥ sābhra ivaiṣa varṇaṃ puṣyaty anekaṃ sarayūpravāhaḥ  Ragh viluptam antaḥpurasundarīṇāṃ yad añjanaṃ naululitābhir adbhiḥ tad badhnatībhir madarāgaśobhāṃ vilocaneṣu pratimuktam āsām  Ragh etā guruśroṇipayodharatvād ātmānam udvohuḍhum aśaknuvantyaḥ gāḍhāṅgadair bāhubhir aspu bālāḥ kleśottaraṃ rāgavaśāt plavante  Ragh amī śirīṣaprasavāvataṃsāḥ prabhraṃśino vārivihāriṇīnām pāriplavāḥ srotasi nimnagāyāḥ śaivālalolāṃś chalayanti mīnān  Ragh āsāṃ jalāsphālanatatparāṇāṃ muktāphalaspardhiṣu śīkareṣu payodharotsarpiṣu śīryamāṇāḥ saṃlakṣyate na cchiduro pi hāraḥ  Ragh āvartaśobhā natanābhikānter bhaṅgyo bhruvāṃ dvandvacarāḥstanānām jātāni rūpāvayavopamānāny adūravartīni vilāsinīnām  Ragh tīrasthalībarhibhir utkalāpaiḥ prasnigdhakekair abhinandyamānam śrotreṣu saṃmūrchati raktam āsāṃ gītānugaṃ vārimṛdaṅgavādyam  Ragh saṃdaṣṭavastreṣv abalānitambeṣv induprakāśāntaritoḍukalpāḥ amī jalāpūritasūtramārgā maunaṃ bhajante raśanākalāpāḥ  Ragh etāḥ karotpīḍitavāridhārā darpāt sakhībhir vadaneṣu siktāḥ vakretarāgrair alakais taruṇyaś cūrṇāruṇān vārilavān vamanti  Ragh udbaddhakeśaś cyutapattrarekho viśleṣimuktāphalapattraveṣṭaḥ manojña eva pramadāmukhānām ambhovihārākulito pi veṣaḥ  Ragh sa nauvimānād avatīrya reme vilolahāraḥ saha tābhir apsu skandhāvalagnoddhṛtapadminīkaḥ kareṇubhir vanya iva dvipendraḥ  Ragh tato nṛpenānugatāḥ striyas tā bhrājiṣṇunā sātiśayaṃ virejuḥ prāg eva muktā nayanābhirāmāḥ prāpyendranīlaṃ kim utonmayūkham  Ragh varṇodakaiḥ kāñcanaśṛṅgamuktais tam āyatākṣyaḥ praṇayād asiñcan tathāgataḥ so tirarāṃ babhāse sadhātunisyanda ivādrirājaḥ  Ragh tenāvarodhapramadāsakhena vigāhanānena saridvarāṃ tām ākāśagaṅgāratir apsarobhir vṛto marutvān anuyātalīlaḥ  Ragh yat kumbhayoner adigamya rāmaḥ kuśāya rājyena samaṃ dideśa tad asya jaitrābharaṇaṃ vihartur ajñātapātaṃ salile mamajja  Ragh snātvā yathākāmam asau sadāras tīropakāryāṃ gatamātra eva divyena śūnyaṃ valayena bāhum upoḍhanepathyavidhir dadarśa  Ragh jayaśriyaḥ saṃvananaṃ yatas tad āmuktapūrvaṃ guruṇā ca yasmāt sehe sya na bhraṃśam ato na lobhāt sa tulyapuṣpābharaṇo hi dhīraḥ  Ragh tataḥ samājñāpayad āśu sarvān ānāyinas tadvicaye nadīṣṇān vandhyaśramās te sarayūṃ vigāhya tam ūcur āmlānamukhaprasādāḥ  Ragh kṛtaḥ prayatno na ca deva labdhaṃ magnaṃ payasy ābharaṇottamaṃ te nāgena laulyāt kumudena nūnam upāttam antarhradavāsinā tat  Ragh tataḥ sa kṛtvā dhanur ātatajyaṃ dhanurdharaḥ kopavilohitākṣaḥ gārutmataṃ tīragatas tarasvī bhujaṃganāśāya samādade stram  Ragh tasmin hradaḥ saṃhitamātra eva kṣobhāt samāviddhataraṅgahastaḥ rodhāṃsy abhighnann avapātamagnaḥ karīva vanyaḥ paruṣaṃ rarāsa  Ragh tasmāt samudrād iva mathyamānād udvṛttanakrāt sahasonmamajja lakṣmyeva sārdhaṃ surarājavṛkṣaḥ kanyāṃ puraskṛtya bhujaṃgarājaḥ  Ragh vibhūṣaṇapratyupahārahastam upasthitaṃ vīkṣya viśāṃpatis tam sauparṇam astraṃ pratisaṃjahāra praheṣv anirbandharuṣo hi santaḥ  Ragh trailokyanāthaprabhavaṃ prabhāvāt kuśaṃ dviṣām aṅkuśam astravidvān mānonantenāpy abhivandya mūrdhnā mūrdhābhiṣiktaṃ kumudo babhāṣe  Ragh avaimi kāryāntaramānuṣasya viṣṇoḥ sutākhyām aparāṃ tanuṃ tvām so haṃ kathaṃ nāma tavācareyam ārādhanīyasya dhṛter vibhātam  Ragh karābhighātotthitakandukeyam ālokya bālātikutūhalena javāt pataj jyotir ivāntarikṣād ādatta jatrābharaṇaṃ tvadīyam  Ragh tad etad ājānuvilambinā te jyāghātarekhākiṇa lāñchanena bhujena rakṣāparigheṇa bhūmer upaitu yogaṃ punar aṃsalena  Ragh imāṃ svasāraṃ ca yavīyasīṃ me kumudvatīṃ nārhasi nānumantum ātmāparādhaṃ nudatīṃ cirāya śuśrūṣayā pārthiva pādayos te  Ragh ity ūcivān upahṛtābharaṇaḥ kṣitīśaṃ ślāghyo bhavān svajana ity anubhāṣitāram saṃyojayāṃ vidhivad āsa sametabandhuḥ kanyāmayena kumudaḥ kulabhūṣaṇena  Ragh tasyāḥ spṛṣṭe manujapatinā sāhacaryāya haste māṅgalyorṇāvalayini puraḥ pāvakasyocchikhasya divyas tūryadhvanir udacarad vyaśnuvāno digantān gandhodagraṃ tadanau vavṛṣuḥ puṣpam āścaryameghāḥ  Ragh itthaṃ nāgas tribhuvanaguror aurasaṃ maithileyaṃ labdhvā bandhuṃ tam api ca kuśaḥ pañcamaṃ takṣakasya ekaḥ śaṅkāṃ pitṛvadharipor atyajad vainateyāc chāntavyālām avanim aparaḥ paurakāntaḥ śaśāsa  Ragh aithiṃ nāma kākutsthāt putraṃ āpakumudvatī paścimād yāminīyāmāt prasādam iva cetanā  Ragh sa pituḥ pitṛmān vaṃśaṃ putraṃ āpakumudvatī apunāt savitevobhau mārgāv uttaradakṣiṇau  Ragh tam ādau kulavidyānām artham arthavidāṃ varaḥ paścāt pārthivakanyānāṃ pāṇim agrāhayat pitā  Ragh jātyas tenābhijātena śūraḥ śauryavatā kuśaḥ amanyataikam ātmānam anekaṃ vaśinā vaśī  Ragh sa kulocitam indrasya sāhāyakam upeyivān jaghāna samare daityaṃ durjayaṃ tena so vadhi  Ragh taṃ svasā nāgarājasya kumudasya kumudvatī anvagāt kumudānandaṃ śaśāṅkam iva kaumudī  Ragh tayor divaspater āsīd ekaḥ siṃhāsanārdhabāk dvitīyāpi sakhī śacyāḥ pārijātāṃśabhāginī  Ragh tadātmasaṃbhavaṃ rājye mantrivṛddāḥ samādadhuḥ smarantaḥ paścimām ājñāṃ bhartuḥ saṃgrāmayāyinaḥ  Ragh te tasya kalpayām āsur abhiṣekāya śilpibhiḥ vimānaṃ navam udvedi catuḥstambhapratiṣṭam  Ragh tatrainaṃ hemakumbheṣu saṃbhṛtais tīrthavāribhiḥ upatasthuḥ prakṛtayo bhadrapīṭhopaveśitam  Ragh nadadhbiḥ snigdhagambhīraṃ tūryair āhatapuṣkaraiḥ anvamīyata kalyāṇaṃ tasyāvicchinnasaṃtati  Ragh dūrvāyavāṅkuraplakṣatvagabhinnapuṭottarān jñātivṛddhaiḥ prayuktān sa bheje nīrājanāvidhīn  Ragh purohitapurogās taṃ jiṣṇuṃ jaitrair atharvabhiḥ upacakramire pūrvam abhiṣektuṃ dvijātayaḥ  Ragh tasyaughamahatī mūrdhni nipatantī vyarocata saśabdam abhiṣekaśrīr gaṅgeva tripuradviṣaḥ  Ragh stūyamānaḥ kṣaṇe tasminn alakṣyata sa bandibhiḥ pravṛddha iva prajanyaḥ cātakair abhinanditaḥ  Ragh tasya san mantrapūtābhiḥ snānam adbhiḥ pratīcchataḥ vavṛdhe vaidyutasyāgner vṛṣṭisekād iva dyutiḥ  Ragh sa tāvad abhiṣekānte snātakebhyo dadau vasu yāvat teṣāṃ samāpyeran yajñāḥ paryāptadakṣiṇāḥ  Ragh te prītamanasas tasmai yām āśiṣam udīrayan sā tasya karmanirvṛttair dūraṃ paścātkṛtā phalaiḥ  Ragh bandhacchedaṃ sa baddhānāṃ vadhārhāṇām avadhyatām dhuryāṇāṃ ca dhuro mokṣam adohaṃ cādiṣad gavām  Ragh krīḍāpatatriṇo py asya pañjarasthāḥ śukādayaḥ labdhamokṣās tadādeśād yatheṣṭagatayo bhavan  Ragh tataḥ kakṣāntaranyastaṃ gajadantāsanaṃ śuci sottaracchadam adhyāsta nepathyagrahaṇāya saḥ  Ragh taṃ dhūpāśyānakeśāntaṃ toyanirṇiktapāṇayaḥ ākalpasādhanais tais tair upaseduḥ prasādhakāḥ  Ragh te sya muktāguṇonnaddhaṃ maulim antargatasrajam pratyūpuḥ padmarāgeṇa prabhāmaṇḍalaśobhinā  Ragh candanenāṅgarāgaṃ ca mṛganābhisugandhinā samāpayya tataś cakruḥ pattraṃ vinyastarocanam  Ragh āmuktābharaṇaḥ sragvī haṃsacihnadukūlavān āsīd atiśayaprekṣyaḥ sa rājyaśrīvadhūvaraḥ  Ragh nepathyadarśinaś chāyā tasyādarśe hiraṇmaye virarājodite sūrye merau kalpataror iva  Ragh sa rājakakudavyagrapāṇibhiḥ pārśvavaribhiḥ yayāv udīritālokaḥ sudharmānavamāṃ sabhām  Ragh vitānasahitaṃ tatra bheje paitṛkam āsanam cūḍāmaṇibhir udghṛṣṭapādapīṭhaṃ mahīkṣitām  Ragh śuśubhe tena cākrāntaṃ maṅgalāyatanaṃ mahat śrīvatsalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣaḥ kaustubheneva kaiśavam  Ragh babhau bhūyaḥ kumāratvād ādhirājyam avāpya saḥ rekhā bhāvād upārūḍhaḥ sāmagryam iva candramāḥ  Ragh prasannamukharāgaṃ taṃ smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇam mūrtimantam amanyanta viśvāsam anujīvinaḥ  Ragh sa puraṃ puruhūtaśrīḥ kalpadrumanibhadhvajām kramamāṇaś cakāra dyāṃ nāgenairāvataujasā  Ragh tasyaikasyocchritaṃ chattraṃ mūrdhni tenāmalatviṣā pūrvarājaviyogauṣmyaṃ kṛtsnasya jagato hṛtam  Ragh dhūmād agneḥ śikhāḥ paścād udayād aṃśavo raveḥ so tītya tejasāṃ vṛttiṃ samam evotthito guṇaiḥ  Ragh taṃ prītiviśadair netrair anvayuḥ paurayoṣitaḥ śaratprasannair jyotirbhir vibhāvarya iva dhruvam  Ragh ayodhyādevatāś cainaṃ praśastāyatanārcitāḥ anudadhyur anudhyeyaṃ sāṃnidhyaiḥ pratimāgataiḥ  Ragh yāvan nāśyāyate vedir abhiṣekajalāplutā tāvad evāsya velāntaṃ pratāpaḥ prāpa duḥsahaḥ  Ragh vasiṣṭhasya guror mantrāḥ sāyakās tasya dhanvinaḥ kiṃ tat sādhyaṃ yad ubhaye sādhayeyur na saṃgatāḥ  Ragh sa dharmasthasakhaḥ śaśvad arthipratyarthināṃ svayam dadarśa saṃśayacchedyān vyavahārān atandritaḥ  Ragh tataḥ param abhivyaktāsaumanasyaniveditaiḥ yuyoja pākābhimukhair bhṛtyān vijñāpanāphalaiḥ  Ragh prajās tadguruṇā nadyo nabhaseva vivardhitāḥ tasmiṃs tu bhūyasīṃ vṛddhiṃ nabhasye tā ivāyayuḥ  Ragh yad uvāca na tan mithyā yad dadau na jahāra tat so bhūd bhagnavrataḥ śatrūn uddhṛtya pratiropayan  Ragh vayorūpavibhūtīnām ekaikaṃ madakāraṇam tāni tasmin samastāni na tasyotsiṣice manaḥ  Ragh itthaṃ janitarāgāsu prakṛtiṣv anuvāsaram akṣobhyaḥ sa navo py āsīd dṛḍhamūla iva drumaḥ  Ragh anityāḥ śatravo bāhyā viprakṛṣṭāś ca te yataḥ ataḥ so bhyantarān nityān ṣaṭ pūrvam ajayad ripūn  Ragh prasādābhimukhe tasmiṃś capalāpi svabhāvataḥ nikaṣe hemarekheva śrīr āsīd anapāyinī  Ragh kātaryaṃ kevalā nītiḥ śauryaṃ śvāpadaceṣṭitam ataḥ siddhiṃ sametābhyām ubhābhyām anviyeṣa saḥ  Ragh na tasya maṇḍale rājño nyastapraṇidhidīdhiteḥ adṛṣṭam abhavat kiṃcid vyabhrasyeva vivasvataḥ  Ragh rātriṃdivavibhāgeṣu yad ādiṣṭaṃ mahīkṣitām tat siṣeve niyogena sa vikalpaparāṅmukhaḥ  Ragh mantraḥ pratidinaṃ tasya babhūva saha mantribhiḥ sa jātu sevyamāno pi guptadvāro na sūcyate  Ragh pareṣu sveṣu ca kṣiptair avijñātaparasparaiḥ so pasarpair jajāgāra yathākālaṃ svapann api  Ragh durgāṇi durgrhāṇy āsaṃs tasya roddhur api dviṣām na hi siṃho gajāskandī bhayād giriguhāśayaḥ  Ragh bahvyamukhyāḥ samārambhāḥ pratyavekṣyā niratyayāḥ garbhaśālisadharmāṇas tasya gūḍhaṃ vipecire  Ragh apathena pravavṛte na jātūpacito pi saḥ vṛddhau nadīmukhenaiva prasthānaṃ lavaṇāmbhasaḥ  Ragh kāmaṃ pratkṛtivairāgyaṃ sadyaḥ śamayituṃ kṣamaḥ yasya kāryaḥ pratīkāraḥ sa tan naivodapādayat  Ragh śakeṣv evābhavad yātrā tasya śaktimataḥ sataḥ samīraṇasahāyo pi nāmbhaḥprārthī davānalaḥ  Ragh na dharmam arthakāmābhyāṃ babādhe na ca tena tau nārthaṃ kāmena kāmaṃ vā so rthena sadṛśas triṣu  Ragh hīnāny anupakartḥṇi pravṛddhāni vikurvate tena madhyamaśaktīni mitrāṇi shtāpitāny ataḥ  Ragh parātmanoḥ paricchidya śaktyādīnāṃ balābalam yayāv ebhir baliṣṭhaś cet parasmād āsta so nyathā  Ragh kośenāśrayaṇīyatvam iti tasyārthasaṃgrahaḥ ambugarbho hi jīmūtaś cātakair abhinandyate  Ragh parakarmāpahaḥ so bhūd udyataḥ sveṣu karmasu āvṛṇod ātmano randhraṃ randhreṣu praharan ripūn  Ragh pitrā saṃvardhito nityaṃ kṛtāstraḥ sāṃparāyikaḥ tasya daṇḍavato daṇḍaḥ svadehān na vyaśiṣyata  Ragh sarpasyeva śiroratnaṃ nāsya śaktitrayaṃ paraḥ sa cakarṣa parasmāt tad ayaskānta ivāyasam  Ragh vāpīṣv iva sravantīṣu vaneṣūpavaneṣv iva sārthāḥ svairaṃ svakīyeṣu cerur veśmasv ivādriṣu  Ragh tapo rakṣan sa vighnebhyas taskarebhyaś ca saṃpadaḥ yathāsvam āśramaiś cakre varṇair api ṣaḍsaṃśabhāk  Ragh khanibhiḥ suṣuve ratnaṃ kṣetraiḥ sasyaṃ vanair gajān dideśa vetanaṃ tasmai rakṣāsadṛśam eva bhūḥ  Ragh sa guṇānāṃ balānāṃ ca ṣaṇṇāṃ ṣaṇmukhavikramaḥ babhūva viniyogajñaḥ sādhanīyeṣu vastuṣu  Ragh iti kramāt prayuñjāno rāja nītiṃ caturvidhām ā tīrthād apratīghātaṃ sa tasyāḥ phalam ānaśe  Ragh kūṭayuddhavidhijñe pi tasmin sanmārgayodhini bheje bhisārikāvṛttiṃ jayaśrīr vīragāminī  Ragh prāyaḥ pratāpabhagnatvād arīṇāṃ tasya durlabhaḥ raṇo gandhavipasyeva gandhabhinnānyadantinaḥ  Ragh pravṛddhau hīyate candraḥ samudro pi tathāvidhaḥ sa tu tasamavṛddhiś ca na cābhūt tāv iva kṣayī  Ragh santas tasyābhigamanād atyarthaṃ mahataḥ kṛṣāḥ udadher iva jīmūtāḥ prāpur dātṛtvam arthinaḥ  Ragh stūyamānaḥ sa jihrāya stutyam eva samācaran tathāpi vavṛdhe tasya tatkāridveṣino yaśaḥ  Ragh duritaṃ darśanena ghnaṃs tattvārthena nudaṃs tamaḥ prajāḥ svatantrayāṃ cakre śaśvat sūrya ivoditaḥ  Ragh indor agatayaḥ padme sūryasya kumude ṃśavaḥ guṇās tasya vipakṣe pi guṇino lebhire ntaram  Ragh parābhisaṃdhānaparaṃ yady apy asya viceṣṭitam jigīṣor aśvamedhāya dharmyam eva babhūva tat  Ragh evam udyan prabhāveṇa śāstgranirdiṣṭavartmanā vṛṣeva devo devānāṃ rājñāṃ rājā babhūva saḥ  Ragh pañcamaṃ lokapālānāṃ tam ūcuḥ sāmyayogataḥ bhūtānāṃ mahatām ṣaṣṭham aṣṭamaṃ kulabhūbhṛtām  Ragh dūrāpavarjitacchattrais tasyājñāṃ śāsanārpitām dadhuḥ śirobhir bhūpālā devaḥ pauraṃdarīm iva  Ragh ṛtvijaḥ sa tathānarca dakṣiṇābhir mahākratau yathā sādhāraṇībhūtaṃ nāmāsya dhanadasya ca  Ragh indrād vṛṣṭir niyamitagadodrekavṛttir yamo bhūd yādonāthaḥ śivajalapathaḥ karmaṇe naucarāṇām pūrvāpekṣī tadanu vidadhe kośavṛddhiṃ kuberas tasmin daṇḍopanatacaritaṃ bhejire lokapālāḥ  Ragh sa naiṣadhasyārthapateḥ sutāyām utpādayām āsa niṣiddhaśatruḥ anūnasāraṃ niṣadhān nagendrāt putraṃ yam āhur niṣadhākhyam eva  Ragh tenoruvīryeṇa pitā prajāyai kalpiṣyamāṇena nananda yūnā suvṛṣtiyogād iva jīvalokaḥ sasyena saṃpattiphalātmakena  Ragh śabdādi nirviśya sukhaṃ cirāya tasmin pratiṣṭhāpitarājaśabdaḥ kaumudvateyaḥ kumudāvadātair dyām arjitāṃ karmabhir āruroha  Ragh pautraḥ kuśasyāpi kuśeśayākṣaḥ sasāgarāṃ sāgaradhīracetāḥ ekātapoatrāṃ bhuvam ekavīraḥ purārgalādīrghabhujo bubhoja  Ragh tasyānalaujās tanayas tadante vaṃśaśriyaṃ prāpa nalābhidhānaḥ yo naḍvalānīva gajaḥ pareṣāṃ balāny amṛdnān nalinābhavaktraḥ  Ragh nabhaścarair gītayaśyāmatanuṃ tanūjam nabhastalaśyāmatanuṃ tanūjam khyātaṃ nabhaḥśabdamayena nāmnā kāntaṃ nabhomāsam iva prajānām  Ragh tasmai viṣrjyottarakosalānāṃ dharmottaras tat prabhave prabhutvam mṛgair ajaryaṃ jaraspodaiṣṭam adehabandhāya punar babandha  Ragh tena dvipānām iva puṇḍarīko rājñām ajayyo jani puṇḍarīkaḥ śānte pitary āhṛtapuṇḍarīkā yaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam ivāśritā śrīḥ  Ragh sa kṣemadhanvānam amoghadhanvā putraṃ prajākṣemavidhānadakṣam kṣmāṃ lambhayitvā kṣamayopapannaṃ vane tapaḥ kṣāntataraś cacāra  Ragh anīkinīnāṃ samare grayāyī tasyāpi devapratimaḥ suto bhūt vyaśrūyatānīkapadāvasānaṃ devādi nāma tridive pi yasya  Ragh pitā samārādhanatatpareṇa putreṇa putrī sa yathaiva tena putras tathaivādhikavatsalena sa tena pitrā pitṛmān babhūva  Ragh pūrvas tayor ātmasame ciroḍhām ātmodbhave varṇacatuṣṭayasya dhuraṃ nidhāyaikanidhir guṇānām jagāma yajvā yajamānalokam  Ragh vaśī sutas tasya vaśaṃvadatvāt sveṣām ivāsīd dviṣatām apīṣṭaḥ sakṛd  vivignān api hi prayuktaṃ mādhuryam īṣṭe hariṇān grahītum  Ragh ahīnagur nāma sa gāṃ samagrām ahīnabāhudraviṇaḥ śaśāsa yo hīna saṃsargaparāṅmukhatvād mādhuryam īṣṭe hariṇān grahītum  Ragh guroḥ sa cānantaram antarjñaḥ puṃsāṃ pumān ādya ivāvatīrṇaḥ upakramair askhalitaiś caturbhiś caturdigīśaś caturo babhūva  Ragh tasmin prayāte paralokayātrāṃ jetary arīṇāṃ tanayaṃ tadīyam uccaiḥśirastvāj jitapāriyātraṃ lakṣmīḥ siṣeve kila pāriyātram  Ragh tasyābhavat sūnur udāraśīlaḥ śilaḥ śilāpaṭṭaviśālavakṣāḥ jitāripakṣo pi śilīmukhair yaḥ śālīnatām avrajad īḍyamānaḥ  Ragh tam ātmasaṃpannam aninditātmā kṛtvā yuvānaṃ yuvarājam eva sukhāni so bhuṅkta sukhoparodhi vṛttaṃ hi rājñām uparuddhavṛttam  Ragh taṃ rāgabandhiṣv avitṛptam eva bhogeṣu saubhāgyaviśeṣabhogyam vilāsinīnām aratikṣamāpi jarā vṛthā matsariṇī jahāra  Ragh unnābha ity udagtasnāmadheyas tasyāyathārthonnatanābhhirandhraḥ suto bhavat paṅkajanābhakalpaḥ kṛtsnasya nābhir nṛpamaṇḍalasya  Ragh tataḥ paraṃ vajradharaprabhāvas tadātmajaḥ saṃyati vajraghoṣaḥ babhūva vajrākarabhuṣaṇāyāḥ patiḥ pṛthivyāḥ kila vajranābhaḥ  Ragh tasmin gate dyāṃ sukṛtopalabdhāṃ tatsaṃbhavaṃ śaṅkhaṇam arṇavāntā utkhātaśatruṃ vasudhopatasthe ratnopahārair uditaiḥ khanibhyaḥ  Ragh tasyāvasāne haridaśvadhāmā pitryaṃ prapede padam aśvirūpaḥ velātaṭeṣūṣitasainikāśvaṃ purāvido yaṃ dhyuṣitāśvam āhuḥ  Ragh ārādhya viśveśvaram īśvareṇa tena kṣiter viśvasaho dhijajñe pātuṃ saho viśvasakhaḥ samagrāṃ viśvaṃbharām ātmajamūrtir ātmā  Ragh aṃśe hiraṇyākśaripoḥ sa jāte hiraṇyanābhe tanaye nayajñaḥ dviṣām asahyaḥ sutarāṃ tarūṇāṃ hiraṇyaretā sānilo bhūt  Ragh pitā pitḥṇām anṛṇas tam ante vayasy anantāni sukhāni lipsuḥ rājānam ājānuvilambibāhuṃ kṛtvā kṛtī valkalavān babhūva  Ragh kausalya ity uttarakosalānāṃ patyuḥ pataṃgānvayabhūṣaṇasya tasyaurasaḥ somasutaḥ suto bhūn netrotsavaḥ soma iva dvitīyaḥ  Ragh kausalya ity uttarakosalānāṃ sa brahmabhūyaṃ gatim ājagāma brahmiṣṭham ādhāya nije dhikāre brahmiṣṭham eva svatanuprasūtam  Ragh yaśobhir ābrahmasabhaṃ prakāśaḥ samyag mahīṃ śāsati śāsanāṅkām prajāś ciraṃ suprajasi prajeśe nanandur ānandajalāvilākṣyaḥ  Ragh pātrīkṛtātmā gurusevanena spṛṣṭākṛtiḥ pattrarathendraketoḥ taṃ putriṇāṃ puṣkarapattranetraḥ putraḥ samāropayad agrasaṃkhyām  Ragh vaṃśasthitiṃ vaṃśakareṇa tena saṃbhāvya bhāvī sa sakhā maghonaḥ upaspṛṣan sparśanivṛttalaulyas tripuṣkareṣu tridaśatvam āpa  Ragh tasya prabhānirjitapuṣparāgaṃ pauṣyaṃ tithau puṣyam asūta patnī yasminn apuṣyann udite samagrāṃ puṣṭiṃ janāḥ puṣya iva dvitīye  Ragh mahīṃ mahecchaḥ parikīrya sūnau manīṣiṇe jaiminaye rpitātmā tasmāt sayogād adhigamya yogam ajanmane kalpata janmabhīruḥ  Ragh tataḥ paraṃ tatprabhavaḥ prapede dhruvopameyo dhruvasaṃdhir urvīm yasminn abhūj jyāyasi satyasaṃdhe saṃdhir dhruvaḥ saṃnamatām arīṇām  Ragh sute śiśāv eva sudarśanākhye darśātyayendupriyadarśane saḥ mṛgāyatākṣo mṛgayāvihārī siṃhād avāpad vipadaṃ nṛsiṃhaḥ  Ragh svargāminas tasya tam aikamatyād amātyavargaḥ kulatantum ekam anāthadīnāḥ prakṛtīr avekṣya sāketanāthaṃ vidhivac cakāra  Ragh vavendunā tan nabhasopameyaṃ śāvaikasiṃhena ca kānanena raghoḥ kulaṃ kuḍmalapaṅkajena toyena cāprauṣhanarendram āsīt  Ragh lokena bhāvī pitur eva tulyaḥ saṃbhāvito mauliparigrahāt saḥ dṛṣṭo hi vṛṇvan kalabhapramāṇo py āśāḥ purovātam avāpya meghaḥ  Ragh taṃ rājavīthyām adhihasti yāntam ādhoraṇālambitam agryaveṣam ṣaḍvarṣadeśiyam api prabhutvāt praikṣanta paurāḥ pitṛgauraveṇa  Ragh kāmaṃ na so kalpata paitṛkasya siṃhāsanasya pratipūraṇāya tejomahimnā punar āvṛtātmā tad vyāpa cāmīkarapiñjareṇa  Ragh tasmād adhaḥ kiṃcid ivāvatīrṇāv asaṃspṛśantau tapanīyapīṭham sālaktakau bhūpatayaḥ prasiddhair vavandire maulibhir asya pādau  Ragh maṇau mahānīla iti prabhāvād alpapramāṇe pi yathā na mithyā śabdo mahārāja iti pratītas tathaiva tasmin yuyuje rbhake pi  Ragh paryantasaṃcāritacāmarasya kapolalolobhayakākapakṣat tasyānanād uccarito vivādaś cakshāla velāsv api nārṇavānām  Ragh nirvṛttajāmbūnadapaṭṭaśobhe nyastaṃ lalāṭe tilakaṃ dadhānaḥ tenaiva śūnyāny arisundarīṇāṃ mukhāni sa smeramukhaś cakāra  Ragh śirīṣapuṣpādhikasaukumāryaḥ khedaṃ sa yāyād api śrutavṛddhayogāt nitāntagurvīm api cānubhāvād dhuraṃ dharitryā bibharāṃ babhūva  Ragh nyastākṣarām akṣarabhūmikāyāṃ kārtsnyena gṛhṇāti lipiṃ na yāvat sarvāṇi tāvac chrutavṛddhayogāt phalāny upāyuṅkta sa daṇḍanīteḥ  Ragh urasy aparyāptabhāgā prauḍhībhaviṣyantam udīkṣamāṇā saṃjātalajjeva tam ātapatrachhāyāchalenopajugūha lakṣmīḥ  Ragh anaśnuvānena yugopamānam abaddhamaurvīkiṇalāñchanena aspṛṣṭakhaḍgatsaruṇāpi cāsīd rakṣāvatī tasya bhujena bhūmiḥ  Ragh na kevalaṃ gacchati tasya kāle yayuḥ śarīrāvayavā vivṛddhim vaṃśyā guṇāḥ khalv api lokakāntāḥ prārambhasūkṣmāḥ prathimānam āpuḥ  Ragh sa pūrvajanmāntaradṛṣṭapārāḥ smarann ivākleśakaro gurūṇām tisras trivargādhigamasya mūlaṃ jagrāha vidyāḥ prakṛtīś ca pitryāḥ  Ragh vyūhya sthitaḥ kiṃcid ivottarārdham unnaddhacūḍo ñcitasvyajānuḥ ākarṇam ākṛṣṭasabānadhanvā vyarocat āste sa vinīyamānaḥ  Ragh atha madhu vanitāṃ netranirveśanīyaṃ manasijatarupuṣpam rāgabandhapravālam akṛtakavidhi sarvāṅgīṇam ākalpajātaṃ vilasitapadam ādyaṃ yauvanaṃ sa prapede  Ragh pratikṛtiracanābhayo dūtisaṃdarśitābhyaḥ samadhikatararūpāḥ śuddhasaṃtānakāmaiḥ adhivividur amātyair āhṛtās tasya yūnaḥ prathamaparigṛhīte śrībhuvau rājakanyāḥ  Ragh agnivarṇam abhiṣicya rāghavaḥ sve pade tanayam agnitejasam śiśriye śrutavatām apaścimaḥ paścime vayasi naimiṣaṃ vaśī  Ragh tatra tīrthasalilena dīrghikās talpam antaritabhūmibhiḥ kuśaiḥ saudhavāsam uṭajena vismṛtaḥ saṃcikāya phalaniḥspṛhas tapaḥ  Ragh labdhapālanavidhau na tatsutaḥ khedam āpa guruṇā hi medinī bhoktum eva bhujanirjitadviṣā na prasādhayitum asya kalpitā  Ragh so dhikāram abhikaḥ kulocitaṃ kāścana svayam avartayat samāḥ taṃ niveśya saciveṣv ataḥ paraṃ strīvidheyanavayauvano bhavat  Ragh kāminīsahacarasya kāminas tasya veśmasu mṛdaṅganādiṣu ṛddhimantam adhikarddhir uttaraḥ pūrvam utsavam apohad utsavaḥ  Ragh indriyārthapariśūnyam akṣarmaḥ soḍhum ekam api sa kṣaṇātaram antare ca viharan divāniśaṃ na vyapaikṣata samutsukāḥ prajāḥ  Ragh gauravād yad api jātu mantriṇāṃ darśanaṃ prakṛtikāṅkṣitaṃ dadau tad gavākṣavivarāvalambinā kevalena caraṇena kalpitam  Ragh taṃ kṛtapraṇatayo nujīvinaḥ komalātmanakharāgarūṣitam bhejire navadivākarātapaspṛṣṭapaṅkajatulādhirohaṇam  Ragh yuvanonnatavilāsinīstanakṣobhalolakamalāś ca dīrghikāḥ gūḍhamohanagṛhās tadambubhiḥ sa vyagāhata vigāḍhamanmathaḥ  Ragh tatra sekahṛtalocanāñjanair dhautarāgaparipāṭalādharaiḥ aṅganās tam adhikaṃ vyalobhayann arpitaprakṛtikāntibhir mukhaiḥ  Ragh ghrāṇakāntamadhugandhakarṣiṇīḥ pānabhūmiracanāḥ priyāsakhaḥ abhyapadyata sa vāsitāsakhaḥ puṣpitāḥ kamalinīr iva dvipaḥ  Ragh sātirekamadakāraṇaṃ rahas tena dattam abhileṣur aṅganāḥ tābhir apy upahṛtaṃ mukhāsavaṃ so pibad bakulatulyadohadaḥ  Ragh aṅkam aṅkaparivartanocite tasya ninyatur aśūnyatām ubhe vallakī ca hṛdayaṃgamasvanā valguvāg api ca vāmalocanā  Ragh sa svayaṃ prahatapuṣkaraḥ kṛtī lolamālyavalayo haran manaḥ nartakīr abhinayātilaṅghinīḥ pārśvavartiṣu guruṣv alajjavat  Ragh cāru nṛtyavigame ca tanmukhaṃ svedabhinnatilakaṃ pariśramāt premadattavadanāniaḥ manaḥ so nvajīvad amarālakeśvarau  Ragh tasya sāvaraṇadṛṣṭasaṃdhayaḥ kāmyavastuṣu naveṣu saṅginaḥ vallabhābhir upasṛtya cakrire sāmibhuktaviṣayāḥ samāgamāḥ  Ragh aṅgulīkisalayāgratarjanaṃ bhrūvibhaṅgakuṭilaṃ ca vīkṣitam mekhalābhir asakṛc ca bandhanaṃ vañcayan praṇayinīr avāpa saḥ  Ragh tena dūtividitaṃ niṣeduṣā pṛṣṭhataḥ suratavārarātriṣu śuśruve priyajanasya kātaraṃ vipralambhapariśaṅkino vacaḥ  Ragh laulyam etya gṛhiṇīparigrahān nartakīṣv asulabhāsu tadvapuḥ vartate sma sa kathaṃcid ālikhann aṅgulīkṣaraṇasannavartikaḥ  Ragh premagarvitavipakṣamatsarād āyatāc ca madanān mahīkṣitam ninyur utsavavidhicchalena taṃ devya ujjitaruṣaḥ kṛtārthatām  Ragh prātar etya paribhogaśobhinā darśanena kṛtakhaṇḍanavyathāḥ prāñjaliḥ praṇayinīḥ prasādayan so dunot praṇayamantharaḥ punaḥ  Ragh svapnakīrtitavipakṣam aṅganāḥ darśanena kṛtakhaṇḍanavyathāḥ pracchadāntagalitāśrubindubhiḥ krodhabhinnavalayair vivartanaiḥ  Ragh kḷptapuṣpaśayanāṃl latāgṛhān etya dūtikṛtamārgadarśanaḥ anvabhūt parijanāṅganārataṃ so varodhabhayavepathūttaram  Ragh nāma vallabhajanasya te mayā prāpya bhāgyam api tasya kāṅkṣyate lolupaṃ bata mano mameti taṃ gotraviskhalitam ūcur aṅganāḥ  Ragh cūrṇababhru lulitasragākulaṃ chinnamekhalam alaktakāṅkitam utthitasya śayanaṃ vilāsinas tasya vibhramartatāny apāvṛṇot  Ragh sa svayaṃ caraṇarāgam ādadhe yoṣitaṃ na ca tathā samāhitaḥ lobhyamānanayanaḥ ślathāṃśukair mekhalāguṇapadair nitambibhiḥ  Ragh cumbane viparivartitādharaṃ hastarodhi raśanāvighaṭṭane vighniteccham api tasya sarvato manmathendhanam abhūd vadhūratam  Ragh darpaṇeṣu paribhogadarśinīr narmapūrvam anupṛṣṭhasaṃsthitaḥ chāyayā smitamanojñayā vadhūr hrīnimīlitamukhīś cakāra saḥ  Ragh kaṇṭhasaktamṛdubāhubandhanaṃ nyastapādatalam agrapādayoḥ prārthayanta śayanotthitaṃ priyās taṃ niśātyayavisargacumbanam  Ragh prekṣya darpaṇatalstham ātmano rājaveṣam atiśakraśobhinam pipriye sa na tathā yathā yuvā vyaktalakṣma paribhogamaṇḍanam  Ragh mitrakṛtyam apadiśya pārśvataḥ prasthitaṃ tam anavasthitaṃ priyāḥ vidma he śaṭha palāyanacchalāny añjaseti rurudhuḥ kacagrahaiḥ  Ragh tasya nirdayaratiśramālasāḥ kaṇṭhasūtram apadiśyayoṣitaḥ adhyaśerata bṛhad bhujāntaraṃ pīvarastanaviluptacandanam  Ragh saṃgamāya niśi gūḍhacāriṇaṃ cāradūtikathitaṃ puro gatāḥ vañcayiṣyasi kutas tamovṛtaḥ kāmuketi cakṛṣus tam aṅganāḥ  Ragh yoṣitām uḍupater ivāciṣāṃ sparśanirvṛtim asāv anāpnuvan āruroha kumudākaropamāṃ rātrijāgaraparo divāśayaḥ  Ragh veṇunā daśanapīḍitādharā vīṇayā nakhapadāṅkitoravaḥ śilapakārya ubhayena vejitās taṃ vijihmanayanā vyalobhayan  Ragh aṅgasattvavacanāśrayaṃ mithaḥ strīṣu nṛtyam upadhāya darśayan sa prayoganipuṇaiḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ saṃjagharṣa saha mitrasaṃnidhau  Ragh aṃsalambikuṭajārjunasrajas tasya nīparajasāṅgarāgiṇaḥ prāvṛṣi pramadabarhiṇeṣv abhūt kṛtimādriṣu vihāravibhramaḥ  Ragh vigrahāc ca śayane parāṅmukhīr nānunetum abalāḥ sa tatvare ācakāṅkṣa ghanaśabdaviklavās tā vivṛtya viśatīr bhujāntaram  Ragh kārttikīṣu savitānaharmyabhāg yāminīṣu lalitāṅganāsakhaḥ anvabhuṅkta surataśramāpahāṃ meghamuktaviśadāṃ sa candrikām  Ragh saikataṃ ca sarayūṃ vivṛṇvatīṃ śroṇibimbam iva haṃsamekhalam svapriyāvilasitānukāriṇīṃ saudhajālvivarair vyalokayat  Ragh marmarair agurudhūpagandhibhir vyaktahemarśanais tam ekataḥ jahrur āgrathanamokṣalolupaṃ haimanair nivsanaiḥ sumadhyamāḥ  Ragh arpitastimitadīpadṛṣṭayo garbhaveśmasu nivātakukṣiṣu tasya sarvasuratāntarakṣamāḥ sākṣitāṃ śiśirarātrayo yayuḥ  Ragh dakṣiṇena pavanena saṃbhṛtaṃ prekṣya cūtakusumaṃ sapallavam anvanaiṣur avadhūtavigrahās taṃ durutsahaviyogam aṅganāḥ  Ragh tāḥ svam aṅkam adhiropya dolayā preṅkhayan parijanāpaviddhayā muktarajju nibiḍaṃ bhayacchalāt kaṇṭhabandhanam avāpa bāhubhiḥ  Ragh taṃ payodharaniṣaktacandanair mauktikagrathitacārubhūṣaṇaiḥ grīṣmaveṣavidhibhiḥ siṣevire śroṇilambimaṇimekhalāḥ priyāḥ  Ragh yat sa bhagnasahakāram āsavaṃ raktapāṭalasamāgamaṃ papau tena tasya madhunirgamāt kṛśaś cittayonir abhavat punarnavaḥ  Ragh evam indriyasukhāni nirviśann anyakāryavimukhaḥ sa pārthivaḥ ātmalakṣaṇaniveditān ṛtūn atyavāhayad anaṅgavāhitaḥ  Ragh taṃ pramattam api na prabhāvataḥ śekur ākramitum anyapārthivāḥ āmayas tu ratirāgasaṃbhavo dakṣaśāpa iva candram akṣiṇot  Ragh dṛṣṭadoṣam api tan na so tyajat saṅgavastu bhiṣajām anāśravaḥ svādubhis tu viṣayair hṛtas tato duḥkham indriyagaṇo nivāryate  Ragh tasya pāṇḍuvadanālpabhūṣaṇā sāvalambagamanā mṛdusvanā yakṣmaṇāpi parihānir āyayau kāmayānasamavasthayā tulām  Ragh vyoma paścimakalāsthitendu vā paṅkaśeṣam iva gharmapalvalam rājñi tatkulam abhūt kṣayāture vāmanārcir iva dīpabhājanam  Ragh bāḍham eṣu divaseṣu karma sādhayati putrajanmane ity adarśitarujo sya mantriṇaḥ śaśvad ūcur aghaśaṅkinīḥ prajāḥ  Ragh sa tv anekavanitāsakho pi san pāvanīm anavalokya saṃtatim vaidyayatnaparibhāvinaṃ gadaṃ na pradīpa iva vāyum atyagāt  Ragh taṃ gṛhopavana eva saṃgatāḥ paścimakratuvidā purodhasā rogaśāntim apadiśya mantriṇaḥ saṃbhṛte śikhini gūḍham ādadhuḥ  Ragh taiḥ kṛtaprakṛtimukhyasaṃgrahair āśu tasya sahadharmacāriṇī sādhu dṛṣṭaśubhagarbhalakṣaṇā pratyapadyata narādhipaśriyam  Ragh tasyās tathāvidhanarendravipattiśokād uṣṇair vilocanajalaiḥ prathamābhitaptaḥ nirvāpitaḥ kanakakumbhamukhojjhitena vaṃśābhiṣekavidhinā śiśireṇa garbhaḥ  Ragh taṃ bhāvāya prasavasamayākāṅkṣiṇīnāṃ prajānām antargūḍhaṃ kṣitir iva babhau bījamuṣṭiṃ dadhānā maulaiḥ sārdhaṃ sthavirasacivair hemasiṃhāsanasthā rājñī rājyaṃ vidhivad aśiṣad bhartur avyāhatājñā  Ragh ADDITIONAL VERSES KEPAKAākīryamāṇam āsannavidhibhiḥ samidāharaiḥ vaikhānasair adṛśyāgnipratyudgamanavṛttibhiḥ  Ragh imāṃ devīm ṛtusnātāṃ smṛtvā sapadi satvaraḥ pradakṣiṇakriyātītas tasyāḥ kopam ajījanaḥ  Ragh tāmralalāṭajāṃ rekhāṃ bibhratī sāsitetarām saṃdhyā prātipadeneva pratibhinnā himāṃśunā  Ragh gāndharvam astraṃ tad itaḥ pratīccha prayogasaṃhāravibhaktamantram saṃdhyā prātipadeneva na cārihiṃsā vijayaḥ svahaste  Ragh nidrāvaśaṃ tvayi gate śaśinā kathaṃcid ātmānam ānanarucā bhavato viyujya lakṣmīr vibhātasamaye pi hi darśanena paryutsukā praṇayinī niśi khaṇḍiteva  Ragh mandaṃ vivāti himasaṃbhṛtaśītabhāvaḥ saṃsṛjyate sarasijair aruṇāṃśubhinnaiḥ saurabhyam īpsur iva te mukhamārutasya yan no guṇān prati niśāpariṇāmavāyuḥ  Ragh iti sa vihatanidras talpam alpetarāṃśaḥ suragaja iva gaṅgāsaikataṃ supratīkaḥ parijanavanitānāṃ pādayor vyāpṛtānāṃ valayamaṇividiṣṭaṃ pracchadāntaṃ mumoca  Ragh sa tatra mañeṣcu vimānakalpeṣv ākalpasaṃmūrchitarūpaśobhān siṃhāsanasthān nṛpatīn apaśyat yūpān praśastān iva haimavedīn  Ragh yadā yadā rājakumārikāsau na pūrvapūrvaṃ ganayāṃ cakāra tadā tadā nāmitarepharekhām āśālatā pallavinī babhūva  Ragh lalāṭabaddhabhṛkuṭītaraṅgais tanutyajāṃ dantanipīḍitoṣṭhaiḥ ātastare bhallanikṛttakaṇṭhair huṃkāragarbhair dviṣatāṃ śirobhiḥ  Ragh atha vīkṣya guṇaiḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ prakṛtiṣv ātmajam ābhigamikaiḥ padavīṃ pariṇāmadeśinīṃ raghur ādatta vanāntagāminīm  Ragh namas trimūrtaye tubhyaṃ guṇatrayavibhāgāya prāk sṛṣṭeḥ kevalātmane paścād bhadram upeyuṣe  Ragh te pi tūrṇam avagamya śāmbhavam āsamāharaṇakarmatatparāḥ svāṃ sakṣiptatikarkaśaṃ hi tac cikṣipur daśāarathātmajāgrataḥ  Ragh nistriṃśakalpasya nidher jalānām eṣā tamāladrumarāja nīlā dūrād arālabhru vibhāti velā kalaṅkarekhā malineva dhārā  Ragh pratyāgatau tatra cirapravāsād apaśyatāṃ dāśarathī jananyau kumudvatī śītamarīcilekhe diveva rūpāntaradurvibhāvye  Ragh keyaṃ vane lakṣmaṇa lakṣmaṇeti dīnākṣaraṃ roditi yoṣid uccaiḥ āṃ jñātam eṣā janakātmajeti kavir vicintyāntikam ājagāma  Ragh tad ākarṇya muner vākyaṃ rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ samaṃ harṣaviṣādābhyāṃ yuyuje nītikovidaḥ  Ragh gaccha lakṣmaṇa śīghraṃ tvaṃ mā bhūd dharmaviparyayaḥ tyāgo vāpi vadho vāpi sādhūnām ubhayaṃ samam  Ragh tasmād babhūvātha dalābhidhāno dalānvitaḥ padmadalābhadṛṣṭiḥ kundāgra danto ripudantisiṃhaḥ patiḥ pṛthivyāḥ kulakair ivenduḥ  Ragh hitvātha bhogāṃs tapasottamena triviṣṭapaṃ prāptavati kṣitīśe tadātmajaḥ sāgaradhīracetāḥ śaśāsa pṛthvīṃ sakalāṃ nṛsomaḥ  Ragh
